"<img alt=""image.png"" src=""1765614214752-ae72c3b7-08a0-4f17-87a9-ecbf0a4f000a.png""><br>摆动序列(不要改变上坡的状态）"	
"<img src=""paste-882ff1c4cc02d6f47b49c063c29f7ee1a982aca0.jpg""><img src=""paste-b712b830fc062244744735e5dce2dc2264213e8d.jpg"">对于第五种左右子树都有的处理，要记住二叉搜索树的特性"	
"<img alt=""image.png"" src=""1765689764255-1f820283-fd42-471c-97be-b335ee120ccb.png""><br><div><div><div>给定&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>&nbsp;和&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">k</span>，将从 1 到&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>&nbsp;之间的所有正整数可以分为两类：A 类数可以被&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">k</span>&nbsp;整除（也就是说是&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">k</span>&nbsp;的倍数），而 B 类数不能。请输出这两类数的平均数，精确到小数点后&nbsp;1&nbsp;位，用空格隔开。</div><div>数据保证两类数的个数都不会是&nbsp;0。</div></div></div><h2>输入格式</h2><div><div><div>输入两个正整数&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>&nbsp;与&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">k</span>。</div></div></div><h2>输出格式</h2><div><div><div>输出一行，两个实数，分别表示 A 类数与 B 类数的平均数。精确到小数点后一位。</div></div></div>"	
"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><br style=""color: rgb(255, 255, 255); white-space-collapse: collapse; background-color: rgb(54, 54, 54);""><span style=""color: rgb(255, 255, 255); white-space-collapse: collapse; background-color: rgb(54, 54, 54);"">高精度阶乘求和</span><br style=""color: rgb(255, 255, 255); white-space-collapse: collapse; background-color: rgb(54, 54, 54);""></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n;
    cin &gt;&gt; n;

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 用数组存储大数字，每位存一个数字</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 比如数字123，我们存为[3,2,1]</span>
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; sum = {<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>}; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 存储总和，初始为0</span>
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; fact = {<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>}; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 存储当前的阶乘，初始为1! = 1</span>

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 从1循环到n</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &lt;= n; i++) {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 计算 i! = (i-1)! * i</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (i &gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>) {
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> carry = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 进位</span>
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> j = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; j &lt; fact.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>(); j++) {
                <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> product = fact[j] * i + carry;
                fact[j] = product % <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">10</span>; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 当前位</span>
                carry = product / <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">10</span>; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 进位</span>
            }
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 处理最后的进位</span>
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (carry &gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>) {
                fact.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">push_back</span>(carry % <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">10</span>);
                carry /= <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">10</span>;
            }
        }

        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 把 i! 加到总和中</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 思路：对齐两个数字的最低位，逐位相加</span>
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> max_len = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">max</span>(sum.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>(), fact.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>());
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> carry = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 加法进位</span>

        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 扩展sum的长度，确保能存放结果</span>
        sum.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">resize</span>(max_len, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>);

        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 逐位相加</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> j = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; j &lt; max_len; j++) {
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> a = (j &lt; sum.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>()) ? sum[j] : <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> b = (j &lt; fact.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>()) ? fact[j] : <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> total = a + b + carry;
            sum[j] = total % <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">10</span>; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 当前位</span>
            carry = total / <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">10</span>; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 进位</span>
        }

        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 处理最后的进位</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (carry &gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>) {
            sum.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">push_back</span>(carry % <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">10</span>);
            carry /= <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">10</span>;
        }
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 输出结果（注意：我们是倒着存的，要倒序输出）</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = sum.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>() - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &gt;= <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; i--) {
        cout &lt;&lt; sum[i];
    }

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}

"<div style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(220, 220, 220); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(51, 51, 51); box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3) 0px 4px 6px; overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">单链表反转
<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span>* <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">reverseList</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span>* head) {
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span>* pre = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span>* next = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (head != <span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>) {
        next = head-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>; <span style=""color:#57A64A"">// 1. 记录</span>
        head-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span> = pre;  <span style=""color:#57A64A"">// 2. 反转</span>
        pre = head;        <span style=""color:#57A64A"">// 3. 推进</span>
        head = next;       <span style=""color:#57A64A"">// 4. 移动</span>
    }
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> pre;
}

            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 双链表反转</span>
<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">DoubleListNode</span>* reverseDoubleList(<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">DoubleListNode</span>* head) {
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">DoubleListNode</span>* pre = <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>;
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">DoubleListNode</span>* next = <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>;
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">while</span> (head != <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {
        next = head-&gt;next;  <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 1. 记录</span>
        head-&gt;next = pre;   <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 2. 反转 Next</span>
        head-&gt;last = next;  <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 3. 反转 Last</span>
        pre = head;         <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 4. 推进</span>
        head = next;        <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 5. 移动</span>
    }
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> pre;
}

"<div style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(220, 220, 220); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(51, 51, 51); box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3) 0px 4px 6px; overflow-x: auto;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 合并两个升序链表</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">static</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">ListNode</span>* mergeTwoLists(<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">ListNode</span>* head1, <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">ListNode</span>* head2) {
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 1. 创建哨兵节点 (Dummy Node)</span>
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 它作为一个占位符，dummy.next 才是真正合并后的链表头</span>
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">ListNode</span> dummy(0); 
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">ListNode</span>* pre = &amp;dummy; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// pre 始终指向结果链表的最后一个节点</span>

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 2. 双指针 PK 过程</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">while</span> (head1 != <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span> &amp;&amp; head2 != <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (head1-&gt;val &lt;= head2-&gt;val) {
            pre-&gt;next = head1;
            head1 = head1-&gt;next; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 移动 head1</span>
        } <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">else</span> {
            pre-&gt;next = head2;
            head2 = head2-&gt;next; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 移动 head2</span>
        }
        pre = pre-&gt;next; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// pre 推进</span>
    }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 3. 收尾工作：将剩下的“尾巴”直接挂载</span>
    pre-&gt;next = (head1 != <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) ? head1 : head2;

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 4. 返回真正的头节点</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> dummy.next;
}

"<div style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(220, 220, 220); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(51, 51, 51); box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3) 0px 4px 6px; overflow-x: auto;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 链表高精度加法（链表逆序存储）</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">static</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">ListNode</span>* addTwoNumbers(<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">ListNode</span>* h1, <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">ListNode</span>* h2) {
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">ListNode</span>* ans = <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 结果头节点</span>
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">ListNode</span>* cur = <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 结果尾指针</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> carry = 0;           <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 进位</span>

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 循环条件：只要 h1 或 h2 还有节点未处理，就继续</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">for</span> (<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> sum, val; 
         h1 != <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span> || h2 != <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>; 
         h1 = (h1 == <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span> ? <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span> : h1-&gt;next), 
         h2 = (h2 == <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span> ? <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span> : h2-&gt;next)) {
        
        <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 1. 求和：节点值 + 节点值 + 进位</span>
        sum = (h1 == <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span> ? 0 : h1-&gt;val)
            + (h2 == <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span> ? 0 : h2-&gt;val)
            + carry;

        val = sum % 10;   <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 当前位保留的数值</span>
        carry = sum / 10; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 产生的新进位</span>

        <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 2. 创建新节点并连接</span>
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (ans == <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {
            ans = <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">new</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">ListNode</span>(val);
            cur = ans;
        } <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">else</span> {
            cur-&gt;next = <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">new</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">ListNode</span>(val);
            cur = cur-&gt;next;
        }
    }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 3. 收尾：如果最后还有进位，补一个节点</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (carry == 1) {
        cur-&gt;next = <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">new</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">ListNode</span>(1);
    }

    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> ans;
}</pre>

"<div style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(220, 220, 220); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(51, 51, 51); box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3) 0px 4px 6px; overflow-x: auto;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 分隔链表（保持相对顺序）</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">static</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">ListNode</span>* partition(<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">ListNode</span>* head, <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> x) {
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// leftHead/Tail 管理小于 x 的节点</span>
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">ListNode</span>* leftHead = <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>;
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">ListNode</span>* leftTail = <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>;
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// rightHead/Tail 管理大于等于 x 的节点</span>
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">ListNode</span>* rightHead = <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>;
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">ListNode</span>* rightTail = <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>;
    
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">ListNode</span>* next = <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>;

    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">while</span> (head != <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {
        next = head-&gt;next;
        head-&gt;next = <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 断开连接，确保干净放入新链表</span>

        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (head-&gt;val &lt; x) {
            <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 放入左区</span>
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (leftHead == <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) leftHead = head;
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">else</span> leftTail-&gt;next = head;
            leftTail = head;
        } <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">else</span> {
            <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 放入右区</span>
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (rightHead == <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) rightHead = head;
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">else</span> rightTail-&gt;next = head;
            rightTail = head;
        }
        head = next;
    }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 拼接：左区为空则直接返回右区，否则左尾连右头</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (leftHead == <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> rightHead;
    
    leftTail-&gt;next = rightHead;
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> leftHead;
}

"<div style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(220, 220, 220); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(51, 51, 51); box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3) 0px 4px 6px; overflow-x: auto;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 数组模拟队列（双指针法）</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">class</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">Queue2</span> {
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt; q;
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> l, r; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// l: 头指针, r: 尾指针(指向下一个空位)</span>

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">Queue2</span>(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> n) : q(n), l(0), r(0) {}
    
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">bool</span> isEmpty() { <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> l == r; }
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">void</span> offer(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> num) { q[r++] = num; } <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 入队：存值后 r 右移</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> poll() { <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> q[l++]; }         <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 出队：取值后 l 右移</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> head() { <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> q[l]; }           <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 查看队头</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> size() { <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> r - l; }
};

            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 数组模拟栈（单指针法）</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">class</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">Stack2</span> {
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt; s;
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> top; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 既代表当前栈的大小，也指向栈顶的下一个位置</span>

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">Stack2</span>(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> n) : s(n), top(0) {}
    
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">bool</span> isEmpty() { <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> top == 0; }
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">void</span> push(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> num) { s[top++] = num; } <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 压栈：先存再移</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> pop() { <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> s[--top]; }         <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 弹栈：先移再取</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> peek() { <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> s[top - 1]; }      <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 查看栈顶：需回退一格</span>

"<div style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(220, 220, 220); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(51, 51, 51); box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3) 0px 4px 6px; overflow-x: auto;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #57A64A;"">数组模拟循环队列</span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 循环队列（Size 变量解耦空/满判断）</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">class</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">MyCircularQueue</span> {
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt; q;
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> l, r, size, limit; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// l:头, r:尾(下个空位), limit:容量</span>

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">MyCircularQueue</span>(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> k) : q(k), l(0), r(0), size(0), limit(k) {}

    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">bool</span> enQueue(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> val) {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (size == limit) <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">false</span>;
        q[r] = val;
        <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 环形步进：若到达数组末尾，回到下标 0</span>
        r = (r == limit - 1) ? 0 : (r + 1); 
        size++;
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">true</span>;
    }

    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">bool</span> deQueue() {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (size == 0) <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">false</span>;
        <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 环形步进：若到达数组末尾，回到下标 0</span>
        l = (l == limit - 1) ? 0 : (l + 1); 
        size--;
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">true</span>;
    }

    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">Front</span>() { <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> size == 0 ? -1 : q[l]; }

    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">Rear</span>() {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (size == 0) <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> -1;
        <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 计算实际尾元素：r 指向的是""下一个""空位，所以要回退一格</span>
        <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 特殊情况：如果 r 是 0，则尾元素在 limit-1</span>
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> lastIndex = (r == 0) ? limit - 1 : r - 1;
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> q[lastIndex];
    }
    
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">bool</span> isEmpty() { <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> size == 0; }
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">bool</span> isFull() { <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> size == limit; }
};

            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 用栈实现队列（双栈“倒水”法）</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">class</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">MyQueue</span> {
    stack&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt; in, out;

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 核心逻辑：当 out 栈为空时，将 in 栈所有数据一次性倒入 out 栈</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">void</span> inToOut() {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (out.empty()) {
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">while</span> (!in.empty()) {
                out.push(in.top());
                in.pop();
            }
        }
    }

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">void</span> push(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> x) {
        in.push(x);
        inToOut(); <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 每次 push 尝试倒数据（可选，也可只在 pop/peek 时调用）</span>
    }

    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> pop() {
        inToOut(); <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 确保 out 有数据</span>
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> val = out.top();
        out.pop();
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> val;
    }

    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> peek() {
        inToOut(); <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 确保 out 有数据</span>
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> out.top();
    }

    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">bool</span> empty() { <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> in.empty() &amp;&amp; out.empty(); }
};

"<div style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(220, 220, 220); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(51, 51, 51); box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3) 0px 4px 6px; overflow-x: auto;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 用队列实现栈（单队列轮转法）</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">class</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">MyStack</span> {
    queue&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt; q;

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 入栈：O(N) </span>
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 新元素入队后，将前面所有元素依次出队再入队，</span>
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 使得新元素排在队首（即栈顶）。</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">void</span> push(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> x) {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> n = q.size();
        q.push(x);
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">for</span> (<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> i = 0; i &lt; n; i++) {
            q.push(q.front());
            q.pop();
        }
    }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 出栈：O(1) - 队首即栈顶</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> pop() {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> val = q.front();
        q.pop();
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> val;
    }

    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> top() { <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> q.front(); }

    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">bool</span> empty() { <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> q.empty(); }
};

"<div style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(220, 220, 220); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(51, 51, 51); box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3) 0px 4px 6px; overflow-x: auto;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 最小栈（双栈同步法）</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">class</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">MinStack</span> {
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">stack</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt; data; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 存数据的栈</span>
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">stack</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt; minS; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 存最小值的栈（与 data 高度同步）</span>

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">void</span> push(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> val) {
        data.push(val);
        <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 核心逻辑：若新值更小（或相等），压入新值；否则重复压入当前的最小值</span>
        <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 这样 minS 的栈顶永远对应 data 当前状态下的最小值</span>
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (minS.empty() || val &lt;= minS.top()) {
            minS.push(val);
        } <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">else</span> {
            minS.push(minS.top());
        }
    }

    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">void</span> pop() {
        <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 由于高度同步，直接同时弹出即可，无需判断</span>
        data.pop();
        minS.pop();
    }

    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> top() { <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> data.top(); }
    
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> getMin() { <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> minS.top(); }
};

            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 最小栈（静态数组实现版）</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">class</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">MinStack2</span> {
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">static</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">const</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">MAXN</span> = 8001; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 根据题目数据范围设定</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> data[<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">MAXN</span>];  <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 数据栈数组</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> minArr[<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">MAXN</span>]; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 最小值栈数组（与 data 下标同步）</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> size;         <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 当前栈顶指针（即元素个数）</span>

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">MinStack2</span>() : size(0) {}

    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">void</span> push(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> val) {
        data[size] = val;
        <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 核心逻辑：若栈空或新值更小，minArr 存新值；否则沿用上一个最小值</span>
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (size == 0 || val &lt;= minArr[size - 1]) {
            minArr[size] = val;
        } <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">else</span> {
            minArr[size] = minArr[size - 1];
        }
        size++;
    }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 逻辑删除：只需减少 size，无需真正清除内存</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">void</span> pop() { size--; }

    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> top() { <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> data[size - 1]; }

    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> getMin() { <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> minArr[size - 1]; }
};

            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 循环双端队列（STL deque 代理版）</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;deque&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">using</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">class</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">MyCircularDeque</span> {
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">deque</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt; dq; <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> limit; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 底层容器与容量上限</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">MyCircularDeque</span>(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> k) : limit(k) {}

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 插入头部：若满返回false，否则头部入队并返回true</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">bool</span> insertFront(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> v) { <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span>(dq.size() == limit) <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">false</span>; dq.push_front(v); <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">true</span>; }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 插入尾部：若满返回false，否则尾部入队并返回true</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">bool</span> insertLast(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> v) { <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span>(dq.size() == limit) <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">false</span>; dq.push_back(v); <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">true</span>; }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 删除头部：若空返回false，否则头部弹出并返回true</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">bool</span> deleteFront() { <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span>(dq.empty()) <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">false</span>; dq.pop_front(); <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">true</span>; }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 删除尾部：若空返回false，否则尾部弹出并返回true</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">bool</span> deleteLast() { <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span>(dq.empty()) <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">false</span>; dq.pop_back(); <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">true</span>; }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 获取头部：若空返回-1，否则返回头部值</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> getFront() { <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> dq.empty() ? -<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span> : dq.front(); }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 获取尾部：若空返回-1，否则返回尾部值</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> getRear() { <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> dq.empty() ? -<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span> : dq.back(); }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 判空</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">bool</span> isEmpty() { <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> dq.empty(); }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 判满</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">bool</span> isFull() { <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> dq.size() == limit; }
};

"<div style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(220, 220, 220); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(51, 51, 51); box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3) 0px 4px 6px; overflow-x: auto;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 归并排序求小和（Small Sum）</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">const</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">MAXN</span> = 100001;
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> arr[<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">MAXN</span>], help[<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">MAXN</span>]; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 全局数组优化效率</span>

<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 核心逻辑：在合并过程中统计跨组的小和</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">long</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">long</span> merge(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> l, <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> m, <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> r) {
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">long</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">long</span> ans = 0;
    
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 1. 统计阶段：利用有序性加速</span>
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 遍历右组的每个数 arr[j]，在左组找 &lt;= arr[j] 的累加和</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">long</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">long</span> current_sum = 0; 
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">for</span> (<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> j = m + 1, i = l; j &lt;= r; j++) {
        <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// i 指针不回退：arr[j] 增大，满足条件的 arr[i] 范围只会向右扩大</span>
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">while</span> (i &lt;= m &amp;&amp; arr[i] &lt;= arr[j]) {
            current_sum += arr[i++];
        }注意上面的current_cum为此时j元素左边的总和，下面为ans的j元素是加上了上一个元素的总和，所以i指针不用回退，意思就是下一个j元素加上了上一个j元素的的总和，并且还要再加上它移动i指针产生的新总和
        ans += current_sum; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 当前右组元素 j 贡献的小和</span>
    }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 2. 排序阶段：标准的归并逻辑</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> i = l, a = l, b = m + 1;
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">while</span> (a &lt;= m &amp;&amp; b &lt;= r) {
        help[i++] = arr[a] &lt;= arr[b] ? arr[a++] : arr[b++];
    }
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">while</span> (a &lt;= m) help[i++] = arr[a++];
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">while</span> (b &lt;= r) help[i++] = arr[b++];

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 3. 拷贝回原数组</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">for</span> (i = l; i &lt;= r; i++) arr[i] = help[i];
    
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> ans;
}

<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 递归入口</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">long</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">long</span> smallSum(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> l, <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> r) {
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (l == r) <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> 0;
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> m = l + ((r - l) &gt;&gt; 1);
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 结果 = 左内部小和 + 右内部小和 + 跨左右产生的小和</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> smallSum(l, m) + smallSum(m + 1, r) + merge(l, m, r);
}
</pre>
        </div>
        <br>"	
"<div style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(51, 51, 51); box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3) 0px 4px 6px; overflow-x: auto;"">
            <pre style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220); margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 归并排序求翻转对（LeetCode 493）</span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">左加右再加跨左右
<span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 核心逻辑：在合并前统计 arr[i] &gt; 2 * arr[j] 的数量</span><font color=""#dcdcdc"">
</font><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><font color=""#dcdcdc""> merge(</font><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">vector</span><font color=""#dcdcdc"">&lt;</font><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><font color=""#dcdcdc"">&gt;&amp; arr, </font><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><font color=""#dcdcdc""> l, </font><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><font color=""#dcdcdc""> m, </font><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><font color=""#dcdcdc""> r) {
    </font><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 1. 统计阶段：双指针不回退</span><font color=""#dcdcdc"">
    </font><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><font color=""#dcdcdc""> ans = 0;
    </font><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 对于左组的每个数 i，在右组找满足条件的 j 的边界</span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">先翻转判断，再排序
    <span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">for</span><font color=""#dcdcdc""> (</font><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><font color=""#dcdcdc""> i = l, j = m + 1; i &lt;= m; i++) {
        </font><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 关键点：使用 long long 防止 arr[j] * 2 溢出</span><font color=""#dcdcdc"">
        </font><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">while</span><font color=""#dcdcdc""> (j &lt;= r &amp;&amp; (</font><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">long</span><font color=""#dcdcdc""> </font><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">long</span><font color=""#dcdcdc"">)arr[i] &gt; (</font><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">long</span><font color=""#dcdcdc""> </font><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">long</span><font color=""#dcdcdc"">)arr[j] * 2) {
            j++;
        }
        </font><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// j 停下的位置是第一个不满足条件的位置</span><font color=""#dcdcdc"">
        </font><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 所以 [m+1 ... j-1] 都是满足条件的，数量为 j - (m + 1)</span><font color=""#dcdcdc"">
        ans += j - m - 1;</font></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><img src=""paste-befd1989892c37a14f6407496d864aec02c1723d.jpg"">右边的第一个是m+1，不满足的索引是j，左边满足的是j-1。所以ans+=j - m - 1;</pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">并且i没有移动，后续的i，肯定比之前的i大，所以i不用回退。<br><font color=""#dcdcdc"">
    }

    </font><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 2. 排序阶段：标准归并</span><font color=""#dcdcdc"">
    </font><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><font color=""#dcdcdc""> i = l, a = l, b = m + 1;
    </font><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">while</span><font color=""#dcdcdc""> (a &lt;= m &amp;&amp; b &lt;= r) {
        help[i++] = arr[a] &lt;= arr[b] ? arr[a++] : arr[b++];
    }
    </font><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">while</span><font color=""#dcdcdc""> (a &lt;= m) help[i++] = arr[a++];
    </font><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">while</span><font color=""#dcdcdc""> (b &lt;= r) help[i++] = arr[b++];
    
    </font><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 3. 拷贝回原数组</span><font color=""#dcdcdc"">
    </font><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">for</span><font color=""#dcdcdc""> (i = l; i &lt;= r; i++) arr[i] = help[i];

    </font><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">return</span><font color=""#dcdcdc""> ans;
}

</font><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 递归入口</span><font color=""#dcdcdc"">
</font><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><font color=""#dcdcdc""> counts(</font><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">vector</span><font color=""#dcdcdc"">&lt;</font><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><font color=""#dcdcdc"">&gt;&amp; arr, </font><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><font color=""#dcdcdc""> l, </font><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><font color=""#dcdcdc""> r) {
    </font><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">if</span><font color=""#dcdcdc""> (l == r) </font><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">return</span><font color=""#dcdcdc""> 0;
    </font><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><font color=""#dcdcdc""> m = l + ((r - l) &gt;&gt; 1);
    </font><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">return</span><font color=""#dcdcdc""> counts(arr, l, m) + counts(arr, m + 1, r) + merge(arr, l, m, r);
}
</font></pre>

"<div style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(220, 220, 220); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(51, 51, 51); box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3) 0px 4px 6px; overflow-x: auto;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 随机快速排序（荷兰国旗划分版）</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> arr[100001];
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> first, last; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 全局变量，用于记录 ==x 区域的左右边界</span>

<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 荷兰国旗划分：将 arr[l...r] 分为 &lt;x, ==x, &gt;x 三部分</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">void</span> partition(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> l, <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> r, <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> x) {
    first = l;   <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// &lt;x 区域的右边界的下一位</span>
    last = r;    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// &gt;x 区域的左边界的上一位</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> i = l;
    
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">while</span> (i &lt;= last) {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (arr[i] == x) {
            i++; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 等于区直接跳过</span>
        } <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">else</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (arr[i] &lt; x) {
            swap(arr[first++], arr[i++]); <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 发配到左边，i 前进</span>
        } <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">else</span> {
            swap(arr[i], arr[last--]); <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 发配到右边，i 原地不动（待检查换回来的数）</span>
        }
    }
}

<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 递归主函数</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">void</span> quickSort(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> l, <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> r) {
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (l &gt;= r) <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span>;

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 1. 灵魂操作：随机选基准值，避免退化</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> x = arr[l + rand() % (r - l + 1)];
    
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 2. 划分区域</span>
    partition(l, r, x);
    
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 3. 记录边界（必须存入局部变量，防递归污染）</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> left = first;
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> right = last;
    
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 4. 递归左右两侧（中间 ==x 部分无需再排）</span>
    quickSort(l, left - 1);
    quickSort(right + 1, r);
}
</pre>

"<div style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(220, 220, 220); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(51, 51, 51); box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3) 0px 4px 6px; overflow-x: auto;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">欢乐跳</pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><div><div><div>一个&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>&nbsp;个元素的整数数组，如果数组两个连续元素之间差的绝对值包括了&nbsp;[1,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>−1]&nbsp;之间的所有整数，则称之符合“欢乐的跳”，如数组&nbsp;{1,4,2,3}&nbsp;符合“欢乐的跳”，因为差的绝对值分别为：3,2,1。</div><div>给定一个数组，你的任务是判断该数组是否符合“欢乐的跳”。</div></div></div><h2>输入格式</h2><div><div><div>每组测试数据第一行以一个整数&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>(1≤<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>≤1000)&nbsp;开始，接下来&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>&nbsp;个空格隔开的在&nbsp;[−108,108]&nbsp;之间的整数。</div></div></div><h2>输出格式</h2><div><div><div>对于每组测试数据，输出一行若该数组符合“欢乐的跳”则输出&nbsp;<code>Jolly</code>，否则输出&nbsp;<code>Not jolly</code>。</div></div></div>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;cmath&gt;</span>     <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 为了使用 abs() 函数</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;algorithm&gt;</span>

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">using</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> main() {
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> n;
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 读取元素个数 n</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (!(cin &gt;&gt; n)) <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>;

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 特例处理：如果只有一个数，n-1=0，直接符合要求</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (n == <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>) {
        cout &lt;&lt; <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""Jolly""</span> &lt;&lt; endl;
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>;
    }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 1. 读取原始数组</span>
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt; a(n);
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">for</span> (<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> i = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>; i &lt; n; i++) {
        cin &gt;&gt; a[i];
    }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 2. 创建一个布尔数组标记 [1, n-1] 范围内的数字是否出现过</span>
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 初始全部为 false</span>
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">bool</span>&gt; has_diff(n, <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">false</span>);

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 3. 计算相邻差值的绝对值</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">for</span> (<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> i = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>; i &lt; n - <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>; i++) {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> diff = abs(a[i] - a[i+<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>]);
        
        <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 如果差值在 1 到 n-1 范围内，标记为“已出现”</span>
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (diff &gt;= <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span> &amp;&amp; diff &lt;= n - <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>) {
            has_diff[diff] = <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">true</span>;
        }
    }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 4. 检查 1 到 n-1 是否每一个都被标记为 true 了</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">for</span> (<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> i = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>; i &lt;= n - <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>; i++) {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (!has_diff[i]) {
            <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 只要有一个没出现，就不是 Jolly</span>
            cout &lt;&lt; <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""Not jolly""</span> &lt;&lt; endl;
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>;
        }
    }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 全部出现了</span>
    cout &lt;&lt; <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""Jolly""</span> &lt;&lt; endl;
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>;
}

"<div style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(220, 220, 220); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(51, 51, 51); box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3) 0px 4px 6px; overflow-x: auto;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #9B9B9B;"">灯泡的异或</span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #9B9B9B;"">#include</span> &lt;iostream&gt;
<span style=""color: #9B9B9B;"">#include</span> &lt;cmath&gt;

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">using</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">namespace</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">std</span>;

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> main() {
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> n;
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 读取操作次数</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (!(cin &gt;&gt; n)) <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> 0;

    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> ans = 0; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 用于存储异或结果的变量</span>
    
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">for</span> (<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> i = 0; i &lt; n; ++i) {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">double</span> a;
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> t;
        <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 读取每一行的 a 和 t</span>
        cin &gt;&gt; a &gt;&gt; t;
        
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">for</span> (<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> j = 1; j &lt;= t; ++j) {
            <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 计算灯的编号并取整</span>
            <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// floor(j * a) 返回不大于 j*a 的最大整数</span>
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> lamp_id = floor(j * a);
            
            <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 核心逻辑：异或运算</span>
            <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 出现偶数次的编号会抵消，出现奇数次的会留下</span>
            ans ^= lamp_id;
        }
    }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 输出最后剩下的那个编号</span>
    cout &lt;&lt; ans &lt;&lt; endl;

    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> 0;
}

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">024<strong>快速选择算法</strong>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;algorithm&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;cstdlib&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">class</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Solution</span> {
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> first, last; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 记录荷兰国旗划分后等于区域的左右边界</span>

排序功能
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 荷兰国旗划分：将数组分为小于x、等于x、大于x三个部分</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">partition</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&amp; arr, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> r, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> x) {
        first = l; last = r; <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = l;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (i &lt;= last) {
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (arr[i] == x) i++; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 等于x，指针后移</span>
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (arr[i] &lt; x) <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">swap</span>(arr[first++], arr[i++]); <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 小于x，换到左边</span>
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">swap</span>(arr[i], arr[last--]); <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 大于x，换到右边</span>
        }
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 随机选择核心逻辑：平均时间复杂度 O(N)</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">findKthLargest</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&amp; nums, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> k) {
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = nums.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>() - k; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 第K大元素即为升序排序后索引为 nums.size()-k 的数</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, r = nums.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>() - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; l &lt;= r; ) {
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 随机选择基准值x并进行划分，保证概率上的 O(N) 性能</span>
先划分
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">partition</span>(nums, l, r, nums[l + <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">rand</span>() % (r - l + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>)]);
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (i &lt; first) r = first - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 目标在小于区域</span>
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (i &gt; last) l = last + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 目标在大于区域</span>
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> nums[i]; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 目标就在等于区域，直接返回</span>
找到了直接返回
        }
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> -<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
    }
};

            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 025 堆结构和堆排序</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;cstdio&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;algorithm&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">using</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">const</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">MAXN</span> = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">100001</span>;
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> arr[<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">MAXN</span>], n;

<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 向上调整大根堆：用于从顶到底建堆过程</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">void</span> heapInsert(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> i) {
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">while</span> (arr[i] &gt; arr[(i - <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>) / <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">2</span>]) { swap(arr[i], arr[(i - <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>) / <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">2</span>]); i = (i - <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>) / <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">2</span>; }
}

<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 向下调整大根堆：用于从底到顶建堆或弹出堆顶后的调整</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">void</span> heapify(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> i, <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> size) {
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> l = i * <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">2</span> + <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 左孩子索引</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">while</span> (l &lt; size) {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> best = l + <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span> &lt; size &amp;&amp; arr[l + <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>] &gt; arr[l] ? l + <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span> : l; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 左右孩子选大的</span>
        best = arr[best] &gt; arr[i] ? best : i; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 孩子与父亲比</span>
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (best == i) <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">break</span>; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 父亲大则停止</span>
        swap(arr[i], arr[best]); i = best; l = i * <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">2</span> + <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>;
    }
}

<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 堆排序改进版：从底到顶建堆O(N)，排序过程O(N*logN)</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">void</span> heapSort() {
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">for</span> (<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> i = n - <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>; i &gt;= <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>; i--) heapify(i, n); <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// O(N) 建堆</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> size = n;
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">while</span> (size &gt; <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>) { swap(arr[<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>], arr[--size]); heapify(<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>, size); } <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 交换并调整</span>
}

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> main() {
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (scanf(<span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""%d""</span>, &amp;n) != <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">EOF</span>) {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">for</span> (<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> i = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>; i &lt; n; i++) scanf(<span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""%d""</span>, &amp;arr[i]);
        heapSort();
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">for</span> (<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> i = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>; i &lt; n; i++) printf(<span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""%d%c""</span>, arr[i], i == n - <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span> ? <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">'\n'</span> : <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">' '</span>);
    }
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>;
}

"<div style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(220, 220, 220); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(51, 51, 51); box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3) 0px 4px 6px; overflow-x: auto;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 025 堆结构和堆排序（填函数版）</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;algorithm&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">using</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">class</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">Solution</span> {
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// i位置的数变小了，向下调整大根堆</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">void</span> heapify(<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt;&amp; arr, <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> i, <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> size) {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> l = i * <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">2</span> + <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 左孩子下标</span>
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">while</span> (l &lt; size) {
            <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 评选最强的孩子：右孩子存在且比左孩子大，则选右，否则选左</span>
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> best = l + <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span> &lt; size &amp;&amp; arr[l + <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>] &gt; arr[l] ? l + <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span> : l;
            <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 父亲与最强的孩子PK，谁大谁是新的 best</span>
            best = arr[best] &gt; arr[i] ? best : i;
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (best == i) <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">break</span>; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 父亲最强，结构已稳</span>
            swap(arr[i], arr[best]); i = best; l = i * <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">2</span> + <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>;
        }
    }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 堆排序入口函数</span>
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt; sortArray(<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt;&amp; nums) {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> n = nums.size();
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (n &lt;= <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>) <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> nums;
        <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 从底到顶建立大根堆，时间复杂度 O(N)</span>
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">for</span> (<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> i = n - <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>; i &gt;= <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>; i--) heapify(nums, i, n);
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> size = n;
        <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 依次将堆顶（最大值）交换到末尾，并缩小堆范围进行调整</span>
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">while</span> (size &gt; <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>) {
            swap(nums[<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>], nums[--size]);
            heapify(nums, <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>, size);
        }
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> nums;
    }
};

            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 026 哈希表与哈希集合的基本用法</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;string&gt;</span>

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">struct</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">Student</span> { <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> age; <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">string</span> name; <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">Student</span>(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> a, <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">string</span> b) : age(a), name(b) {} };

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> main() {
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 1. 字符串比较逻辑</span>
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">string</span> str1 = <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""Hello""</span>, str2 = <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""Hello""</span>;
    cout &lt;&lt; (str1 == str2) &lt;&lt; endl; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// C++ string 的 == 直接比较值，返回 1 (true)</span>

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 2. unordered_set (哈希集合)</span>
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">unordered_set</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">string</span>&gt; <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">set</span>;
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">set</span>.insert(str1); <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 添加元素</span>
    cout &lt;&lt; <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">set</span>.count(<span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""Hello""</span>) &lt;&lt; endl; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// count 返回出现次数（0或1），模拟 contains</span>
    cout &lt;&lt; <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">set</span>.size() &lt;&lt; endl; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 获取大小</span>
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">set</span>.erase(str1); <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 删除元素</span>
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">set</span>.clear(); <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 清空集合</span>

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 3. unordered_map (哈希表)</span>
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">unordered_map</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">string</span>, <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">string</span>&gt; map1;
    map1[str1] = <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""World""</span>; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 插入或修改</span>
    cout &lt;&lt; map1.count(str2) &lt;&lt; endl; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 判断 key 是否存在</span>
    cout &lt;&lt; map1[<span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""Hello""</span>] &lt;&lt; endl; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 获取 value</span>
    map1.erase(<span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""Hello""</span>); <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 根据 key 删除</span>

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 4. 笔试技巧：用数组替代哈希表 (当 key 范围固定可控时)</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> arr[<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">100</span>] = {<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>}; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 假设 key 范围在 0-99</span>
    arr[<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">56</span>] = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">7285</span>; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 增/改，效率远高于哈希表</span>

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 5. 自定义对象作为 key</span>
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">Student</span> *s1 = <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">new</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">Student</span>(<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">17</span>, <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""张三""</span>), *s2 = <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">new</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">Student</span>(<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">17</span>, <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""张三""</span>);
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">unordered_map</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">Student</span>*, <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">string</span>&gt; map3; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 用指针模拟 Java 默认的引用比较</span>
    map3[s1] = <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""这是张三""</span>;
    cout &lt;&lt; (map3.count(s1)) &lt;&lt; <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">"" ""</span> &lt;&lt; (map3.count(s2)) &lt;&lt; endl; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// s1 存在，s2 不存在（地址不同）</span>

    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>;
}

            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 026 有序表与优先级队列</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;map&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;set&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;queue&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;string&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">using</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> main() {
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 1. TreeMap 对应 std::map，基于红黑树，Key 有序</span>
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">map</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>, <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">string</span>&gt; treeMap;
    treeMap[<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">5</span>] = <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""这是5""</span>; treeMap[<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">7</span>] = <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""这是7""</span>; treeMap[<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>] = <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""这是1""</span>;
    treeMap[<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">2</span>] = <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""这是2""</span>; treeMap[<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">3</span>] = <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""这是3""</span>; treeMap[<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">4</span>] = <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""这是4""</span>;
    treeMap[<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">8</span>] = <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""这是8""</span>;

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 查找与获取</span>
    cout &lt;&lt; treeMap.count(<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>) &lt;&lt; <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">"" ""</span> &lt;&lt; treeMap.count(<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">10</span>) &lt;&lt; endl; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// count=1 代表存在</span>
    treeMap[<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">4</span>] = <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""张三是4""</span>; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 修改 Value</span>
    treeMap.erase(<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">4</span>); <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 删除 Key</span>

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 获取最值</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (!treeMap.empty()) {
        cout &lt;&lt; treeMap.begin()-&gt;first &lt;&lt; endl;  <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 最小 Key: 1</span>
        cout &lt;&lt; treeMap.rbegin()-&gt;first &lt;&lt; endl; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 最大 Key: 8</span>
    }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// floorKey (&lt;=4 且最近): 找第一个 &gt;4 的元素，向前退一步</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">auto</span> it_f = treeMap.upper_bound(<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">4</span>);
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (it_f != treeMap.begin()) cout &lt;&lt; (--it_f)-&gt;first &lt;&lt; endl; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 输出 3</span>

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// ceilingKey (&gt;=4 且最近): 直接找第一个 &gt;=4 的元素</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">auto</span> it_c = treeMap.lower_bound(<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">4</span>);
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (it_c != treeMap.end()) cout &lt;&lt; it_c-&gt;first &lt;&lt; endl; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 输出 5 (因为4被删了)</span>

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 2. TreeSet 对应 std::set，有序且去重</span>
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">set</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt; treeSet = {<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">3</span>, <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">3</span>, <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">4</span>, <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">4</span>};
    cout &lt;&lt; <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""set size: ""</span> &lt;&lt; treeSet.size() &lt;&lt; endl; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 结果为 2</span>

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 3. PriorityQueue 对应 std::priority_queue</span>
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// C++ 默认是大根堆，Java 默认是小根堆</span>
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">priority_queue</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>, <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt;, greater&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt;&gt; minHeap; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 小根堆写法</span>
    minHeap.push(<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">3</span>); minHeap.push(<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">4</span>); minHeap.push(<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">3</span>);
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">while</span> (!minHeap.empty()) { cout &lt;&lt; minHeap.top() &lt;&lt; <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">"" ""</span>; minHeap.pop(); }

    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">priority_queue</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt; maxHeap; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 大根堆写法</span>
    maxHeap.push(<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">3</span>); maxHeap.push(<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">4</span>); maxHeap.push(<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">3</span>);
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">while</span> (!maxHeap.empty()) { cout &lt;&lt; maxHeap.top() &lt;&lt; <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">"" ""</span>; maxHeap.pop(); }

    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>;
}

    sort(arr.begin(), arr.end(), [](<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">const</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">Employee</span>&amp; a, <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">const</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">Employee</span>&amp; b) {

    });

    });

        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> a.age &lt; b.age;

    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>;

            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 027 合并K个有序链表</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;queue&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">using</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">struct</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">ListNode</span> { <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> val; <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">ListNode</span> *next; }; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 链表节点定义</span>

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">class</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">Solution</span> {
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 自定义比较器：值小的排在堆顶（实现小根堆）</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">struct</span> cmp { <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">bool</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">operator</span>()(<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">ListNode</span>* a, <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">ListNode</span>* b) { <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> a-&gt;val &gt; b-&gt;val; } };</pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">小根堆比较器

    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">ListNode</span>* mergeKLists(<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">ListNode</span>*&gt;&amp; lists) {
        <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">priority_queue</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">ListNode</span>*, <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">ListNode</span>*&gt;, cmp&gt; heap;
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">for</span> (<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">auto</span> h : lists) <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (h) heap.push(h); <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 1. 所有链表的头节点入堆</span>
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (heap.empty()) <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 若所有链表都为空</span>
        
        <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">ListNode</span> *head = heap.top(); heap.pop(); <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 2. 弹出全局最小作为合并后的头</span>
        <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">ListNode</span> *pre = head;
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (pre-&gt;next) heap.push(pre-&gt;next); <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 谁弹出，谁的下一个节点就入堆补位</span>
        
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">while</span> (!heap.empty()) {
            <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">ListNode</span> *cur = heap.top(); heap.pop(); <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 3. 弹出当前最小节点</span>
            pre-&gt;next = cur; pre = cur; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 4. 将其连在结果链表末尾</span>
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (cur-&gt;next) heap.push(cur-&gt;next); <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 5. 该节点的后续节点入堆</span>
        }
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> head;
    }
};
