            </span><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 028 基数排序</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">
</span><span style=""color: rgb(172, 118, 167);"">#include</span><span style=""color: rgb(197, 134, 192);""> </span><span style=""color: rgb(214, 157, 133);"">&lt;cstdio&gt;</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">
</span><span style=""color: rgb(172, 118, 167);"">#include</span><span style=""color: rgb(158, 110, 155);""> </span><span style=""color: rgb(214, 157, 133);"">&lt;algorithm&gt;</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">
</span><span style=""color: rgb(172, 118, 167);"">#include</span><span style=""color: rgb(197, 134, 192);""> </span><span style=""color: rgb(214, 157, 133);"">&lt;cstring&gt;</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">
</span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">using</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">namespace</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> std;

</span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">const</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> </span><span style=""color: rgb(78, 201, 176);"">BASE</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> = </span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">10</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">; </span><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 进制基数</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">
</span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">const</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> </span><span style=""color: rgb(78, 201, 176);"">MAXN</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> = </span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">100001</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">;
</span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> arr[</span><span style=""color: rgb(78, 201, 176);"">MAXN</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">], help[</span><span style=""color: rgb(78, 201, 176);"">MAXN</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">], cnts[</span><span style=""color: rgb(78, 201, 176);"">BASE</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">], n;

</span><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 获取当前最大值在BASE进制下的位数</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">
</span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> getBits(</span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> max_val) {
    </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> bits = </span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">0</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">;
    </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">while</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> (max_val &gt; </span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">0</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">) { bits++; max_val /= </span><span style=""color: rgb(78, 201, 176);"">BASE</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">; }
    </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">returnnn</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> bits;
}

</span><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 基数排序核心逻辑：按位从低到高进行计数排序</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">
</span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">void</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> radixSort(</span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> bits) {
    </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">for</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> (</span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> offset = </span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">1</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">; bits &gt; </span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">0</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">; offset *= </span><span style=""color: rgb(78, 201, 176);"">BASE</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">, bits--) {
        memset(cnts, </span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">0</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">, </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">sizeof</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">(cnts)); </span><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 每一轮清空计数器</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">
        </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">for</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> (</span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> i = </span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">0</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">; i &lt; n; i++) cnts[(arr[i] / offset) % </span><span style=""color: rgb(78, 201, 176);"">BASE</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">]++; </span><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 统计当前位各数字出现频次</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">
        </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">for</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> (</span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> i = </span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">1</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">; i &lt; </span><span style=""color: rgb(78, 201, 176);"">BASE</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">; i++) cnts[i] += cnts[i - </span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">1</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">]; </span><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 转换为前缀和，确定分区边界</span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">上面这一行，假设0一次 1一次 2二次 3一次</pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">那么前缀和一下0-1  1-2 2-4 3-5</pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">所以，如果是0 那就从0倒着排，如果是2就从3（下标）倒着排
        <span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 从后往前遍历以保证排序稳定性</span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">下面这行很难，就是前缀和数组直接找到下标，然后减减表示排序了一次，注意减减是先操作，这样可以定位下标
        <span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">for</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> (</span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> i = n - </span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">1</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">; i &gt;= </span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">0</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">; i--) help[--cnts[(arr[i] / offset) % </span><span style=""color: rgb(78, 201, 176);"">BASE</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">]] = arr[i];</span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">注意这里i初始值是n-1，i--，所以它是倒着排序，如果原本是23 24 15 36（已经经过第一轮个位数排序），它倒着排序就不会打乱个位数排序的结果。原本的24一定比23先排在后面
        </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">for</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> (</span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> i = </span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">0</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">; i &lt; n; i++) arr[i] = help[i]; </span><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 收集回原数组</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">
    }
}

</span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> main() {
    </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">if</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> (scanf(</span><span style=""color: rgb(214, 157, 133);"">""%d""</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">, &amp;n) != </span><span style=""color: rgb(78, 201, 176);"">EOF</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">) {
        </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> min_val = </span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">0</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">;
        </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">for</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> (</span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> i = </span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">0</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">; i &lt; n; i++) {
            scanf(</span><span style=""color: rgb(214, 157, 133);"">""%d""</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">, &amp;arr[i]);
            min_val = min(min_val, arr[i]);
        }
        </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> max_val = </span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">0</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">;
        </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">for</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> (</span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> i = </span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">0</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">; i &lt; n; i++) {
            arr[i] -= min_val; </span><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 平移成非负数</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">
            max_val = max(max_val, arr[i]);
        }
        radixSort(getBits(max_val)); </span><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 根据位数进行多轮排序</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">
        </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">for</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> (</span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> i = </span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">0</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">; i &lt; n; i++) printf(</span><span style=""color: rgb(214, 157, 133);"">""%d%c""</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">, arr[i] + min_val, i == n - </span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">1</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> ? </span><span style=""color: rgb(214, 157, 133);"">'\n'</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> : </span><span style=""color: rgb(214, 157, 133);"">' '</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">);
    }
    </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">return</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> </span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">0</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">;
}

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">class</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">Solution</span> {
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> missingNumber(<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt;&amp; nums) {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> eorAll = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>, eorHas = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>, n = nums.size();
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">for</span> (<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> i = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>; i &lt; n; i++) {
            eorAll ^= i;      <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 累积异或 0 到 n-1</span>

        }
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> eorAll ^ n ^ eorHas; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 补上最后一个数字 n 后整体异或，剩下的即为缺失值</span>
    }

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">class</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">Solution</span> {

        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">for</span> (<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> n : nums) eor1 ^= n; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 最终 eor1 = a ^ b</span>

        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> eor2 = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>;
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">for</span> (<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> n : nums) {
            <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 利用 rightOne 将数组分为两组，eor2 只负责其中一组</span>
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> ((n &amp; rightOne) == <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>) eor2 ^= n; 
        }
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> {eor2, (<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>)(eor1 ^ eor2)}; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 两个结果分别为 eor2 和 a ^ b ^ eor2</span>
    }

    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">bool</span> isPowerOfTwo(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> n) {

            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 031 返回大于等于 n 的最小 2 的幂</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">near2power</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (n &lt;= <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 规定非正数返回 1</span>
    n--; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 关键：防止 n 本身就是 2 的幂时结果翻倍</span>
    n |= (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">unsigned</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>)n &gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;  <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 将最高位的 1 拷贝到第 1 位</span>
    n |= (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">unsigned</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>)n &gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>;  <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 将连续的 1 拷贝到后续 2 位</span>
    n |= (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">unsigned</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>)n &gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">4</span>;  <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 拷贝到后续 4 位</span>
    n |= (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">unsigned</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>)n &gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">8</span>;  <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 拷贝到后续 8 位</span>
    n |= (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">unsigned</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>)n &gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">16</span>; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 拷贝到后续 16 位，至此 32 位全满</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> n + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 满位 11...11 加 1 变为 100...00</span>
}

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    cout &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">near2power</span>(<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">100</span>) &lt;&lt; endl; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 输出 128</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>

            </span><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 031 数字范围按位与</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">
</span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">class</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> </span><span style=""color: rgb(78, 201, 176);"">Solution</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> {
</span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">public</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">:
    </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> rangeBitwiseAnd(</span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> left, </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> right) {
        </span><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 核心：只要 left &lt; right，说明区间内必然有数使得 right 的低位 1 变 0</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">
        </span><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 利用 Brian Kernighan 算法不断抹掉 right 最右侧的 1</span><span style=""color: rgb(0, 255, 255);"">(效率极高）</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">
        </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">while</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> (left &lt; right) {
            </span><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// right &amp; -right 提取最右侧的 1，减去它即为抹掉该位</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">
            right -= right &amp; -right; 
        }
        </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">return</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> right;
    }
};

        </span></div>

"<div style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(51, 51, 51); box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3) 0px 4px 6px; overflow-x: auto;"">
            <pre style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220); margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 032 位图的实现</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">using</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">class</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">Bitset</span> {
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt; <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">set</span>;
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 构造函数：n个数字需要 (n+31)/32 个 int 空间</span>
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">Bitset</span>(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> n) : <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">set</span>((n + <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">31</span>) / <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">32</span>, <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>) {}

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 添加数字：将对应位置的 bit 设为 1</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">void</span> add(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> num) { <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">set</span>[num &gt;&gt; <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">5</span>] |= (<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span> &lt;&lt; (num &amp; <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">31</span>)); } <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// num/32 可写为 num&gt;&gt;5</span>
<strong><code>num &amp; 31</code></strong>：等同于&nbsp;<code>num % 32</code>
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 删除数字：将对应位置的 bit 设为 0</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">void</span> remove(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> num) { <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">set</span>[num &gt;&gt; <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">5</span>] &amp;= ~(<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span> &lt;&lt; (num &amp; <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">31</span>)); } <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 使用取反掩码</span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">保护其他位置

    <span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 翻转数字：1变0，0变1</span><font color=""#dcdcdc"">
    </font><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">void</span><font color=""#dcdcdc""> reverse(</font><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><font color=""#dcdcdc""> num) { </font><span style=""color: rgb(78, 201, 176);"">set</span><font color=""#dcdcdc"">[num &gt;&gt; </font><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">5</span><font color=""#dcdcdc"">] ^= (</font><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">1</span><font color=""#dcdcdc""> &lt;&lt; (num &amp; </font><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">31</span><font color=""#dcdcdc"">)); }

    </font><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 查询数字：检查对应 bit 是否为 1</span><font color=""#dcdcdc"">
    </font><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">bool</span><font color=""#dcdcdc""> contains(</font><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><font color=""#dcdcdc""> num) { </font><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">return</span><font color=""#dcdcdc""> (</font><span style=""color: rgb(78, 201, 176);"">set</span><font color=""#dcdcdc"">[num &gt;&gt; </font><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">5</span><font color=""#dcdcdc"">] &gt;&gt; (num &amp; </font><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">31</span><font color=""#dcdcdc"">)) &amp; </font><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">1</span><font color=""#dcdcdc"">; }
};

"<div style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(51, 51, 51); box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3) 0px 4px 6px; overflow-x: auto;""><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">
            </span><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 032 设计位图（支持O(1)翻转）</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">
</span><span style=""color: rgb(197, 134, 192);"">#include </span><span style=""color: rgb(214, 157, 133);"">&lt;vector&gt;</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">
</span><span style=""color: rgb(197, 134, 192);"">#include </span><span style=""color: rgb(214, 157, 133);"">&lt;string&gt;</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">
</span><span style=""color: rgb(197, 134, 192);"">#include </span><span style=""color: rgb(214, 157, 133);"">&lt;algorithm&gt;</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">
</span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">using</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">namespace</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> std;

</span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">class</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> </span><span style=""color: rgb(78, 201, 176);"">Bitset</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> {
    </span><span style=""color: rgb(78, 201, 176);"">vector</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">&lt;</span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">&gt; </span><span style=""color: rgb(78, 201, 176);"">set</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">; </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> sz, zeros, ones; </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">bool</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> rev; </span><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 数组、总大小、0计数、1计数、翻转标志</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">
</span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">public</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">:
    </span><span style=""color: rgb(78, 201, 176);"">Bitset</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">(</span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> n) : </span><span style=""color: rgb(78, 201, 176);"">set</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">((n + </span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">31</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">) / </span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">32</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">, </span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">0</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">), sz(n), zeros(n), ones(</span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">0</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">), rev(</span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">false</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">) {}

    </span><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 将第i位设为1：根据rev状态判断当前位是否已经是逻辑上的1</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">
    </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">void</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> fix(</span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> i) {
        </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> idx = i &gt;&gt; </span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">5</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">, bit = i &amp; </span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">31</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">;
        </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">if</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> (!rev) { </span><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 正常模式：1是1。若为0则变1。</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">
            </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">if</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> (!(</span><span style=""color: rgb(78, 201, 176);"">set</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">[idx] &amp; (</span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">1</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> &lt;&lt; bit))) { zeros--; ones++; </span><span style=""color: rgb(78, 201, 176);"">set</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">[idx] |= (</span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">1</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> &lt;&lt; bit); }
        } </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">else</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> { </span><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 翻转模式：0是1。若为1则变0。</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">
            </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">if</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> (</span><span style=""color: rgb(78, 201, 176);"">set</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">[idx] &amp; (</span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">1</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> &lt;&lt; bit)) { zeros--; ones++; </span><span style=""color: rgb(78, 201, 176);"">set</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">[idx] ^= (</span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">1</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> &lt;&lt; bit); }
        }
    }

    </span><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 将第i位设为0：逻辑同上</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">
    </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">void</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> unfix(</span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> i) {
        </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> idx = i &gt;&gt; </span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">5</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">, bit = i &amp; </span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">31</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">;</span><span style=""color: rgb(83, 158, 71);"">//这个就是%31</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">
        </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">if</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> (!rev) { </span><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 正常模式：0是0。若为1则变0。</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">
            </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">if</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> (</span><span style=""color: rgb(78, 201, 176);"">set</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">[idx] &amp; (</span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">1</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> &lt;&lt; bit)) { ones--; zeros++; </span><span style=""color: rgb(78, 201, 176);"">set</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">[idx] ^= (</span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">1</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> &lt;&lt; bit); }
        } </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">else</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> { </span><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 翻转模式：1是0。若为0则变1。</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">
            </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">if</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> (!(</span><span style=""color: rgb(78, 201, 176);"">set</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">[idx] &amp; (</span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">1</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> &lt;&lt; bit))) { ones--; zeros++; </span><span style=""color: rgb(78, 201, 176);"">set</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">[idx] |= (</span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">1</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> &lt;&lt; bit); }
        }
    }

    </span><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// O(1)翻转：切换解释权，并交换0和1的计数</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">
    </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">void</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> flip() { rev = !rev; swap(ones, zeros); }

    </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">bool</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> all() { </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">return</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> ones == sz; } </span><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 1的数量等于总大小</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">
    </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">bool</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> one() { </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">return</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> ones &gt; </span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">0</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">; }   </span><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 1的数量大于0</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">
    </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> count() { </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">return</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> ones; }

    </span><span style=""color: rgb(78, 201, 176);"">string</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> toString() {
        </span><span style=""color: rgb(78, 201, 176);"">string</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> res = </span><span style=""color: rgb(214, 157, 133);"">""""</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">;
        </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">for</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> (</span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> i = </span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">0</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">, k = </span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">0</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">; i &lt; sz; k++) {
            </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> val = </span><span style=""color: rgb(78, 201, 176);"">set</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">[k];
            </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">for</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> (</span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> j = </span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">0</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">; j &lt; </span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">32</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> &amp;&amp; i &lt; sz; j++, i++) {
                </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> s = (val &gt;&gt; j) &amp; </span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">1</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">; </span><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 提取原始状态</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">
                res += (s ^ (rev ? </span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">1</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> : </span><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">0</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">)) + </span><span style=""color: rgb(214, 157, 133);"">'0'</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">; </span><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 根据rev异或出逻辑状态</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);"">
            }
        }
        </span><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">return</span><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220);""> res;
    }
};

"<div style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(51, 51, 51); box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3) 0px 4px 6px; overflow-x: auto;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><font color=""#c586c0"">乘法中有补码溢出，非常难</font></pre><pre style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220); margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;climits&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">class</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">Solution</span> {
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 加法：无进位相加 (^) 与 进位信息 (&amp; &lt;&lt; 1) 循环迭代</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> add(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> a, <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> b) {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">while</span> (b != <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>) {
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> sum = a ^ b;                       <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 无进位相加</span>
            b = (<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">unsigned</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>)(a &amp; b) &lt;&lt; <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>;        <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 计算进位并左移</span>
            a = sum;
        }
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> a;
    }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 取负：取反加 1 (~n + 1)</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> neg(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> n) { 
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> add(~n, <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>); 
    }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 减法：a - b 等于 a + (-b)</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> minus(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> a, <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> b) { 
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> add(a, neg(b)); 
    }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 乘法：模拟手工竖式乘法，b 的每一位 1 去乘并累加 a 的位移结果</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> multiply(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> a, <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> b) {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> ans = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>;
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">unsigned</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> ub = (<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">unsigned</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>)b;</pre><pre style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220); margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">这里一定要把b转为无符号，这样可以处理负数，也可以处理a和b同时为负数</pre><pre style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220); margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">        
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">while</span> (ub != <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>) {
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (ub &amp; <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>) {
                ans = add(ans, a);                 <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 只要 b 最右侧是 1，就累加当前的 a</span>
            }
            a &lt;&lt;= <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>; 
            ub &gt;&gt;= <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>;
        }
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> ans;
    }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 基础除法：类似长除法，从高位向低位试除</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> div(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> a, <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> b) {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> x = (a &lt; <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>) ? neg(a) : a;
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> y = (b &lt; <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>) ? neg(b) : b;
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> ans = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>;

        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">for</span> (<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> i = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">30</span>; i &gt;= <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>; i = minus(i, <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>)) {
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> ((x &gt;&gt; i) &gt;= y) {
                ans |= (<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span> &lt;&lt; i);
                x = minus(x, y &lt;&lt; i);
            }
        }
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> (a &lt; <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span> ^ b &lt; <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>) ? neg(ans) : ans;
    }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 完整除法：处理 INT_MIN 溢出和边界</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> divide(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> a, <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> b) {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (a == <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">INT_MIN</span> &amp;&amp; b == <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">INT_MIN</span>) <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>;
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (b == <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">INT_MIN</span>) <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>;

        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (a == <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">INT_MIN</span>) {
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (b == neg(<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>)) <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">INT_MAX</span>;       <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 溢出特例：-2147483648 / -1</span>
            
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> offset = (b &gt; <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>) ? b : neg(b);</pre><pre style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220); margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">遇到最小值，不能取绝对值，会超出数值范围。但是可以先将它减小（加上一个整数，也就是加b）
            <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 补偿法：先加一个 |b| 缩小范围再除</span>
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> ans = div(add(a, offset), b);

        }

        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> div(a, b);
    }
};

            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 034 返回两个无环链表相交的第一个节点</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">struct</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span> { <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> val; <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span> *next; }; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 链表节点定义</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">class</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Solution</span> {
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span> *<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">getIntersectionNode</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span> *h1, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span> *h2) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (!h1 || !h2) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>;
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span> *a = h1, *b = h2;
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> diff = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 走到尾部并计算长度差值：a每走一步diff自增，b每走一步diff自减</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (a-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>) { a = a-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>; diff++; }
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (b-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>) { b = b-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>; diff--; }
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (a != b) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 如果尾节点地址不同，说明两个链表根本没连在一起</span>
        a = diff &gt;= <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span> ? h1 : h2; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 令 a 指向长链表的头，b 指向短链表的头</span>
        b = a == h1 ? h2 : h1;
        diff = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">abs</span>(diff); <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 取差值的绝对值</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (diff--) a = a-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 4. 长链表先走完多出来的部分</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (a != b) { a = a-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>; b = b-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>; } <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 5. 两者同步走，碰撞处即为交点</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> a;
    }
};

            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#57A64A"">// 034 每k个节点一组翻转链表</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#D69D85"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">struct</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span> { <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> val; <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span> *next; }; <span style=""color:#57A64A"">// 节点定义</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">class</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Solution</span> {
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color:#57A64A"">// 找到从s开始第k个节点并返回，若不足k个则返回nullptr</span>
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span>* <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">teamEnd</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span>* s, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> k) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (--k &gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span> &amp;&amp; s) s = s.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> s;
    }

    <span style=""color:#57A64A"">// 翻转从s到e的局部链表，并让原头部s指向下一组的开头</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">reverse</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span>* s, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span>* e) {
        e = e-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>; <span style=""color:#57A64A"">// 暂存下一组的开头</span>
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span> *pre = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>, *cur = s, *nxt = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (cur != e) { <span style=""color:#57A64A"">// 标准三指针翻转</span>
            nxt = cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>;
            cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span> = pre;
            pre = cur;
            cur = nxt;
        }
        s-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span> = e; <span style=""color:#57A64A"">// 翻转后s成了尾部，接上下一组</span>
    }

    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span>* <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">reverseKGroup</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span>* head, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> k) {
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span> *start = head, *end = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">teamEnd</span>(start, k);
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (!end) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> head; <span style=""color:#57A64A"">// 第一组都不够k个，直接返回</span>
        head = end; <span style=""color:#57A64A"">// 第一组翻转后的新头就是全链表的新头</span>
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">reverse</span>(start, end);
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span>* lastEnd = start; <span style=""color:#57A64A"">// 记录上一组翻转后的结尾</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (lastEnd-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>) {
            start = lastEnd-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>;
            end = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">teamEnd</span>(start, k);
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (!end) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> head; <span style=""color:#57A64A"">// 剩余部分不足k个，停止翻转</span>
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">reverse</span>(start, end);
            lastEnd-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span> = end; <span style=""color:#57A64A"">// 重要：上一组结尾指向本组翻转后的新头</span>
            lastEnd = start; <span style=""color:#57A64A"">// 更新上一组结尾</span>
        }
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> head;
    }
};

            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 034 复制带随机指针的链表</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">struct</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Node</span> { <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> val; <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Node</span> *next, *random; <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Node</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> v) : <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">val</span>(v), <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">next</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>), <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">random</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>) {} };

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">class</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Solution</span> {
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Node</span>* <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">copyRandomList</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Node</span>* head) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (!head) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>;
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Node</span> *cur = head, *nxt = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>, *copy = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>;
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 克隆节点并插空：1 -&gt; 2 变为 1 -&gt; 1' -&gt; 2 -&gt; 2'</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (cur) {
            nxt = cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>;
            cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span> = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">new</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Node</span>(cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">val</span>);

            cur = nxt;
        }
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 设置克隆节点的 random 指针：copy-&gt;random = cur-&gt;random-&gt;next</span>

        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (cur) {
            nxt = cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>;
            copy = cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>;
            copy-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">random</span> = cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">random</span> ? cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">random</span>-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span> : <span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>;因为next才是copy要指的地方，问号前面那个结点是条件
            cur = nxt;</pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">图示：
   +------------------+
   |                  v
 [ 1 ] -&gt; [ 1' ] -&gt; [ 2 ] -&gt; [ 2' ] -&gt; [ 3 ] -&gt; [ 3' ]
            |                            ^
            +----------------------------+
        }
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 拆分链表：恢复原链表并提取克隆链表</span>
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Node</span>* ans = head-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>;
        cur = head;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (cur) {
            nxt = cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>;

            cur = nxt;
        }
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> ans;
    }

            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 034 判断链表是否是回文结构</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">struct</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span> {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> val;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span> *next;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">class</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Solution</span> {
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">bool</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">isPalindrome</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span>* head) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (!head || !head-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">true</span>;</pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">1 -&gt; 2 -&gt; 3 &lt;- 2 &lt;- 1 核心

        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 快慢指针找中点</span>
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span> *slow = head;
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span> *fast = head;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (fast-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span> &amp;&amp; fast-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>) {
            slow = slow-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>;
            fast = fast-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>;
        }

        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 反转后半部分链表</span>
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span> *pre = slow;
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span> *cur = slow-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>;
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span> *nxt = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>;
        pre-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span> = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 断开前半部分</span>

        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (cur) {
            nxt = cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>;
            cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span> = pre;
            pre = cur;
            cur = nxt;
        }

        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 双端对比判断回文</span>
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span> *l = head;
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span> *r = pre; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// pre 现在是原链表的尾节点，反转后的头节点</span>
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">bool</span> ans = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">true</span>;
        
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (l &amp;&amp; r) {
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (l-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">val</span> != r-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">val</span>) {
                ans = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">false</span>;
                <span style=""color:#C586C0"">break</span>;
            }
            l = l-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>;
            r = r-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>;
        }

        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 4. 准备还原链表结构 (保持原样是良好的编程习惯)</span>
        cur = pre-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>;
        pre-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span> = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>;
        
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (cur) {
            nxt = cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>;
            cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span> = pre;
            pre = cur;
            cur = nxt;
        }

        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> ans;
    }
};

            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 035 带 setAll 功能的哈希表</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;cstdio&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;unordered_map&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">using</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 存储结构：first为值，second为时间戳</span>
<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">unordered_map</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>, <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">pair</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>, <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt;&gt; dataMap;
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> setAllValue, setAllTime = -<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>, cnt = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 全局setAll值、全局时间、当前时间计数</span>

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">void</span> put(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> k, <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> v) { dataMap[k] = {v, cnt++}; } <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 正常放入，赋予当前时间戳</span>

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">void</span> setAll(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> v) { setAllValue = v; setAllTime = cnt++; } <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 更新全局值，更新全局时间</span>

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> get(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> k) {
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (dataMap.find(k) == dataMap.end()) <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> -<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 不存在返回-1</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">auto</span>&amp; p = dataMap[k];
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 如果记录的时间戳早于 setAll 时间，说明该值已被覆盖</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> p.second &gt; setAllTime ? p.first : setAllValue;
}

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> main() {
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> n, op, a, b;
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">while</span> (scanf(<span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""%d""</span>, &amp;n) != <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">EOF</span>) {
        dataMap.clear(); setAllTime = -<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>; cnt = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 每一组测试数据前重置</span>
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">for</span> (<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> i = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>; i &lt; n; i++) {
            scanf(<span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""%d""</span>, &amp;op);
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (op == <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>) { scanf(<span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""%d %d""</span>, &amp;a, &amp;b); put(a, b); }
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">else</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (op == <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">2</span>) { scanf(<span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""%d""</span>, &amp;a); printf(<span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""%d\n""</span>, get(a)); }
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">else</span> { scanf(<span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""%d""</span>, &amp;a); setAll(a); }
        }
    }
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>;
}

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 035 实现 LRU 结构</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;unordered_map&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 双向链表节点定义</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">struct</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Node</span> {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> k, v;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Node</span> *last;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Node</span> *next;

    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Node</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> key, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> val) 
        : <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">k</span>(key), <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">v</span>(val), <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">last</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>), <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">next</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>) {}
};

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">class</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">LRUCache</span> {
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">private</span>:
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">unordered_map</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Node</span>*&gt; <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">map</span>;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Node</span> *head; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 头部节点，表示最久未访问 (Least Recently Used)</span>
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Node</span> *tail; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 尾部节点，表示最新访问 (Most Recently Used)</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> cap;

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 将节点移动到尾部：表示该节点刚被访问，优先级提升到最高</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">moveToTail</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Node</span>* node) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (tail == node) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span>;

        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (head == node) {
            head = node-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>;
            head-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">last</span> = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>;
        } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 从中间位置摘除节点</span>
            node-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">last</span>-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span> = node-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>;
            node-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">last</span> = node-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">last</span>;
        }

        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 重新连接到尾部</span>
        node-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">last</span> = tail;
        node-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span> = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>;
        tail-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span> = node;
        tail = node;
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 移除头部节点：淘汰那个最久没被访问的节点</span>
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Node</span>* <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">removeHead</span>() {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (!head) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>;

        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Node</span>* res = head;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (head == tail) {
            head = tail = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>;
        } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
            head = head-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>;
            head-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">last</span> = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>;
            res-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span> = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>;
        }
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> res;
    }

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">LRUCache</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> capacity) 
        : <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">head</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>), <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">tail</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>), <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">cap</span>(capacity) {}

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 获取数据：若存在则移动到尾部并返回值，否则返回 -1</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">get</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> key) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">map</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">find</span>(key) == <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">map</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">end</span>()) {
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> -<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
        }
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">moveToTail</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">map</span>[key]);
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">map</span>[key]-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">v</span>;
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 存入数据：若存在则更新并移到尾部；若不存在，满额则踢掉头节点再插入新节点</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">put</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> key, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> value) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">map</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">count</span>(key)) {
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 节点已存在，更新值并移动到末尾</span>
            <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">map</span>[key]-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">v</span> = value;
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">moveToTail</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">map</span>[key]);
        } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 节点不存在，检查容量</span>
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">map</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>() == cap) {
                <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Node</span>* old = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">removeHead</span>();
                <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">map</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">erase</span>(old-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">k</span>);
                <span style=""color:#569CD6"">delete</span> old;
            }

            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 插入新节点</span>
            <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Node</span>* node = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">new</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Node</span>(key, value);
            <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">map</span>[key] = node;

            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (!head) {
                head = tail = node;
            } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
                tail-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span> = node;
                node-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">last</span> = tail;
                tail = node;
            }
        }
    }
};

            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 035 插入、删除和获取随机元素 O(1)</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;unordered_map&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;cstdlib&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">using</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">class</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">RandomizedSet</span> {
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">unordered_map</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>, <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt; <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">map</span>; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// key: 元素值, value: 在数组中的下标</span>
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt; arr;            <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 存储实际元素，用于随机访问</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">RandomizedSet</span>() {}

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 插入：若不存在，则加到数组末尾并在哈希表记录下标</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">bool</span> insert(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> val) {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">map</span>.count(val)) <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">false</span>;
        <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">map</span>[val] = arr.size(); arr.push_back(val);
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">true</span>;
    }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 删除：将待删元素与末尾元素交换，更新末尾元素的下标，最后弹出</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">bool</span> remove(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> val) {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (!<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">map</span>.count(val)) <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">false</span>;
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> idx = <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">map</span>[val], lastVal = arr.back();
        arr[idx] = lastVal; <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">map</span>[lastVal] = idx; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 覆盖待删位置，更新末尾值下标</span>
        arr.pop_back(); <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">map</span>.erase(val);         <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 物理删除末尾，删除哈希记录</span>
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">true</span>;
    }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 随机获取：利用数组下标实现等概率随机</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> getRandom() { <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> arr[rand() % arr.size()]; }
};

            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 035 插入、删除和获取随机元素 O(1) 允许重复</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;unordered_map&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;unordered_set&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;cstdlib&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">using</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">namespace</span> std;
一个map一个arr
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">class</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">RandomizedCollection</span> {
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">unordered_map</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>, <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">unordered_set</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt;&gt; <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">map</span>; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// key: 值, value: 该值出现的所有下标集合</span>
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt; arr; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 存储实际数据</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">RandomizedCollection</span>() {}

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 插入：记录下标并加入数组。若该值之前不存在则返回 true</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">bool</span> insert(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> val) {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">bool</span> res = <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">map</span>[val].empty();
        <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">map</span>[val].insert(arr.size()); arr.push_back(val);
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> res;
    }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 删除：取任意一个下标，用数组末尾元素覆盖之。</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">bool</span> remove(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> val) {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">map</span>[val].empty()) <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">false</span>;
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> idx = *<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">map</span>[val].begin(), lastVal = arr.back(); <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 取出待删位和末尾值</span>
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (val == lastVal) { <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 特殊处理：如果要删的就是末尾的值</span>
            <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">map</span>[val].erase(arr.size() - <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>);
        } <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">else</span> {</pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">先讲lastval的map中的地址改，然后再把arr中val（要删除）的数据用lastval覆盖。接着抹除lastval原本的map位置。再将val的map地址删除。
            <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">map</span>[lastVal].insert(idx); <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 1. 末尾值的新家</span>
            arr[idx] = lastVal;      <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 2. 物理覆盖</span>
            <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">map</span>[lastVal].erase(arr.size() - <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>); <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 3. 抹除末尾旧址</span>
            <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">map</span>[val].erase(idx);     <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 4. 抹除待删位</span>
        }</pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">最后把lastval的原本arr中的位置减掉
        arr.pop_back(); <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 5. 缩容</span>
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">true</span>;
    }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 随机获取：数组下标 O(1) 等概率</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> getRandom() { <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> arr[rand() % arr.size()]; }
};

"<div style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(220, 220, 220); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(51, 51, 51); box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3) 0px 4px 6px; overflow-x: auto;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 035 快速获得数据流的中位数的结构</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;queue&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;cmath&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">using</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">class</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">MedianFinder</span> {
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">priority_queue</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt; maxH; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 大根堆：存较小的一半</span>
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">priority_queue</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>, <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt;, greater&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt;&gt; minH; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 小根堆：存较大的一半</span>
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 维持两个堆的数量平衡，差值不能超过1</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">void</span> balance() {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (abs((<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>)maxH.size() - (<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>)minH.size()) == <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">2</span>) {
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (maxH.size() &gt; minH.size()) { minH.push(maxH.top()); maxH.pop(); }
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">else</span> { maxH.push(minH.top()); minH.pop(); }
        }
    }
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">MedianFinder</span>() {}
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 新增数字：根据与大根堆顶的比较决定去向，并调平衡</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">void</span> addNum(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> num) {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (maxH.empty() || maxH.top() &gt;= num) maxH.push(num);
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">else</span> minH.push(num);
        balance();
    }
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 获取中位数：数量不等取较多的堆顶，相等则取两堆顶平均值</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">double</span> findMedian() {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (maxH.size() == minH.size()) <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> (maxH.top() + minH.top()) / <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">2</span>.<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>;
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> maxH.size() &gt; minH.size() ? maxH.top() : minH.top();
    }
};
</pre>
        </div>
        <br>"	
"<div style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(220, 220, 220); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(51, 51, 51); box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3) 0px 4px 6px; overflow-x: auto;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 035 最大频率栈</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;unordered_map&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;algorithm&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">using</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">class</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">FreqStack</span> {
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> topTimes = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 当前出现的最大频率</span>
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">unordered_map</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>, <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt;&gt; cntValues; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 频率 -&gt; 该频率下的元素栈</span>
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">unordered_map</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>, <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt; valueTimes; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 元素 -&gt; 当前出现的次数</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 入栈：更新频率，并将元素加入对应频率的层级中</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">void</span> push(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> val) {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> curTimes = ++valueTimes[val]; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 频率加1</span>
        cntValues[curTimes].push_back(val); <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 加入对应频率层</span>
        topTimes = max(topTimes, curTimes); <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 更新最高频率</span>
    }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 出栈：从最高频率层弹出最近进入的元素</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> pop() {
        <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt;&amp; topStack = cntValues[topTimes];
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> ans = topStack.back(); topStack.pop_back(); <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 弹出最高频层末尾元素</span>
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (topStack.empty()) cntValues.erase(topTimes--); <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 该层空了，最高频率下降</span>
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (--valueTimes[ans] == <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>) valueTimes.erase(ans); <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 更新元素总频率</span>
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> ans;
    }
};
</pre>
