"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 035 全 O(1) 的数据结构</span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;unordered_map&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;unordered_set&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;string&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">class</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">AllOne</span> {
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">private</span>:
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 桶结构：具有相同频率的 Key 存放在同一个桶里</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">struct</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Bucket</span> {
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> cnt;
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">unordered_set</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span>&gt; keys;
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Bucket</span> *last, *next;

        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Bucket</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> s, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> c) : <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">cnt</span>(c), <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">last</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>), <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">next</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>) {
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (s != <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""""</span>) keys.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">insert</span>(s);
        }
    };

    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Bucket</span> *head, *tail;               <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 哨兵节点：头（最小频率）、尾（最大频率）</span>
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">unordered_map</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span>, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Bucket</span>*&gt; <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">map</span>; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 快速查找 Key 对应的桶</span>

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 在 cur 桶后面插入一个新桶 pos</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">insert</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Bucket</span>* cur, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Bucket</span>* pos) {
        pos-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span> = cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>;
        pos-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">last</span> = cur;
        cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">last</span> = pos;
        cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span> = pos;
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 从双向链表中移除空桶</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">remove</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Bucket</span>* cur) {
        cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">last</span>-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span> = cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>;
        cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">last</span> = cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">last</span>;
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">delete</span> cur;
    }

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">AllOne</span>() {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 初始化哨兵，head 为最小值，tail 为最大值</span>
        head = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">new</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Bucket</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""""</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>);
        tail = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">new</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Bucket</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""""</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2147483647</span>);
        head-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span> = tail;
        tail-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">last</span> = head;
    }
    
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 增加 Key 的频率</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">inc</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> key) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">map</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">find</span>(key) == <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">map</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">end</span>()) { 
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 情况 1: 新增 Key，目标频率为 1</span>
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (head-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">cnt</span> != <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>) {
                <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 如果当前不存在频率为 1 的桶，则新建</span>
                <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">insert</span>(head, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">new</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Bucket</span>(key, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>));
            } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
                <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 否则直接加入频率为 1 的桶</span>
                head-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">keys</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">insert</span>(key);
            }
            <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">map</span>[key] = head-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>;
        } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> { 
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 情况 2: 已有 Key，频率 +1</span>
            <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Bucket</span> *cur = <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">map</span>[key];
            <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Bucket</span> *nxt = cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>;

            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (nxt-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">cnt</span> != cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">cnt</span> + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>) {
                <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 如果不存在频率为 cur-&gt;cnt + 1 的桶，则新建</span>
                nxt = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">new</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Bucket</span>(key, cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">cnt</span> + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
                <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">insert</span>(cur, nxt);
            } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
                <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 否则加入已有的频率桶</span>
                nxt-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">keys</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">insert</span>(key);
            }
            <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">map</span>[key] = nxt;
            
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 从原桶移除，若原桶变空则删除原桶</span>
            cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">keys</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">erase</span>(key);
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">keys</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">empty</span>()) <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">remove</span>(cur);
        }
    }
    
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 减少 Key 的频率</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">dec</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> key) {
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Bucket</span> *cur = <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">map</span>[key];

        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">cnt</span> == <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>) {
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 频率降为 0，直接从哈希表中移除</span>
            <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">map</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">erase</span>(key);
        } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 频率减少，移动到前一个频率桶</span>
            <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Bucket</span> *pre = cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">last</span>;
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (pre-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">cnt</span> != cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">cnt</span> - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>) {
                <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 如果前一个桶频率不匹配，新建频率桶</span>
                pre = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">new</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Bucket</span>(key, cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">cnt</span> - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
                <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">insert</span>(cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">last</span>, pre);
            } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
                pre-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">keys</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">insert</span>(key);
            }
            <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">map</span>[key] = pre;
        }

        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 清理旧桶逻辑</span>
        cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">keys</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">erase</span>(key);
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">keys</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">empty</span>()) <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">remove</span>(cur);
    }
    
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 获取频率最高的 Key</span>
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">getMaxKey</span>() {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// tail-&gt;last 如果是 head，说明链表为空</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> tail-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">last</span> == head ? <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""""</span> : *tail-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">last</span>-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">keys</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">begin</span>();
    }
    
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 获取频率最低的 Key</span>
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">getMinKey</span>() {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// head-&gt;next 如果是 tail，说明链表为空</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> head-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span> == tail ? <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""""</span> : *head-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">keys</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">begin</span>();
    }
};

"<div style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(220, 220, 220); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(51, 51, 51); box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3) 0px 4px 6px; overflow-x: auto;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><div><div><div>输入一个偶数&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>，验证&nbsp;4∼<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>&nbsp;所有偶数是否符合哥德巴赫猜想：任一大于&nbsp;2&nbsp;的偶数都可写成两个质数之和。如果一个数不止一种分法，则输出第一个加数相比其他分法最小的方案。例如&nbsp;10，10=3+7=5+5，则&nbsp;10=5+5&nbsp;是错误答案。</div></div></div><h2>输入格式</h2><div><div><div>第一行输入一个正偶数&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span></div></div></div><h2>输出格式</h2><div><div><div>输出&nbsp;2<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>−2​&nbsp;行。对于第&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>&nbsp;行：</div><div>首先先输出正偶数&nbsp;2<span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>+2，然后输出等号，再输出加和为&nbsp;2<span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>+2&nbsp;且第一个加数最小的两个质数，以加号隔开。</div></div></div><h2>输入输出样例</h2><div><div><div><b>输入 #1</b>复制</div><pre>10</pre></div><div><div><b>输出 #1</b>复制</div><pre>4=2+2
6=3+3
8=3+5
10=3+7</pre></div></div></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""font-family: inherit; color: rgb(197, 134, 192);"">#include </span><span style=""font-family: inherit; color: rgb(214, 157, 133);"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span><br></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #569CD6;"">using</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 判断一个数是否为质数</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">bool</span> isPrime(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> x) {
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (x &lt;= <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>) <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">false</span>;   <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 1及以下不是质数</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (x == <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">2</span>) <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">true</span>;    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 2是质数</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (x % <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">2</span> == <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>) <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">false</span>; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 偶数（除2外）不是质数</span>
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 从3开始，遍历到sqrt(x)，步长为2（只检查奇数）</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">for</span> (<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> i = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">3</span>; i * i &lt;= x; i += <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">2</span>) {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (x % i == <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>) <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">false</span>;
    }
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">true</span>;
}

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> main() {
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">N</span>;
    cin &gt;&gt; <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">N</span>;  <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 输入正偶数N</span>
    
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 遍历4到N之间的所有偶数</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">for</span> (<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> num = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">4</span>; num &lt;= <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">N</span>; num += <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">2</span>) {
        <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 寻找第一个加数最小的质数对</span>
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">for</span> (<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> p = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">2</span>; p &lt;= num / <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">2</span>; ++p) {
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (isPrime(p) &amp;&amp; isPrime(num - p)) {
                cout &lt;&lt; num &lt;&lt; <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""=""</span> &lt;&lt; p &lt;&lt; <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""+""</span> &lt;&lt; (num - p) &lt;&lt; endl;
                <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">break</span>; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 找到最小的p后，跳出循环处理下一个偶数</span>
            }
        }
    }
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>;
}</pre>
        </div>
        <br><br>"	
"<div style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(220, 220, 220); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(51, 51, 51); box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3) 0px 4px 6px; overflow-x: auto;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 036 二叉树的层序遍历</span>
<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 1. 二叉树节点结构定义 (TreeNode Struct)</span>
<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 2. 普通BFS解法 (使用哈希表记录层级的BFS)</span>
<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 3. 优化BFS解法 (手动数组模拟队列，分层处理的优化BFS)</span>

<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;queue&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;unordered_map&gt;</span>

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">using</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 不提交这个类</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">struct</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span> {
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> val;
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span> *left;
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span> *right;
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> x) : val(x), left(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>), right(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {}
};

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">class</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">Code01_LevelOrderTraversal</span> {
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 提交时把方法名改为levelOrder，此方法为普通bfs，此题不推荐</span>
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt;&gt; levelOrder1(<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>* root) {
        <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt;&gt; ans;
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (root != <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {
            <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">queue</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>*&gt; q;
            <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">unordered_map</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>*, <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt; levels;
            q.push(root);
            levels[root] = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>;
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">while</span> (!q.empty()) {
                <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>* cur = q.front();
                q.pop();
                <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> level = levels[cur];
                <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 如果结果数组大小等于当前层级，说明开启了新的一层</span>
                <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (ans.size() == level) {
                    ans.push_back(<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt;());
                }
                ans[level].push_back(cur-&gt;val);
                <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (cur-&gt;left != <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {
                    q.push(cur-&gt;left);
                    levels[cur-&gt;left] = level + <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>;
                }
                <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (cur-&gt;right != <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {
                    q.push(cur-&gt;right);
                    levels[cur-&gt;right] = level + <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>;
                }
            }
        }
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> ans;
    }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 如果测试数据量变大了就修改这个值</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">static</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">const</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">MAXN</span> = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">2001</span>;
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// C++ 中为了完全对应原代码逻辑，使用手动数组模拟队列</span>
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>* q_arr[<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">MAXN</span>];
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> l, r;

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 提交时把方法名改为levelOrder，此方法为每次处理一层的优化bfs，此题推荐</span>
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt;&gt; levelOrder2(<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>* root) {
        <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt;&gt; ans;
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (root != <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {
            l = r = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>;
            q_arr[r++] = root;
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">while</span> (l &lt; r) { <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 队列里还有东西</span>
                <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> size = r - l; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 当前层的节点个数</span>
                <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt; current_level;
                <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">for</span> (<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> i = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>; i &lt; size; i++) {
                    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>* cur = q_arr[l++];
                    current_level.push_back(cur-&gt;val);
                    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (cur-&gt;left != <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {
                        q_arr[r++] = cur-&gt;left;
                    }
                    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (cur-&gt;right != <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {
                        q_arr[r++] = cur-&gt;right;
                    }
                }
                ans.push_back(current_level);
            }
        }
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> ans;
    }
};

"<div style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(220, 220, 220); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(51, 51, 51); box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3) 0px 4px 6px; overflow-x: auto;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 036 二叉树的锯齿形层序遍历</span>
<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 1. 二叉树节点结构定义 (TreeNode Struct)</span>
<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 2. 锯齿形层序遍历实现 (使用手动数组模拟队列，通过双向索引控制收集顺序)</span>
锯齿就是从左往右，再从右往左
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">using</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 不提交这个类</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">struct</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span> {
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> val;
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span> *left;
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span> *right;
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> x) : val(x), left(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>), right(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {}
};

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">class</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">Code02_ZigzagLevelOrderTraversal</span> {
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 如果测试数据量变大了就修改这个值</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">static</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">const</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">MAXN</span> = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">2001</span>;
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 使用静态数组模拟队列，提高性能</span>
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>* q[<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">MAXN</span>];
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> l, r;

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 用每次处理一层的优化bfs就非常容易实现</span>
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt;&gt; zigzagLevelOrder(<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>* root) {
        <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt;&gt; ans;
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (root != <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {
            l = r = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>;
            q[r++] = root;
            <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// false 代表从左往右</span>
            <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// true 代表从右往左</span>
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">bool</span> reverse = <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">false</span>;
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">while</span> (l &lt; r) {
                <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> size = r - l;
                <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt; current_level;
                
                <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 根据 reverse 标志决定遍历方向</span>
                <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// reverse == false, 左 -&gt; 右， l....r-1, 收集size个</span>
                <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// reverse == true,  右 -&gt; 左， r-1....l, 收集size个</span>
                <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// i 为起始索引，j 为步长方向，k 为计数器</span>
                <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">for</span> (<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> i = reverse ? r - <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span> : l, j = reverse ? -<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span> : <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>, k = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>; k &lt; size; i += j, k++) {
                    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>* cur = q[i];
                    current_level.push_back(cur-&gt;val);
                }
                
                <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 正常的队列弹出逻辑，并放入下一层的孩子节点</span>
                <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">for</span> (<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> i = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>; i &lt; size; i++) {
                    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>* cur = q[l++];
                    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (cur-&gt;left != <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {
                        q[r++] = cur-&gt;left;
                    }
                    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (cur-&gt;right != <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {
                        q[r++] = cur-&gt;right;
                    }
                }
                
                ans.push_back(current_level);
                <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 每一层结束后反转方向</span>
                reverse = !reverse;
            }
        }
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> ans;
    }
};

            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 036 二叉树的最大宽度</span>
<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 1. 二叉树节点结构定义 (TreeNode Struct)</span>
<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 2. 最大宽度实现 (使用两个数组模拟队列，通过 ID 编号计算宽度)</span>

<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;algorithm&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">using</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 不提交这个类</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">struct</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span> {
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> val;
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span> *left;
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span> *right;
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> x) : val(x), left(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>), right(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {}
};

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">class</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">Code03_WidthOfBinaryTree1</span> {
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 如果测试数据量变大了就修改这个值</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">static</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">const</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">MAXN</span> = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">3001</span>;

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// nq 数组模拟存储节点的队列</span>
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>* nq[<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">MAXN</span>];

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// iq 数组模拟存储节点对应 ID 的队列</span>
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 使用 long long 对应 Java 的 long，防止编号在深度较大时溢出</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">long</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">long</span> iq[<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">MAXN</span>];

    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> l, r;

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 用每次处理一层的优化bfs就非常容易实现</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> widthOfBinaryTree(<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>* root) {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (root == <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>;
        }
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> ans = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>;
        l = r = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>;
        nq[r] = root;
        <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 初始节点编号为 1</span>
        iq[r++] = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>;
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">while</span> (l &lt; r) {
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> size = r - l;
            <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 每一层结算一次最大宽度</span>
            <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 当前层的宽度 = 右端点 ID - 左端点 ID + 1</span>
            ans = max(ans, (<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>)(iq[r - <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>] - iq[l] + <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>));
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">for</span> (<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> i = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>; i &lt; size; i++) {
                <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>* node = nq[l];
                <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">long</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">long</span> id = iq[l++];
                <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (node-&gt;left != <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {
                    nq[r] = node-&gt;left;
                    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 左孩子编号 = 父编号 * 2</span>
                    iq[r++] = id * <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">2</span>;
                }
                <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (node-&gt;right != <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {
                    nq[r] = node-&gt;right;
                    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 右孩子编号 = 父编号 * 2 + 1</span>
                    iq[r++] = id * <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">2</span> + <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>;
                }
            }
        }
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> ans;
    }
};
</pre>

"<div style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(220, 220, 220); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(51, 51, 51); box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3) 0px 4px 6px; overflow-x: auto;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 036 求二叉树的最大、最小深度</span>
<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 1. 二叉树节点结构定义 (TreeNode Struct)</span>
<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 2. 求二叉树的最大深度 (maxDepth)</span>
<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 3. 求二叉树的最小深度 (minDepth)</span>

<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;algorithm&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;climits&gt;</span>

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">using</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 不提交这个类</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">struct</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span> {
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> val;
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span> *left;
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span> *right;
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> x) : val(x), left(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>), right(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {}
};

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">class</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">Code04_DepthOfBinaryTree</span> {
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 测试链接 : https://leetcode.cn/problems/maximum-depth-of-binary-tree/</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> maxDepth(<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>* root) {
        <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 递归求解：左子树深度和右子树深度的最大值 + 1</span>
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> root == <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span> ? <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span> : max(maxDepth(root-&gt;left), maxDepth(root-&gt;right)) + <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>;
    }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 测试链接 : https://leetcode.cn/problems/minimum-depth-of-binary-tree/</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> minDepth(<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>* root) {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (root == <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {
            <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 当前的树是空树</span>
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>;
        }
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (root-&gt;left == <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span> &amp;&amp; root-&gt;right == <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {
            <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 当前root是叶节点</span>
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>;
        }
        
        <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 初始化深度为最大整数，方便后面取最小值</span>
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> ldeep = <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">INT_MAX</span>;
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> rdeep = <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">INT_MAX</span>;
        
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (root-&gt;left != <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {
            ldeep = minDepth(root-&gt;left);
        }
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (root-&gt;right != <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {
            rdeep = minDepth(root-&gt;right);
        }
        
        <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 最小深度是子树最小深度 + 1</span>
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> min(ldeep, rdeep) + <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>;
    }
};
</pre>
        </div>
        <br>"	
"<div style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(220, 220, 220); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(51, 51, 51); box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3) 0px 4px 6px; overflow-x: auto;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 036 二叉树先序序列化和反序列化</span>
<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 1. 二叉树节点结构定义 (TreeNode Struct)</span>
<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 2. 序列化逻辑实现 (serialize)</span>
<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 3. 反序列化逻辑实现 (deserialize)</span>

<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;string&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;sstream&gt;</span>

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">using</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 不提交这个类</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">struct</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span> {
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> val;
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span> *left;
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span> *right;
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> x) : val(x), left(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>), right(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {}
};

<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 二叉树可以通过先序、后序或者按层遍历的方式序列化和反序列化</span>
<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 但是，二叉树无法通过中序遍历的方式实现序列化和反序列化</span>
<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 因为不同的两棵树，可能得到同样的中序序列，即便补了空位置也可能一样。</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">class</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">Codec</span> {
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 2. 序列化逻辑实现</span>
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">string</span> serialize(<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>* root) {
        <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">string</span> res = <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""""</span>;
        f(root, res);
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> res;
    }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 先序遍历递归函数</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">void</span> f(<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>* root, <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">string</span>&amp; res) {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (root == <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {
            res += <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""#,""</span>;
        } <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">else</span> {
            res += to_string(root-&gt;val) + <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">"",""</span>;
            f(root-&gt;left, res);
            f(root-&gt;right, res);
        }
    }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 3. 反序列化逻辑实现</span>
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>* deserialize(<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">string</span> data) {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (data.empty()) <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>;
        
        <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 模拟 Java 的 split("","")</span>
        <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">string</span>&gt; vals;
        <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">stringstream</span> ss(data);
        <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">string</span> item;
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">while</span> (getline(ss, item, <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">','</span>)) {
            vals.push_back(item);
        }
        
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> cnt = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>; <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 当前数组消费到哪了</span>
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> g(vals, cnt);
    }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 递归重建二叉树</span>
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>* g(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">const</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">string</span>&gt;&amp; vals, <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&amp; cnt) {
        <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">string</span> cur = vals[cnt++];
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (cur == <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""#""</span>) {
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>;
        } <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">else</span> {
            <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// stoi 将字符串转换为整数，对应 Java 的 Integer.valueOf</span>
            <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>* head = <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">new</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>(stoi(cur));
            head-&gt;left = g(vals, cnt);
            head-&gt;right = g(vals, cnt);
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> head;
        }
    }
};
</pre>

"<div style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(220, 220, 220); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(51, 51, 51); box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3) 0px 4px 6px; overflow-x: auto;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 036 二叉树按层序列化和反序列化</span>
<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 1. 二叉树节点结构定义 (TreeNode Struct)</span>
<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 2. 按层序列化实现 (serialize)</span>
<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 3. 按层反序列化实现 (deserialize)</span>

<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;string&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;sstream&gt;</span>

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">using</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 不提交这个类</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">struct</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span> {
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> val;
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span> *left;
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span> *right;
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> x) : val(x), left(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>), right(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {}
};

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">class</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">Codec</span> {
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 如果测试数据量变大了就修改这个值</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">static</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">const</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">MAXN</span> = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">10001</span>;
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>* q[<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">MAXN</span>];
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> l, r;

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 按层序列化</span>
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">string</span> serialize(<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>* root) {
        <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">string</span> res = <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""""</span>;
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (root != <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {
            res += to_string(root-&gt;val) + <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">"",""</span>;</pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">c++的stirng可以直接添加字符
            l = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>;
            r = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>;
            q[r++] = root;
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">while</span> (l &lt; r) {
                root = q[l++];
                <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (root-&gt;left != <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {
                    res += to_string(root-&gt;left-&gt;val) + <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">"",""</span>;
                    q[r++] = root-&gt;left;</pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">把左右节点塞入节点数组
                } <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">else</span> {
                    res += <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""#,""</span>;
                }
                <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (root-&gt;right != <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {
                    res += to_string(root-&gt;right-&gt;val) + <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">"",""</span>;
                    q[r++] = root-&gt;right;
                } <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">else</span> {
                    res += <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""#,""</span>;
                }
            }
        }
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> res;
    }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 按层反序列化</span>
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>* deserialize(<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">string</span> data) {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (data == <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""""</span>) {
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>;
        }
        
        <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 模拟 Java 的 split("","")</span>
        <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">string</span>&gt; nodes;
        <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">stringstream</span> ss(data);
        <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">string</span> item;
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">while</span> (getline(ss, item, <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">','</span>)) {</pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">切割字符串！！！
            nodes.push_back(item);
        }

        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> index = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>;
        <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>* root = generate(nodes[index++]);
        l = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>;
        r = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>;
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (root != <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {
            q[r++] = root;
        }

        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">while</span> (l &lt; r) {
            <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>* cur = q[l++];
            cur-&gt;left = generate(nodes[index++]);</pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">写成函数判断空节点
            cur-&gt;right = generate(nodes[index++]);
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (cur-&gt;left != <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {
                q[r++] = cur-&gt;left;
            }
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (cur-&gt;right != <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {
                q[r++] = cur-&gt;right;
            }
        }
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> root;
    }

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">private</span>:
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 辅助方法：根据字符串生成节点</span>
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>* generate(<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">string</span> val) {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (val == <span style=""color: #D69D85;"">""#""</span>) {
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>;
        }
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">new</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>(stoi(val));
    }
};
</pre>

"<div style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(51, 51, 51); box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3) 0px 4px 6px; overflow-x: auto;"">
            <pre style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220); margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 036 利用先序与中序遍历序列构造二叉树</span>
<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 1. 二叉树节点结构定义 (TreeNode Struct)</span>
<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 2. 构造二叉树主函数 (buildTree)</span>
<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 3. 递归构造辅助函数 (f)</span>

<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;unordered_map&gt;</span>

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">using</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 不提交这个类</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">struct</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span> {
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> val;
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span> *left;
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span> *right;
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> x) : val(x), left(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>), right(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {}
};

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">class</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">Code07_PreorderInorderBuildBinaryTree</span> {
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 提交如下的方法</span>
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>* buildTree(<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt;&amp; pre, <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt;&amp; in) {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (pre.empty() || in.empty() || pre.size() != in.size()) {
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>;
        }
        <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 使用哈希表记录中序遍历中值与索引的对应关系，实现 O(1) 查找</span>
        <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">unordered_map</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>, <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt; posMap;
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">for</span> (<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> i = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>; i &lt; in.size(); i++) {
            posMap[in[i]] = i;
        }
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> f(pre, <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>, pre.size() - <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>, in, <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>, in.size() - <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>, posMap);
    }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 递归函数 f</span>
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// pre: 先序数组, l1...r1 是当前处理范围</span>
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// in: 中序数组, l2...r2 是当前处理范围</span>
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// map: 中序位置索引表</span>
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>* f(<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt;&amp; pre, <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> l1, <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> r1, <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt;&amp; in, <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> l2, <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> r2, <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">unordered_map</span>&lt;<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>, <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span>&gt;&amp; <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">map</span>) {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (l1 &gt; r1) {
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>;</pre><pre style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220); margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">见下方绿色注释
        }
        <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>* head = <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">new</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>(pre[l1]);
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (l1 == r1) {
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> head;
        }
        
        <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 找到当前根节点在中序遍历中的位置</span>
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> k = <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">map</span>[pre[l1]];
            
        <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// pre : l1(........)[.......r1]</span>
        <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// in  : (l2......)k[........r2]</span></pre><pre style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 220); margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #57A64A;"">左子树长度L= k-l2 </span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">k不在中序的左区间，是l2到k-1，再加上左子树（或者右子树）可能是空树，L = 0左子树 r1 = <font color=""#dcdcdc"">l1 + </font><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">1，l1 = l1+ L </span>所以l1可能会&gt;r1</pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">        <span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// (...) 是左子树对应范围，[...] 是右子树对应范围</span><font color=""#dcdcdc"">
        </font><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 左子树长度为 k - l2</span><font color=""#dcdcdc"">
        
        </font><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 递归构建左子树</span><font color=""#dcdcdc"">
        head-&gt;left = f(pre, l1 + </font><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">1</span><font color=""#dcdcdc"">, l1 + k - l2, in, l2, k - </font><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">1</span><font color=""#dcdcdc"">, </font><span style=""color: rgb(78, 201, 176);"">map</span><font color=""#dcdcdc"">);
        </font><span style=""color: rgb(87, 166, 74);"">// 递归构建右子树</span><font color=""#dcdcdc"">
        head-&gt;right = f(pre, l1 + k - l2 + </font><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">1</span><font color=""#dcdcdc"">, r1, in, k + </font><span style=""color: rgb(181, 206, 168);"">1</span><font color=""#dcdcdc"">, r2, </font><span style=""color: rgb(78, 201, 176);"">map</span><font color=""#dcdcdc"">);
        
        </font><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">return</span><font color=""#dcdcdc""> head;
    }
};
</font></pre>
        </div>
        <br>"	
"<div style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(220, 220, 220); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(51, 51, 51); box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3) 0px 4px 6px; overflow-x: auto;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 036 验证完全二叉树</span>
<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 1. 二叉树节点结构定义 (TreeNode Struct)</span>
<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 2. 验证完全二叉树实现 (使用 BFS 逻辑与叶节点阶段标记)</span>

<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">using</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 不提交这个类</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">struct</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span> {
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> val;
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span> *left;
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span> *right;
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> x) : val(x), left(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>), right(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {}
};

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">class</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">Code08_CompletenessOfBinaryTree</span> {
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 如果测试数据量变大了就修改这个值</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">static</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">const</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">MAXN</span> = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">101</span>;
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 使用数组模拟队列</span>
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>* q[<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">MAXN</span>];
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> l, r;

    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">bool</span> isCompleteTree(<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>* h) {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (h == <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">true</span>;
        }
        l = r = <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>;
        q[r++] = h;

        <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 是否遇到过左右两个孩子不双全的节点</span>
        <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 一旦遇到不双全的节点，后续所有节点都必须是叶子节点</span>
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">bool</span> leaf = <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">false</span>;

        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">while</span> (l &lt; r) {
            h = q[l++];

            <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 两个错误的任一情况出现都不是完全二叉树：</span>
            <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 1) 有右孩子但没左孩子</span>
            <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 2) 已经开启了叶节点阶段，</span>一旦遇到不双全的节点，后续所有节点都必须是叶子节点<span style=""color: #57A64A;""><br></span>
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> ((h-&gt;left == <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span> &amp;&amp; h-&gt;right != <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) || 
                (leaf &amp;&amp; (h-&gt;left != <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span> || h-&gt;right != <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>))) {
                <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">false</span>;
            }

            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (h-&gt;left != <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {
                q[r++] = h-&gt;left;
            }
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (h-&gt;right != <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {
                q[r++] = h-&gt;right;
            }

            <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 如果当前节点孩子不全（只有左没右，或者左右都没），开启叶节点阶段</span>
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (h-&gt;left == <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span> || h-&gt;right == <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {
                leaf = <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">true</span>;
            }
        }
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">true</span>;
    }
};
</pre>

        <br>"	
"<div style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(220, 220, 220); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(51, 51, 51); box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3) 0px 4px 6px; overflow-x: auto;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 036 求完全二叉树的节点个数</span>
<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 1. 二叉树节点结构定义 (TreeNode Struct)</span>
<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 2. 求完全二叉树节点个数主逻辑 (countNodes)</span>
<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 3. 递归分治求解 (f)</span>
<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 4. 求当前子树最左深度 (mostLeft)</span>

<span style=""color: #C586C0;"">#include </span><span style=""color: #D69D85;"">&lt;algorithm&gt;</span>

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">using</span> <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 不提交这个类</span>
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">struct</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span> {
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> val;
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span> *left;
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span> *right;
    <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> x) : val(x), left(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>), right(<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {}
};

<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">class</span> <span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">Code09_CountCompleteTreeNodes</span> {
<span style=""color: #569CD6;"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 提交如下的方法</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> countNodes(<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>* head) {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (head == <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">0</span>;
        }
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> f(head, <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>, mostLeft(head, <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>));
    }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// cur : 当前来到的节点</span>
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// level :  当前来到的节点在第几层</span>
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// h : 整棵树的高度，不是cur这棵子树的高度</span>
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 求 : cur这棵子树上有多少节点</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> f(<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>* cur, <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> level, <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> h) {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (level == h) {
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>;
        }
        <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 如果右子树的最左节点能达到整棵树的最大高度</span>
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">if</span> (mostLeft(cur-&gt;right, level + <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>) == h) {
            <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 说明左子树是满二叉树，高度为 h - level</span>
            <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 左子树节点数(含根) = 2^(h-level)，再加上递归处理右子树</span>
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> (<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span> &lt;&lt; (h - level)) + f(cur-&gt;right, level + <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>, h);
        } <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">else</span> {
            <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 说明右子树是满二叉树，高度为 h - level - 1</span>
            <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 右子树节点数(含根) = 2^(h-level-1)，再加上递归处理左子树</span>
            <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> (<span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span> &lt;&lt; (h - level - <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>)) + f(cur-&gt;left, level + <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>, h);
        }
    }

    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 当前节点是cur，并且它在level层</span>
    <span style=""color: #57A64A;"">// 返回从cur开始不停往左，能扎到几层</span>
    <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> mostLeft(<span style=""color: #4EC9B0;"">TreeNode</span>* cur, <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">int</span> level) {
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">while</span> (cur != <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">nullptr</span>) {
            level++;
            cur = cur-&gt;left;
        }
        <span style=""color: #569CD6;"">return</span> level - <span style=""color: #B5CEA8;"">1</span>;
    }
};
</pre>
        </div>

"<div><div><div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><div><div><div>一组数，分别表示地平线的高度变化。高度值为整数，相邻高度用直线连接。找出并统计有多少个可能积水的低洼地？</div><div>如图：地高变化为&nbsp;[0,1,0,2,1,2,0,0,2,0]。</div><div><img alt="""" src=""c1zyz8wu.png""></div></div></div><h2>输入格式</h2><div><div><div>两行，第一行&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>,&nbsp;表示有&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>&nbsp;个数。第&nbsp;2&nbsp;行连续&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>&nbsp;个数表示地平线高度变化的数据，保证首尾为&nbsp;0。(3≤<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>≤10000,0≤&nbsp;高度&nbsp;≤1000)。</div></div></div><h2>输出格式</h2><div><div><div>一个数，可能积水低洼地的数目。</div></div></div><h2>输入输出样例</h2><div><div><div><b>输入 #1</b>复制</div><pre>10
0 1 0 2 1 2 0 0 2 0
</pre></div><div><div><b>输出 #1</b>复制</div><pre>3</pre></div></div></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>(){
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n;
    cin&gt;&gt; n;


    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">h</span>(n);
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i =<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;i&lt;n;i++){
        cin&gt;&gt;h[i];
    
    }
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> count =<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">bool</span> falling=<span style=""color:#569CD6"">false</span>;

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i=<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;i&lt;n;i++){
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span>(h[i]&lt;h[i-<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>]){
            falling =<span style=""color:#569CD6"">true</span>;

        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span>(h[i]&gt;h[i-<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>]&amp;&amp;falling){
            count++;
            falling = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">false</span>;
            
        }
    }
    cout&lt;&lt;count&lt;&lt;endl;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><div><div><div>设某汉字由&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>×<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>&nbsp;的&nbsp;0&nbsp;和&nbsp;1&nbsp;的点阵图案组成。</div><div>我们依照以下规则生成压缩码。连续一组数值：从汉字点阵图案的第一行第一个符号开始计算，按书写顺序从左到右，由上至下。第一个数表示连续有几个&nbsp;0，第二个数表示接下来连续有几个&nbsp;1，第三个数再接下来连续有几个&nbsp;0，第四个数接着连续几个&nbsp;1，以此类推……</div><div>例如: 以下汉字点阵图案：</div><div><pre><code>0001000
0001000
0001111
0001000
0001000
0001000
1111111
</code></pre></div><div>对应的压缩码是：&nbsp;7&nbsp;3&nbsp;1&nbsp;6&nbsp;1&nbsp;6&nbsp;4&nbsp;3&nbsp;1&nbsp;6&nbsp;1&nbsp;6&nbsp;1&nbsp;3&nbsp;7&nbsp;（第一个数是&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>&nbsp;,其余各位表示交替表示0和1 的个数，压缩码保证&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>×<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>=&nbsp;交替的各位数之和）</div></div></div><h2>输入格式</h2><div><div><div>数据输入一行，由空格隔开的若干个整数，表示压缩码。</div><div>其中，压缩码的第一个数字就是&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>，表示这个点阵应当是&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>×<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>&nbsp;的大小。</div><div>接下来的若干个数字，含义如题目描述所述。</div></div></div><h2>输出格式</h2><div><div><div>输出一个&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>×<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>&nbsp;的 01 矩阵，表示最后的汉字点阵图（点阵符号之间不留空格）。</div></div></div><h2>输入输出样例</h2><div><div><div><b>输入 #1</b>复制运行</div><pre>7 3 1 6 1 6 4 3 1 6 1 6 1 3 7</pre></div><div><div><b>输出 #1</b>复制运行</div><pre>0001000
0001000
0001111
0001000
0001000
0001000
1111111</pre></div></div></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>(){
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n;

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span>(!(cin&gt;&gt;n)) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;

    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> count;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> printed_in_line= <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> current_val= <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span>(cin&gt;&gt;count){
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;i&lt;count;++i){
            cout&lt;&lt; current_val;
            printed_in_line++;
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span>(printed_in_line == n){
                cout&lt;&lt;endl;
                printed_in_line=<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
                
            }
        }
        current_val^=<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
        
    }
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    
}</pre>

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><div><div><div>设某汉字由&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>×<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>&nbsp;的&nbsp;0&nbsp;和&nbsp;1&nbsp;的点阵图案组成。</div><div>我们依照以下规则生成压缩码。连续一组数值：从汉字点阵图案的第一行第一个符号开始计算，按书写顺序从左到右，由上至下。第一个数表示连续有几个&nbsp;0，第二个数表示接下来连续有几个&nbsp;1，第三个数再接下来连续有几个&nbsp;0，第四个数接着连续几个&nbsp;1，以此类推……</div><div>例如: 以下汉字点阵图案：</div><div><pre><code>0001000
0001000
0001111
0001000
0001000
0001000
1111111
</code></pre></div><div>对应的压缩码是：&nbsp;7&nbsp;3&nbsp;1&nbsp;6&nbsp;1&nbsp;6&nbsp;4&nbsp;3&nbsp;1&nbsp;6&nbsp;1&nbsp;6&nbsp;1&nbsp;3&nbsp;7&nbsp;（第一个数是&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>，其余各位表示交替表示&nbsp;0&nbsp;和&nbsp;1&nbsp;的个数，压缩码保证&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>×<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>=&nbsp;交替的各位数之和）</div></div></div><h2>输入格式</h2><div><div><div>汉字点阵图（点阵符号之间不留空格）。</div></div></div><h2>输出格式</h2><div><div><div>输出一行，压缩码。</div></div></div><h2>输入输出样例</h2><div><div><div><b>输入 #1</b>复制</div><pre>0001000
0001000
0001111
0001000
0001000
0001000
1111111
</pre></div><div><div><b>输出 #1</b>复制</div><pre>7 3 1 6 1 6 4 3 1 6 1 6 1 3 7</pre></div></div></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;string&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 优化 I/O 速度</span>
    ios_base::<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">sync_with_stdio</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">false</span>);
    cin.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">tie</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">NULL</span>);

    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> line;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> total_bits = <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""""</span>;
    
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 读取第一行，确定 N 的大小</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (cin &gt;&gt; line) {
        total_bits += line;
    }
    
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n = line.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">length</span>();
    
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 读取剩余的 N-1 行</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &lt; n; ++i) {
        cin &gt;&gt; line;
        total_bits += line;
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 输出 N</span>
    cout &lt;&lt; n &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#CE9178"">"" ""</span>;

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 4. 扫描统计</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 题目要求第一个输出的是 '0' 的个数，所以我们假设当前正在统计 '0'</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">char</span> current_target = <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'0'</span>;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> count = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">char</span> c : total_bits) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (c == current_target) {
            count++;
        } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 遇到不同的字符，输出当前统计结果，并切换目标</span>
            cout &lt;&lt; count &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#CE9178"">"" ""</span>;
            count = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 新的一段已经有一个字符了（即当前字符 c）</span>
            
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 切换目标字符：如果是 '0' 变 '1'，是 '1' 变 '0'</span>
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (current_target == <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'0'</span>) {
                current_target = <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'1'</span>;
            } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
                current_target = <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'0'</span>;</pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><img src=""paste-ef24f5b26a9f2b03cb7035e12822db0505d0d557.jpg"">这里可以用异或写，挺巧的
            }
        }
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 5. 输出最后一段的计数</span>
    cout &lt;&lt; count &lt;&lt; endl;

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><div><div><div>我有一个长度为&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">l</span>&nbsp;的字符串，最开始时，这个字符串由&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">l</span>&nbsp;个句号（<code>.</code>）组成。</div><div>我在这个字符串中，将多次把&nbsp;<code>boy</code>&nbsp;或者&nbsp;<code>girl</code>&nbsp;两单词，依次贴到这个字符串中。</div><div>后贴上单词，会覆盖之前贴上的单词，或者覆盖句号。最终，每个单词至少有一个字符没有被覆盖。</div><div>请问，一共贴有几个&nbsp;<code>boy</code>&nbsp;几个&nbsp;<code>girl</code>？</div></div></div><h2>输入格式</h2><div><div><div>一行被反复贴有&nbsp;<code>boy</code>&nbsp;和&nbsp;<code>girl</code>&nbsp;两单词的字符串。</div></div></div><h2>输出格式</h2><div><div><div>两行，两个整数。第一行为&nbsp;<code>boy</code>&nbsp;的个数，第二行为&nbsp;<code>girl</code>&nbsp;的个数。</div></div></div><h2>输入输出样例</h2><div><div><div><b>输入 #1</b>复制</div><pre>......boyogirlyy......girl.......
</pre></div><div><div><b>输出 #1</b>复制</div><pre>4
2
</pre></div></div><h2>说明/提示</h2><div><div><div>数据保证，3≤<span style=""font-style: italic;"">l</span>≤255，字符串仅仅包含如下字符：.bgilory。</div></div></div></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;string&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 基础设置</span>
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> s;
    cin &gt;&gt; s;
    
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> cnt_boy = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> cnt_girl = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> len = s.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">length</span>(); <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 获取字符串长度，转为 int 防止无符号整数溢出</span>

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 统计 boy 的个数</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 我们遍历所有可能的 boy 起始位置。</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// boy 长度为 3，所以起始位置 i 最大只能到 len-3</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; i &lt;= len - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">3</span>; i++) {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 只要 b, o, y 中任意一个字符出现在了它应该出现的位置</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 就说明这里贴过一个 boy</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (s[i] == <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'b'</span> || s[i+<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>] == <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'o'</span> || s[i+<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>] == <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'y'</span>) {
            cnt_boy++;
        }
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 统计 girl 的个数</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// girl 长度为 4，起始位置 i 最大只能到 len-4</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; i &lt;= len - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">4</span>; i++) {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 同理，只要 g, i, r, l 中任意一个字符对应上了</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 就说明这里贴过一个 girl</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (s[i] == <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'g'</span> || s[i+<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>] == <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'i'</span> || s[i+<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>] == <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'r'</span> || s[i+<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">3</span>] == <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'l'</span>) {
            cnt_girl++;
        }
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 输出结果</span>

    cout &lt;&lt; cnt_girl &lt;&lt; endl;

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}
