"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">package class037;

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 普通二叉树上寻找两个节点的最近公共祖先</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 测试链接 : https://leetcode.cn/problems/lowest-common-ancestor-of-a-binary-tree/</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">public</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">class</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Code01_LowestCommonAncestor</span> {

	<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 不提交这个类</span>
	<span style=""color:#569CD6"">public</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">static</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">class</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span> {
		<span style=""color:#569CD6"">public</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> val;
		<span style=""color:#569CD6"">public</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span> left;
		<span style=""color:#569CD6"">public</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span> right;
	}

	<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 提交如下的方法</span>
	<span style=""color:#569CD6"">public</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">static</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">lowestCommonAncestor</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span> root, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span> p, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span> q) {
		<span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (root == null || root == p || root == q) {
			<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 遇到空，或者p，或者q，直接返回</span>
			<span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> root;
		}
		<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span> l = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">lowestCommonAncestor</span>(root.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">left</span>, p, q);
		<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span> r = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">lowestCommonAncestor</span>(root.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">right</span>, p, q);
		<span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (l != null &amp;&amp; r != null) {
			<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 左树也搜到，右树也搜到，返回root</span>
			<span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> root;
		}
		<span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (l == null &amp;&amp; r == null) {
			<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 都没搜到返回空</span>
			<span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> null;
		}
		<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// l和r一个为空，一个不为空</span>
		<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 返回不空的那个</span>
		<span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> l != null ? l : r;
	}

}

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 037 搜索二叉树上寻找两个节点的最近公共祖先</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 二叉树节点结构定义 (TreeNode Struct)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 搜索二叉树最近公共祖先实现 (lowestCommonAncestor)</span>

<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;algorithm&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 不提交这个类</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">struct</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span> {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> val;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span> *left;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span> *right;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> x) : <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">val</span>(x), <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">left</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>), <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">right</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>) {}
};

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">class</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Code02_LowestCommonAncestorBinarySearch</span> {
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 提交如下的方法</span>
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span>* <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">lowestCommonAncestor</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span>* root, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span>* p, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span>* q) {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// root从上到下</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 如果先遇到了p，说明p是答案</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 如果先遇到了q，说明q是答案</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 如果root在p~q的值之间，不用管p和q谁大谁小，只要root在中间，那么此时的root就是答案</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 如果root在p~q的值的左侧，那么root往右移动</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 如果root在p~q的值的右侧，那么root往左移动</span>
        
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 在 C++ 中使用 std::min 和 std::max</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (root-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">val</span> != p-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">val</span> &amp;&amp; root-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">val</span> != q-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">val</span>) {</pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">这里如果root等于p，直接就返回root了
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> minVal = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">min</span>(p-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">val</span>, q-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">val</span>);
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> maxVal = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">max</span>(p-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">val</span>, q-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">val</span>);</pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">判断走左还是走右，为什么大小值可以判断呢。因为如果root值比两个都小，那么一定是走右边（大的值
            
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (minVal &lt; root-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">val</span> &amp;&amp; root-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">val</span> &lt; maxVal) {
                <span style=""color:#C586C0"">break</span>;
            }
            
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 利用搜索二叉树性质进行路径选择</span>
            root = root-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">val</span> &lt; minVal ? root-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">right</span> : root-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">left</span>;</pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">        }
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> root;
    }
};

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 037 收集累加和等于aim的所有路径</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 二叉树节点结构定义 (TreeNode Struct)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 路径总和主函数 (pathSum)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 深度优先搜索与回溯逻辑 (f)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 4. 路径拷贝辅助函数 (copy)</span>

<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 不提交这个类</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">struct</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span> {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> val;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span> *left;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span> *right;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> x) : <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">val</span>(x), <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">left</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>), <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">right</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>) {}
};

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">class</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Code03_PathSumII</span> {
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 提交如下的方法</span>
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">pathSum</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span>* root, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> aim) {
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&gt; ans;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (root != <span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>) {
            <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; path;
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f</span>(root, aim, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, path, ans);
        }
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> ans;
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 递归函数 f</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// cur: 当前节点</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// aim: 目标累加和</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// sum: 到达当前节点上方的累加和</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// path: 当前路径轨迹</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// ans: 收集结果的容器</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span>* cur, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> aim, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> sum, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&amp; path, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&gt;&amp; ans) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">left</span> == <span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span> &amp;&amp; cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">right</span> == <span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>) {
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 叶节点</span>
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">val</span> + sum == aim) {
                path.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">push_back</span>(cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">val</span>);
                <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">copy</span>(path, ans);
                <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 回溯：移除当前添加的叶子节点值</span>
                path.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">pop_back</span>();
            }
        } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 不是叶节点</span>
            path.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">push_back</span>(cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">val</span>);
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">left</span> != <span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>) {
                <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f</span>(cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">left</span>, aim, sum + cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">val</span>, path, ans);
            }
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">right</span> != <span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>) {
                <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f</span>(cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">right</span>, n-aim, sum + cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">val</span>, path, ans);
            }
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 回溯：在返回父节点之前，清理当前路径</span>
            path.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">pop_back</span>();
        }
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 路径拷贝逻辑</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 将当前满足条件的路径深度拷贝并存入答案</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">copy</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&amp; path, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&gt;&amp; ans) {
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; cp;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> num : path) {
            cp.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">push_back</span>(num);
        }
        ans.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">push_back</span>(cp);
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 注意：在 C++ 中，ans.push_back(path) 本身就会触发拷贝构造</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 这里为了完全对应 Java 原代码的手动拷贝逻辑进行编写</span>
    }
};
</pre>
        </div>

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 037 验证平衡二叉树</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 二叉树节点结构定义 (TreeNode Struct)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 验证平衡二叉树主逻辑 (isBalanced)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 递归高度计算与平衡性判定 (height)</span>

<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;algorithm&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;cmath&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 不提交这个类</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">struct</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span> {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> val;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span> *left;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span> *right;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> x) : <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">val</span>(x), <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">left</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>), <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">right</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>) {}
};

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">class</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Code04_BalancedBinaryTree</span> {
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 提交如下的方法</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// balance 是成员变量，对应 Java 中的全局/静态变量逻辑</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">bool</span> balance;

    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">bool</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">isBalanced</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span>* root) {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// balance 是成员变量，所有递归调用过程共享</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 每次判断开始时，设置为 true</span>
        balance = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">true</span>;
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">height</span>(root);
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> balance;
    }

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">private</span>:
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 一旦发现不平衡，返回什么高度已经不重要了</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">height</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span>* cur) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (!balance || cur == <span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>) {
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
        }
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> lh = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">height</span>(cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">left</span>);
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> rh = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">height</span>(cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">right</span>);
        
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 判断当前节点是否平衡：左右子树高度差绝对值不超过 1</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">abs</span>(lh - rh) &gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>) {
            balance = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">false</span>;
        }
        
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 返回当前子树的高度</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">max</span>(lh, rh) + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
    }
};

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 037 验证搜索二叉树</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 二叉树节点结构定义 (TreeNode Struct)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 基于中序遍历的迭代验证 (isValidBST1)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 基于递归采集范围信息的验证 (isValidBST2)</span>

<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;algorithm&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;climits&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 不提交这个类</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">struct</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span> {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> val;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span> *left;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span> *right;

};

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">class</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Code05_ValidateBinarySearchTree</span> {
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 基于中序遍历的迭代实现</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 搜索二叉树的中序遍历结果必须是严格升序的</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">static</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span> = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">10001</span>;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span>* <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">stack</span>[<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span>];
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> r;

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 提交时改名为isValidBST</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">bool</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">isValidBST1</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span>* head) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (head == <span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>) {
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">true</span>;
        }
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span>* pre = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>;
        r = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (r &gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span> || head != <span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>) {
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (head != <span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>) {
                <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">stack</span>[r++] = head;
                head = head-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">left</span>;
            } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
                head = <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">stack</span>[--r];
                <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 当前节点值必须大于前驱节点值</span>
                <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (pre != <span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span> &amp;&amp; pre-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">val</span> &gt;= head-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">val</span>) {
                    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">false</span>;
                }
                pre = head;
                head = head-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">right</span>;
            }
        }
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">true</span>;
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 基于递归采集信息的实现</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 使用 long long 防止节点值为 int 的极值时判断溢出</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> min_val, max_val;

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 提交时改名为isValidBST</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">bool</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">isValidBST2</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span>* head) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (head == <span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>) {
            min_val = <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">LLONG_MAX</span>;
            max_val = <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">LLONG_MIN</span>;
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">true</span>;
        }
        
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 递归左树</span>
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">bool</span> lok = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">isValidBST2</span>(head-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">left</span>);
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> lmin = min_val;
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> lmax = max_val;
        
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 递归右树</span>
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">bool</span> rok = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">isValidBST2</span>(head-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">right</span>);
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> rmin = min_val;
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> rmax = max_val;
        
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 更新当前子树的最小值和最大值</span>
        min_val = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">min</span>({(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span>)head-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">val</span>, lmin, rmin});
        max_val = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">max</span>({(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span>)head-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">val</span>, lmax, rmax});
        
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 验证：左树合法 &amp;&amp; 右树合法 &amp;&amp; 左树最大值 &lt; 头 &amp;&amp; 头 &lt; 右树最小值</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> lok &amp;&amp; rok &amp;&amp; lmax &lt; head-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">val</span> &amp;&amp; head-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">val</span> &lt; rmin;
    }
};
</pre>

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 037 修剪搜索二叉树</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 二叉树节点结构定义 (TreeNode Struct)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 修剪搜索二叉树递归实现 (trimBST)</span>

<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;cstddef&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 不提交这个类</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">struct</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span> {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> val;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span> *left;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span> *right;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> x) : <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">val</span>(x), <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">left</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>), <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">right</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>) {}
};

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">class</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Code06_TrimBinarySearchTree</span> {
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 提交以下的方法</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 修剪范围 [low, high]</span>
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span>* <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">trimBST</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span>* cur, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> low, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> high) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (cur == <span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>) {
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>;
        }
        
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 如果当前节点的值小于最小值，说明该节点及其左子树都不在范围内</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 直接返回其右子树修剪后的结果</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">val</span> &lt; low) {
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">trimBST</span>(cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">right</span>, low, high);
        }
        
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 如果当前节点的值大于最大值，说明该节点及其右子树都不在范围内</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 直接返回其左子树修剪后的结果</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">val</span> &gt; high) {
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">trimBST</span>(cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">left</span>, low, high);
        }
        
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 当前节点值在范围内，保留该节点</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 递归地修剪其左右子树，并将返回的新子树连接到当前节点上</span>
        cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">left</span> = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">trimBST</span>(cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">left</span>, low, high);
        cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">right</span> = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">trimBST</span>(cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">right</span>, low, high);
        
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> cur;
    }
};

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 037 二叉树打家劫舍问题</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 二叉树节点结构定义 (TreeNode Struct)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 核心递归函数 (f) - 计算偷与不偷当前节点的最大收益</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 打家劫舍主逻辑 (rob)</span>

<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;algorithm&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 不提交这个类</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">struct</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span> {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> val;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span> *left;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span> *right;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> x) : <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">val</span>(x), <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">left</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>), <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">right</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>) {}
};

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">class</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Code07_HouseRobberIII</span> {
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 提交如下的方法</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">rob</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span>* root) {
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f</span>(root);
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">max</span>(yes, no);
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// yes 变成，X子树在偷头节点的情况下，最大的收益</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// C++ 中使用成员变量来对应 Java 的静态/全局变量</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> yes;

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// no 变成，X子树在不偷头节点的情况下，最大的收益</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> no;

    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">TreeNode</span>* root) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (root == <span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>) {
            yes = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
            no = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
        } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// y 记录当前节点偷的情况下的收益，初值为当前节点的钱</span>
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> y = root-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">val</span>;
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// n 记录当前节点不偷的情况下的收益，初值为 0</span>
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
            
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 处理左子树</span>
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f</span>(root-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">left</span>);
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 如果偷当前节点，那么左子树只能选“不偷”的结果</span>
            y += no;
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 如果不偷当前节点，那么左子树可以选“偷”或“不偷”中较大的那个</span>
            n += <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">max</span>(yes, no);
            
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 处理右子树</span>
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f</span>(root-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">right</span>);
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 如果偷当前节点，那么右子树只能选“不偷”的结果</span>
            y += no;
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 如果不偷当前节点，那么右子树可以选“偷”或“不偷”中较大的那个</span>
            n += <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">max</span>(yes, no);
            
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 将当前子树的结果写回“全局”变量，供父节点使用</span>
            yes = y;
            no = n;
        }
    }
};
</pre>
        </div>
        <br>"	
"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><div><div><div>有一次，小鱼要从 A 处沿直线往右边游，小鱼第一秒可以游&nbsp;7&nbsp;米，从第二秒开始每秒游的距离只有前一秒的&nbsp;98%。有个极其邪恶的猎人在距离 A 处右边&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">s</span>&nbsp;米的地方，安装了一个隐蔽的探测器，探测器左右&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">x</span>&nbsp;米之内是探测范围。一旦小鱼进入探测器的范围，探测器就会在这一秒结束时把信号传递给那个猎人，猎人在一秒后就要对探测器范围内的水域进行抓捕，这时如果小鱼还在这范围内就危险了。也就是说小鱼一旦进入探测器范围，如果能在下&nbsp;1&nbsp;秒的时间内马上游出探测器的范围，还是安全的。现在给出&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">s</span>&nbsp;和&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">x</span>&nbsp;的数据，请你判断小鱼会不会有危险？如果有危险输出&nbsp;<code>y</code>，没有危险输出&nbsp;<code>n</code>。</div></div></div><h2>输入格式</h2><div><div><div>一行内输入两个实数，用空格分隔，表示&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">s</span>&nbsp;和&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">x</span>。</div></div></div><h2>输出格式</h2><div><div><div>一行内输出&nbsp;<code>y</code>&nbsp;或者&nbsp;<code>n</code>&nbsp;表示小鱼是否会有危险。</div></div></div><h2>输入输出样例</h2><div><div><div><b>输入 #1</b>复制运行</div><pre>14 1</pre></div><div><div><b>输出 #1</b>复制运行</div><pre>n</pre></div></div></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0""><br></span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">double</span> s, x;
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 读取实数 s 和 x</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (!(cin &gt;&gt; s &gt;&gt; x)) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;

    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">double</span> current_pos = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 小鱼当前的总路程</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">double</span> step = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">7</span>;        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 当前这一秒能游的距离</span>

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 让小鱼一直游，直到进入探测范围的左边 (s - x)</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (current_pos &lt; s - x) {
        current_pos = current_pos + step;
        step = step * <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>.<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">98</span>;
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 此时小鱼已经进入了范围。</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 我们要看再过一秒（即猎人抓捕时），小鱼的位置是否还在 (s + x) 以内。</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 这里的 step 已经是进入范围后的那一秒的速度了。</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (current_pos + step &lt;= s + x) {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 如果位置还在右边界内，输出 y</span>
        cout &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""y""</span> &lt;&lt; endl;
    } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 如果已经游出了右边界，输出 n</span>
        cout &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""n""</span> &lt;&lt; endl;
    }

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}

            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><div><div><div>小鱼最近被要求参加一个数字游戏，要求它把看到的一串数字&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">a</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>​（长度不一定，以&nbsp;0&nbsp;结束），记住了然后反着念出来（表示结束的数字&nbsp;0&nbsp;就不要念出来了）。这对小鱼的那点记忆力来说实在是太难了，你也不想想小鱼的整个脑袋才多大，其中一部分还是好吃的肉！所以请你帮小鱼编程解决这个问题。</div></div></div><h2>输入格式</h2><div><div><div>一行内输入一串整数，以&nbsp;0&nbsp;结束，以空格间隔。</div></div></div><h2>输出格式</h2><div><div><div>一行内倒着输出这一串整数，以空格间隔。</div></div></div><h2>输入输出样例</h2><div><div><div><b>输入 #1</b>复制运行</div><pre>3 65 23 5 34 1 30 0</pre></div><div><div><b>输出 #1</b>复制运行</div><pre>30 1 34 5 23 65 3</pre></div></div></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> num;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; a; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 创建一个动态数组来存储数字</span>

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 持续读入数字，直到读到 0</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (cin &gt;&gt; num &amp;&amp; num != <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>) {
        a.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">push_back</span>(num); <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 把数字放到数组末尾</span>
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 从数组的最后一个元素开始往前遍历</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// a.size() 获取数组长度</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = a.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>() - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &gt;= <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; i--) {
        cout &lt;&lt; a[i];
        
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 如果不是最后一个输出的数字，就补一个空格</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (i &gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>) {
            cout &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#CE9178"">"" ""</span>;
        }
    }

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><div><div><div>现代数学的著名证明之一是 Georg Cantor 证明了有理数是可枚举的。他是用下面这一张表来证明这一命题的：</div>1/12/13/14/15/1​1/22/23/24/2⋯​1/32/33/3⋯​1/42/4⋯​1/5⋯⋯<div>这次与 NOIp1999 第一题不同的是：这次需输入两个分数（不一定是最简分数），算出这两个分数的积（注意需要约分至最简分数），输出积在原表的第几列第几行（若积形如&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">a</span>（即结果为整数）或者&nbsp;1/<span style=""font-style: italic;"">a</span>，则看作表内的&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">a</span>/1&nbsp;或&nbsp;1/<span style=""font-style: italic;"">a</span>&nbsp;结算）。</div></div></div><h2>输入格式</h2><div><div><div>共两行。每行输入一个分数（不一定是最简分数）。</div></div></div><h2>输出格式</h2><div><div><div>两个整数，表示输入的两个分数的积在表中的第几列第几行。</div></div></div></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;algorithm&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>(){
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> a1,a2,b1,b2;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">char</span> spc;
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">scanf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""%d""</span>,&amp;a1); spc  = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">getchar</span>(); <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">scanf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""%d""</span>,&amp;b1);
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">scanf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""%d""</span>,&amp;a2); spc  = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">getchar</span>(); <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">scanf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""%d""</span>,&amp;b2);
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> c1 = a1 * a2,c2 = b2* b1;

    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""%d %d\n""</span>,c2 / <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">__gcd</span>(c1,c2),c1 / <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">__gcd</span>(c1,c2));
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><div><div><div>现有&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>&nbsp;名同学参加了期末考试，并且获得了每名同学的信息：语文、数学、英语成绩（均为不超过&nbsp;150&nbsp;的自然数）。如果某对学生&nbsp;⟨<span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">j</span>⟩&nbsp;的每一科成绩的分差都不大于&nbsp;5，且总分分差不大于&nbsp;10，那么这对学生就是“旗鼓相当的对手”。现在想知道这些同学中，有几对“旗鼓相当的对手”？同样一个人可能会和其他好几名同学结对。</div></div></div><h2>输入格式</h2><div><div><div>第一行一个正整数&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>。</div><div>接下来&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>&nbsp;行，每行三个整数，其中第&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>&nbsp;行表示第&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>&nbsp;名同学的语文、数学、英语成绩。最先读入的同学编号为&nbsp;1。</div></div></div><h2>输出格式</h2><div><div><div>输出一个整数，表示“旗鼓相当的对手”的对数。</div></div></div><h2>输入输出样例</h2><div><div><div><b>输入 #1</b>复制</div><pre>3
90 90 90
85 95 90
80 100 91</pre></div><div><div><b>输出 #1</b>复制</div><pre>2</pre></div></div></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;cmath&gt;</span> <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 用于 abs() 函数取绝对值</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 定义学生结构体</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">struct</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Student</span> {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> chinese;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> math;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> english;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> total;
};

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (!(cin &gt;&gt; n)) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;

    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Student</span>&gt; <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">stu</span>(n);
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 读入所有学生信息</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; i &lt; n; i++) {
        cin &gt;&gt; stu[i].<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">chinese</span> &gt;&gt; stu[i].<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">math</span> &gt;&gt; stu[i].<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">english</span>;
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 计算总分</span>
        stu[i].<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">total</span> = stu[i].<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">chinese</span> + stu[i].<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">math</span> + stu[i].<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">english</span>;
    }

    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> count = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 两两比较 (i 和 j)</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; i &lt; n; i++) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> j = i + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; j &lt; n; j++) {
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 判定条件1：单科分差 &lt;= 5</span>
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">bool</span> c1 = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">abs</span>(stu[i].<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">chinese</span> - stu[j].<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">chinese</span>) &lt;= <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">5</span>;
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">bool</span> c2 = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">abs</span>(stu[i].<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">math</span> - stu[j].<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">math</span>) &lt;= <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">5</span>;
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">bool</span> c3 = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">abs</span>(stu[i].<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">english</span> - stu[j].<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">english</span>) &lt;= <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">5</span>;
            
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 判定条件2：总分分差 &lt;= 10</span>
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">bool</span> c4 = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">abs</span>(stu[i].<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">total</span> - stu[j].<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">total</span>) &lt;= <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">10</span>;

            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 如果全部满足，则是旗鼓相当的对手</span>
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (c1 &amp;&amp; c2 &amp;&amp; c3 &amp;&amp; c4) {
                count++;
            }
        }
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 输出结果</span>
    cout &lt;&lt; count &lt;&lt; endl;

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}
</pre>

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><div><div><div>现有一个长宽高分别为&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">w</span>,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">x</span>,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">h</span>&nbsp;组成的实心玻璃立方体，可以认为是由&nbsp;1×1×1&nbsp;的数个小方块组成的，每个小方块都有一个坐标&nbsp;(<span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">j</span>,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">k</span>)。现在需要进行&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">q</span>&nbsp;次切割。每次切割给出&nbsp;(<span style=""font-style: italic;"">x</span>1​,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">y</span>1​,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">z</span>1​),(<span style=""font-style: italic;"">x</span>2​,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">y</span>2​,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">z</span>2​)&nbsp;这 6 个参数，保证&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">x</span>1​≤<span style=""font-style: italic;"">x</span>2​，<span style=""font-style: italic;"">y</span>1​≤<span style=""font-style: italic;"">y</span>2​，<span style=""font-style: italic;"">z</span>1​≤<span style=""font-style: italic;"">z</span>2​；每次切割时，使用激光工具切出一个立方体空洞，空洞的壁平行于立方体的面，空洞的对角点就是给出的切割参数的两个点。</div><div>换句话说，所有满足&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">x</span>1​≤<span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>≤<span style=""font-style: italic;"">x</span>2​，<span style=""font-style: italic;"">y</span>1​≤<span style=""font-style: italic;"">j</span>≤<span style=""font-style: italic;"">y</span>2​，<span style=""font-style: italic;"">z</span>1​≤<span style=""font-style: italic;"">k</span>≤<span style=""font-style: italic;"">z</span>2​&nbsp;的小方块&nbsp;(<span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">j</span>,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">k</span>)&nbsp;的点都会被激光蒸发。例如有一个&nbsp;4×4×4&nbsp;的大方块，其体积为&nbsp;64；给出参数&nbsp;(1,1,1),(2,2,2)&nbsp;时，中间的&nbsp;8&nbsp;块小方块就会被蒸发，剩下&nbsp;56&nbsp;个小方块。现在想知道经过所有切割操作后，剩下的工艺品还剩下多少格小方块的体积？</div></div></div><h2>输入格式</h2><div><div><div>第一行三个正整数&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">w</span>,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">x</span>,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">h</span>。</div><div>第二行一个正整数&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">q</span>。</div><div>接下来&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">q</span>&nbsp;行，每行六个整数&nbsp;(<span style=""font-style: italic;"">x</span>1​,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">y</span>1​,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">z</span>1​),(<span style=""font-style: italic;"">x</span>2​,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">y</span>2​,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">z</span>2​)。</div></div></div><h2>输出格式</h2><div><div><div>输出一个整数表示答案。</div></div></div><h2>输入输出样例</h2><div><div><div><b>输入 #1</b>复制运行</div><pre>4 4 4
1
1 1 1 2 2 2
</pre></div><div><div><b>输出 #1</b>复制运行</div><pre>56</pre></div></div></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 数组稍微开大一点，比如 25，防止越界</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// box[x][y][z] 如果是 0 表示方块在，1 表示被挖走</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> box[<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">25</span>][<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">25</span>][<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">25</span>];

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> w, x, h, q;
    
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 读取大盒子的长宽高</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (!(cin &gt;&gt; w &gt;&gt; x &gt;&gt; h)) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 读取要挖几次洞</span>
    cin &gt;&gt; q;
    
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 循环 q 次，每次处理一个激光切割</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (q &gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>) {
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> x1, y1, z1, x2, y2, z2;
        cin &gt;&gt; x1 &gt;&gt; y1 &gt;&gt; z1 &gt;&gt; x2 &gt;&gt; y2 &gt;&gt; z2;
        
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 激光范围：从 x1 到 x2，从 y1 到 y2，从 z1 到 z2</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = x1; i &lt;= x2; i++) {
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> j = y1; j &lt;= y2; j++) {
                <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> k = z1; k &lt;= z2; k++) {
                    box[i][j][k] = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 标记为 1，代表被蒸发了</span>
                }
            }
        }
        q = q - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 处理完一次，次数减 1</span>
    }
    
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 最后统计还剩下多少个 0</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> count = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &lt;= w; i++) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> j = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; j &lt;= x; j++) {
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> k = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; k &lt;= h; k++) {
                <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (box[i][j][k] == <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>) {
                    count = count + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
                }
            }
        }
    }
    
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 输出结果</span>
    cout &lt;&lt; count &lt;&lt; endl;
    
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}
</pre>

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><img src=""paste-f2b3f0cc2b0dec9c7bb6a5fe74dcab4521534d0c.jpg""><span style=""color:#C586C0""><br></span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n,m;cin&gt;&gt;n&gt;&gt;m;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MOD</span> = 1e9 +<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">7</span>;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span>&gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">dp</span>(n +<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>,<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span>&gt;(m+<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>,<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>));
    
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i=<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;i&lt;=n;++i){
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> j=<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;j&lt;=m;++j){
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span>(i==<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>||j==<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>){
                dp[i][j] =<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;

            }<span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span>{
                dp[i][j]=(dp[i-<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>][j] + dp[i][j-<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>])%<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MOD</span>;
            }
        }
    }
    cout&lt;&lt;dp[n][m]&lt;&lt;endl;
}
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 64 位输出请用 printf(""%lld"")</span></pre>

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 048 利用二维前缀和信息迅速得到二维区域和</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. NumMatrix 类定义 (NumMatrix Class)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 构造函数：计算二维前缀和 (Constructor: Calculate 2D Prefix Sum)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 区域和查询 (sumRegion)</span>

<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">class</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">NumMatrix</span> {
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 存储二维前缀和的矩阵</span>
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&gt; sum;

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 构造函数</span>
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">NumMatrix</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&gt;&amp; matrix) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (matrix.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">empty</span>() || matrix[<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>].<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">empty</span>()) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span>;
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n = matrix.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>();
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> m = matrix[<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>].<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>();
        
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 初始化 n+1 行 m+1 列的矩阵，索引从 1 开始更方便计算边界</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// C++ vector 自动初始化为 0</span>
        sum.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">resize</span>(n + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;(m + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>));

        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 将原矩阵内容填入 sum 矩阵的 [1,1] 到 [n,m] 区域</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> a = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, c = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; c &lt; n; a++, c++) {
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> b = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, d = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; d &lt; m; b++, d++) {
                sum[a][b] = matrix[c][d];
            }
        }

        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 核心逻辑：计算二维前缀和</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// sum[i][j] 代表从 [0,0] 到 [i-1][j-1] 区域内所有元素的总和</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &lt;= n; i++) {
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> j = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; j &lt;= m; j++) {
                sum[i][j] += sum[i][j - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>] + sum[i - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>][j] - sum[i - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>][j - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>];
            }
        }
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 区域和查询</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// (a, b) 为左上角坐标，(c, d) 为右下角坐标</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">sumRegion</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> a, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> b, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> c, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> d) {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 因为 sum 矩阵是 1-indexed，所以右下角坐标需要加 1</span>
        c++;
        d++;
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 二维前缀和公式：右下大矩形 - 左侧长条 - 上方长条 + 左上重叠块</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> sum[c][d] - sum[c][b] - sum[a][d] + sum[a][b];
    }
};
</pre>

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 048 边框为1的最大正方形</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 查找最大 1 边框正方形主函数 (largest1BorderedSquare)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 构建二维前缀和 (build)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 区域求和计算 (sum)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 4. 边界安全访问辅助函数 (get)</span>

<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;algorithm&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">class</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Code02_LargestOneBorderedSquare</span> {
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 时间复杂度O(n * m * min(n,m))，额外空间复杂度O(1)</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 复杂度指标上绝对是最优解</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">largest1BorderedSquare</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&gt;&amp; g) {
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n = g.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>();
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> m = g[<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>].<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>();
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 预处理：原地将 g 转换为二维前缀和数组，节省空间</span>
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>(n, m, g);
        
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 如果整个矩阵和为 0，说明没有 1，直接返回 0</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">sum</span>(g, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, n - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, m - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>) == <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>) {
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
        }

        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 找到的最大合法正方形的边长，初始为 1（因为已经确认存在 1）</span>
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> ans = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> a = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; a &lt; n; a++) {
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> b = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; b &lt; m; b++) {
                <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// (a,b) 作为所有可能的左上角点</span>
                <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// (c,d) 是更大边长的右下角点，k 是当前尝试的边长</span>
                <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 从 ans + 1 开始尝试，因为我们要寻找比当前 ans 更大的正方形</span>
                <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> c = a + ans, d = b + ans, k = ans + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; c &lt; n &amp;&amp; d &lt; m; c++, d++, k++) {
                    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 核心逻辑：</span>
                    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 外层正方形总和 - 内部正方形总和 = 边框上 1 的数量</span>
                    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 对于边长为 k 的正方形，若边框全是 1，则数量应为 (k-1) * 4</span>
                    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">sum</span>(g, a, b, c, d) - <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">sum</span>(g, a + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, b + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, c - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, d - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>) == (k - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>) &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>) {
                        ans = k;
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> ans * ans;
    }

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">private</span>:
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 构建二维前缀和逻辑</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 把 g 变成原始二维数组的前缀和数组 sum，复用自己</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> m, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&gt;&amp; g) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; i &lt; n; i++) {
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> j = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; j &lt; m; j++) {
                g[i][j] += <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">get</span>(g, i, j - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>) + <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">get</span>(g, i - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, j) - <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">get</span>(g, i - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, j - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
            }
        }
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 区域求和计算</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">sum</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&gt;&amp; g, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> a, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> b, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> c, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> d) {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 如果左上角坐标已经越过右下角（如计算 1x1 正方形的内部区域），返回 0</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> a &gt; c ? <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span> : (g[c][d] - <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">get</span>(g, c, b - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>) - <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">get</span>(g, a - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, d) + <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">get</span>(g, a - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, b - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>));
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 4. 边界安全访问辅助函数</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 对应 Java 中的 get 静态方法，处理索引越界返回 0</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">get</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&gt;&amp; g, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> j) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> (i &lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span> || j &lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>) ? <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span> : g[i][j];
    }
};
</pre>
        </div>
        <br>"	
"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 048 二维差分模版(洛谷)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 二维差分更新逻辑 (add)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 前缀和还原矩阵逻辑 (build)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 矩阵清空逻辑 (clear)</span>

<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;cstring&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">class</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Code03_DiffMatrixLuogu</span> {
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">static</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span> = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1002</span>;

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 二维差分数组</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> diff[<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span>][<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span>];

    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n, q;

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 二维差分更新</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 在左上角 (a, b) 到右下角 (c, d) 的矩形区域内每个位置加上 k</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">add</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> a, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> b, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> c, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> d, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> k) {
        diff[a][b] += k;
        diff[c + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>][b] -= k;
        diff[a][d + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>] -= k;
        diff[c + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>][d + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>] += k;
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 构建最终矩阵</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 对差分数组求二维前缀和，从而还原出每个位置被修改后的最终值</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>() {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &lt;= n; i++) {
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> j = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; j &lt;= n; j++) {
                diff[i][j] += diff[i - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>][j] + diff[i][j - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>] - diff[i - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>][j - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>];
            }
        }
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 清空矩阵</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 为处理多组测试数据，清空 diff 数组</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">clear</span>() {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &lt;= n + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i++) {
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> j = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; j &lt;= n + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; j++) {
                diff[i][j] = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
            }
        }
    }
};
</pre>

        <br>"	
"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 048 用邮票贴满网格图</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 邮票放置判定主逻辑 (possibleToStamp)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 构建二维前缀和 (build)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 区域求和查询 (sumRegion)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 4. 二维差分区域增加 (add)</span>

<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">class</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Code04_StampingTheGrid</span> {
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 时间复杂度O(n*m)，额外空间复杂度O(n*m)</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">bool</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">possibleToStamp</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&gt;&amp; grid, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> h, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> w) {
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n = grid.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>();
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> m = grid[<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>].<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>();
        
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 构建原始矩阵的前缀和数组 sum</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 用于快速查询 grid 中某个区域是否全为 0（即是否可以放邮票）</span>
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">sum</span>(n + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;(m + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>));
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; i &lt; n; i++) {
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> j = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; j &lt; m; j++) {
                sum[i + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>][j + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>] = grid[i][j];
            }
        }
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>(sum);

        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 准备差分矩阵 diff</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// diff 用来标记哪些格子被邮票覆盖了</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 因为后面 add 操作会访问到 c+1, d+1，所以大小开到 n+2, m+2</span>
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">diff</span>(n + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;(m + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>));
        
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 遍历每一个可能的邮票左上角 (a, b)</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> a = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, c = a + h - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; c &lt;= n; a++, c++) {
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> b = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, d = b + w - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; d &lt;= m; b++, d++) {
                <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 如果原始矩阵中该矩形区域累加和为 0，说明全是空格，可以贴邮票</span>
                <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">sumRegion</span>(sum, a, b, c, d) == <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>) {
                    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">add</span>(diff, a, b, c, d);
                }
            }
        }

        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 将差分矩阵还原成前缀和矩阵，此时 diff[i][j] &gt; 0 代表被邮票覆盖过</span>
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>(diff);

        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 4. 最后检查：所有的空格子是否都被至少一张邮票覆盖</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; i &lt; n; i++) {
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> j = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; j &lt; m; j++) {
                <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// grid[i][j] == 0 说明是空格</span>
                <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// diff[i+1][j+1] == 0 说明没被邮票盖住</span>
                <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (grid[i][j] == <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span> &amp;&amp; diff[i + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>][j + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>] == <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>) {
                    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">false</span>;
                }
            }
        }
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">true</span>;
    }

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">private</span>:
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 构建二维前缀和</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&gt;&amp; m) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &lt; m.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>(); i++) {
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> j = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; j &lt; m[<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>].<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>(); j++) {
                m[i][j] += m[i - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>][j] + m[i][j - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>] - m[i - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>][j - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>];
            }
        }
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 区域求和查询</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">sumRegion</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&gt;&amp; sum, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> a, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> b, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> c, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> d) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> sum[c][d] - sum[c][b - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>] - sum[a - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>][d] + sum[a - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>][b - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>];
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 4. 二维差分区域增加</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">add</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&gt;&amp; diff, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> a, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> b, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> c, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> d) {
        diff[a][b] += <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
        diff[c + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>][d + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>] += <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
        diff[c + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>][b] -= <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
        diff[a][d + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>] -= <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
    }
};
</pre>

    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">eliminated</span>(n,<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>);

                k = (k+<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>)%n;
            }
        }
        eliminated[k] = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
        count--;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span>(eliminated[k]){
            k = (k+<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>) %n;
        }
    }
    cout&lt;&lt;k;
