"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><div><div>旺仔哥哥非常喜欢玩扫雷。现在给定一个初始的扫雷矩阵，其中用字符 `*` 表示雷，用 `.` 表示空白。<br>请你生成完整的扫雷矩阵。对于每个非雷格子，输出它周围八个方向中雷的个数；如果当前位置是雷，则仍输出 `*`。<br><br>【名词解释】<br><b>雷</b>: 用 `*` 表示的地雷；<br><b>邻格</b>: 与当前位置在八个方向上相邻的格子；<br><b>完整扫雷矩阵</b>: 填写完相应数字后的矩阵。</div><h3>输入描述：</h3><div>在一行中输入两个整数&nbsp;n,m<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">m</span>&nbsp;(1≦n,m≦1000)(1≦<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">m</span>≦1000)，分别表示矩阵的行数和列数。<br>接下来&nbsp;n<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>&nbsp;行，每行包含&nbsp;m<span style=""font-style: italic;"">m</span>&nbsp;个字符，每个字符是 `*` 或 `.`，无空格分隔，表示初始的扫雷矩阵。<br></div><h3>输出描述：</h3><div>输出&nbsp;n<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>&nbsp;行&nbsp;m<span style=""font-style: italic;"">m</span>&nbsp;列，表示完整的扫雷矩阵。对于每个位置：<br><br>∙ ∙如果该位置是雷，输出 `*`；<br>∙ ∙否则输出一个数字，该数字等于该位置周围八个邻格中雷的个数。<br></div></div><div><h2>示例1</h2><div><div>输入：<pre>4 4
....
..**
*.*.
.*.*</pre>复制</div><div>输出：<pre>0122
13**
*4*4
2*3*</pre>复制</div><div>说明：<pre>∙ ∙第一行 `....` 中没有雷，对应 `0122`； <br>∙ ∙第二行 `..**` 中两个雷，对应 `13**`； <br>∙ ∙第三行 `*.*.` 中除自身外有 4 个雷邻格，对应 `*4*4`； <br>∙ ∙第四行 `.*.*` 对应 `2*3*`。</pre></div></div></div></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;string&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n, m;
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 读取行列大小</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (!(cin &gt;&gt; n &gt;&gt; m)) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 读取扫雷地图</span>
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span>&gt; <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">grid</span>(n);
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; i &lt; n; i++) {
        cin &gt;&gt; grid[i];
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 定义 8 个方向的坐标偏移量</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> dx[] = {-<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, -<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, -<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>};
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> dy[] = {-<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, -<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, -<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>};

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 遍历并生成结果</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; i &lt; n; i++) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> j = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; j &lt; m; j++) {
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 如果当前是雷，直接输出</span>
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (grid[i][j] == <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'*'</span>) {
                cout &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'*'</span>;
            } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
                <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 如果是空白，开始数周围的雷</span>
                <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> count = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
                <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> k = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; k &lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">8</span>; k++) {
                    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> ni = i + dx[k]; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 邻居的行坐标</span>
                    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> nj = j + dy[k]; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 邻居的列坐标</span>
                    
                    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 判断邻居坐标是否在合法范围内</span>
                    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (ni &gt;= <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span> &amp;&amp; ni &lt; n &amp;&amp; nj &gt;= <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span> &amp;&amp; nj &lt; m) {
                        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (grid[ni][nj] == <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'*'</span>) {
                            count++;
                        }
                    }
                }
                <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 输出该格子的雷数</span>
                cout &lt;&lt; count;
            }
        }
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 每一行处理完后换行</span>
        cout &lt;&lt; endl;
    }

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}
</pre>

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><div><div>给定一个正整数&nbsp;N<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>&nbsp;(1≦N≦2×109)(1≦<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>≦2×109)。<br>现在需要将其转换为千分位格式，即从整数最低位开始，每三位数字插入一个英文逗号，以提高可读性。<br>例如，对于&nbsp;980364535980364535，转换后为&nbsp;980,364,535980,364,535。<br>请编写程序完成该格式转换。</div><h3>输入描述：</h3><div>在一行中输入一个整数&nbsp;N<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>&nbsp;(1≦N≦2×109)(1≦<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>≦2×109)。<br></div><h3>输出描述：</h3><div>输出一个字符串，表示将&nbsp;N<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>&nbsp;转换为千分位格式后的结果。<br>请不要输出多余的空格或换行。<br></div></div><div><h2>示例1</h2><div><div>输入：<pre>980364535</pre>复制</div><div>输出：<pre>980,364,535</pre>复制</div></div></div><div><h2>示例2</h2><div><div>输入：<pre>6</pre>复制</div><div>输出：<pre>6</pre></div></div></div></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;string&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> n;
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 将数字作为字符串读取，这样处理位数更方便</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (!(cin &gt;&gt; n)) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;

    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> len = n.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">length</span>();

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; i &lt; len; ++i) {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 输出当前数字</span>
        cout &lt;&lt; n[i];

        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 判断是否需要插入逗号：</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. (len - 1 - i) 是当前字符后面剩余的字符数</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 如果剩余字符数是 3 的倍数，且剩余数不为 0（即不是最后一位），则加逗号</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> ((len - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> - i) % <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">3</span> == <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span> &amp;&amp; i != len - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>) {
            cout &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#CE9178"">"",""</span>;
        }
    }

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><img src=""paste-d5fb4cb7242295e98994ca1025b0b3929269acc6.jpg"">旺仔哥哥经常在牛客上刷题，但有一天他突然忘记了登录密码（他没有绑定邮箱或手机）。<span style=""color:#C586C0""><br></span></pre><div><div>他记得密码是通过对原文字符串&nbsp;s<span style=""font-style: italic;"">s</span>&nbsp;中的每个小写英文字母向后错位&nbsp;n<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>&nbsp;次得到的。字母&nbsp;zz&nbsp;向后错位一次会变为&nbsp;aa，以此类推循环。<br>现给出原文字符串&nbsp;s<span style=""font-style: italic;"">s</span>&nbsp;和错位次数&nbsp;n<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>，请帮助旺仔哥哥计算出最终密码。<br></div><h3>输入描述：</h3><div>第一行输入一个整数&nbsp;n<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>&nbsp;(1≦n≦100)(1≦<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>≦100)，表示错位次数。<br>第二行输入一个由小写英文字母组成的字符串&nbsp;s<span style=""font-style: italic;"">s</span>&nbsp;(1≦∣s∣≦103)(1≦∣<span style=""font-style: italic;"">s</span>∣≦103)，表示原文字符串。<br></div><h3>输出描述：</h3><div>输出一个字符串，表示对&nbsp;s<span style=""font-style: italic;"">s</span>&nbsp;中每个字符向后错位&nbsp;n<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>&nbsp;次后得到的密码字符串。<br></div></div><div><h2>示例1</h2><div><div>输入：<pre>1
abcdefg</pre>复制</div><div>输出：<pre>bcdefgh</pre>复制</div><div>说明：<pre>∙ ∙每个字母向后移动 11 次，""a""→""b""""a""→""b""，""b""→""c""""b""→""c""，…，""g""→""h""""g""→""h""，得到 ""bcdefgh""""bcdefgh""。</pre></div></div></div><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;string&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> s;

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 读入位移次数和字符串</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (!(cin &gt;&gt; n &gt;&gt; s)) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">char</span> &amp;c : s) {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 使用循环移位公式</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 注意：先减去 'a' 变成 0-25，处理完再加回 'a'</span>
        c = (c - <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'a'</span> + n) % <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">26</span> + <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'a'</span>;
    }

    cout &lt;&lt; s &lt;&lt; endl;

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;""><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><img src=""paste-c37ef8aabaec243e8696e403c162fda4ad3e3749.jpg""></pre><div><div>规定一种对于复合词的简写方式：只保留每个组成单词的首字母，并将首字母大写后再连接在一起。<br>例如：<br>∙ ∙“College English Test”可简写为“CET”；<br>∙ ∙“Computer Science”可简写为“CS”；<br>∙ ∙“I am Bob”可简写为“IAB”。<br>现在输入一个由若干单词组成的复合词，请输出它的简写形式。<br></div><h3>输入描述：</h3><div>在一行中输入一个复合词，由若干单词组成。<br>∙ ∙单词数&nbsp;sum<span style=""font-style: italic;"">s</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">u</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">m</span>&nbsp;满足&nbsp;1≦sum≦1001≦<span style=""font-style: italic;"">s</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">u</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">m</span>≦100；<br>∙ ∙每个单词长度&nbsp;len<span style=""font-style: italic;"">l</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">e</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>&nbsp;满足&nbsp;1≦len≦501≦<span style=""font-style: italic;"">l</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">e</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>≦50；<br>∙ ∙单词之间由单个空格分隔；<br>∙ ∙每个单词仅由大小写英文字母组成。<br></div><h3>输出描述：</h3><div>输出一个字符串，为复合词的简写形式。<br>简写方式为：取每个单词的首字母并将其转换为大写，然后按原单词顺序依次连接。<br>请不要输出多余的空格或换行。<br></div></div><div><h2>示例1</h2><div><div>输入：<pre>International Collegiate Programming Contest</pre>复制</div><div>输出：<pre>ICPC</pre><br></div></div></div><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;bits/stdc++.h&gt;</span> <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 万能头文件，包含所有工具</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 竞赛优化：加速输入输出</span>
    ios::<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">sync_with_stdio</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">false</span>);
    cin.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">tie</span>(<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>);

    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> word;
    
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 核心技巧：只要还能读入单词（cin 会自动以空格为界限）</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (cin &gt;&gt; word) {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 取首字母并转大写，直接输出</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// toupper 返回的是 int，所以要强转回 char</span>
        cout &lt;&lt; (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">char</span>)<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">toupper</span>(word[<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>]);
    }
    
    cout &lt;&lt; endl; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 最后换行</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><div><div>众所周知，牛牛是一个 “1+1” 都能回答错误的小可爱，因此经常遭受旺仔哥哥的头槌惩罚。<br>今天，旺仔哥哥出了一场选择题测验，牛牛决定按照坊间传说来猜答案：<br>∙ ∙三长一短选最短；<br>∙ ∙三短一长选最长；<br>∙ ∙参差不齐就选 C。<br><br>【名词解释】<br>【三长一短】<u>三长一短</u>&nbsp;是指在四个选项长度中恰有一个选项的长度严格小于另外三个选项，且不存在四个选项长度中恰有一个选项的长度严格大于另外三个选项；<br>【三短一长】<u>三短一长</u>&nbsp;是指在四个选项长度中恰有一个选项的长度严格大于另外三个选项，且不存在四个选项长度中恰有一个选项的长度严格小于另外三个选项；<br>【参差不齐】<u>参差不齐</u>&nbsp;是指既不满足“三长一短”也不满足“三短一长”的情况。<br></div><h3>输入描述：</h3><div>第一行输入一个整数&nbsp;T<span style=""font-style: italic;"">T</span>&nbsp;(1≦T≦500)(1≦<span style=""font-style: italic;"">T</span>≦500)，表示题目数。<br>接下来共有&nbsp;T<span style=""font-style: italic;"">T</span>&nbsp;道题，每道题由 4 行字符串组成，分别对应选项 A、B、C、D；每个字符串长度不超过 600，由可见字符（字母、数字、符号等）组成。<br></div><h3>输出描述：</h3><div>对于每道题，输出按照上述坊间传说应选的选项字母（A、B、C 或 D），每个字母独占一行。<br></div></div><div><h2>示例1</h2><div><div>输入：<pre>3
A.3.141592653589
B.2.718281828459
C.0.618033988749
D.0.577215664901532860
A.wo_shi_cuo_de
B.wo_bu_dui
C.wo_shi_dui_de
D.C_shi_dui_de
A.3.141592653589
B.2.718281828459
C.0.618033988749
D.0.577215664901</pre>复制</div><div>输出：<pre>D
B
C</pre>复制</div><div>说明：<pre>∙ ∙第 1 道题中，选项长度分别为 14、14、14、18，恰有一个最长，符合“三短一长”，选最长 D； <br>∙ ∙第 2 道题中，选项长度分别为 13、9、13、12，恰有一个最短，符合“三长一短”，选最短 B； <br>∙ ∙第 3 道题中，四个选项长度均相同，属于“参差不齐”，选 C。</pre></div></div></div></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;bits/stdc++.h&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 解决单组测试用例的函数</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">solve</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> s[<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">4</span>];
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> len[<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">4</span>];
    
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 读入 4 个选项并记录长度</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; i &lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">4</span>; ++i) {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 虽然题目没说有空格，但在处理这种整行字符串时，getline 比 cin 更稳</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (!(<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">getline</span>(cin, s[i]))) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span>;
        len[i] = s[i].<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">length</span>();
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 统计长度分布</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> minL = *<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">min_element</span>(len, len + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">4</span>);
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> maxL = *<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">max_element</span>(len, len + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">4</span>);</pre><div>段代码使用的是 C++ 标准库（STL）中的算法函数，用于在一个数组（或容器）中寻找<b>最小值</b>和<b>最大值</b>。</div><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">简单来说，这两行代码的作用是：从长度为 4 的数组 <code>len</code> 中，分别找出最小的元素和最大的元素，并将它们的值赋给 <code>minL</code> 和 <code>maxL</code>。    
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> cntMin = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, cntMax = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> minIdx = -<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, maxIdx = -<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
    
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; i &lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">4</span>; ++i) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (len[i] == minL) {
            cntMin++;
            minIdx = i;
        }
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (len[i] == maxL) {
            cntMax++;
            maxIdx = i;
        }
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 根据题目定义的逻辑进行判断</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 三长一短：恰有一个最短，且不存在恰有一个最长</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">bool</span> isThreeLongOneShort = (cntMin == <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> &amp;&amp; cntMax != <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 三短一长：恰有一个最长，且不存在恰有一个最短</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">bool</span> isThreeShortOneLong = (cntMax == <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> &amp;&amp; cntMin != <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (isThreeLongOneShort) {
        cout &lt;&lt; (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">char</span>)(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">'A'</span> + minIdx) &lt;&lt; endl;
    } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (isThreeShortOneLong) {
        cout &lt;&lt; (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">char</span>)(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">'A'</span> + maxIdx) &lt;&lt; endl;
    } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
        cout &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""C""</span> &lt;&lt; endl; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 参差不齐</span>
    }
}

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 竞赛必备：优化 I/O</span>
    ios::<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">sync_with_stdio</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">false</span>);
    cin.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">tie</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">NULL</span>);

    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">T</span>;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (cin &gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">T</span>) {
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> dummy;
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">getline</span>(cin, dummy); <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 吸收掉 T 后面多余的换行符</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">T</span>--) {
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">solve</span>();
        }
    }
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}
</pre>

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <div><div>给定&nbsp;N<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>&nbsp;名学生及其信息，包含：<br>∙ ∙&nbsp;姓名&nbsp;s<span style=""font-style: italic;"">s</span>，仅含小写字母，长度不超过&nbsp;88；<br>∙ ∙&nbsp;语文、数学、英语成绩&nbsp;c1,c2,c3<span style=""font-style: italic;"">c</span>1​,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">c</span>2​,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">c</span>3​，整数且&nbsp;0≦ci≦1500≦<span style=""font-style: italic;"">c</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>​≦150。<br>定义总分&nbsp;T=c1+c2+c3<span style=""font-style: italic;"">T</span>=<span style=""font-style: italic;"">c</span>1​+<span style=""font-style: italic;"">c</span>2​+<span style=""font-style: italic;"">c</span>3​，求总分最大的学生信息；若存在多名，取输入顺序最小者。<br></div><h3>输入描述：</h3><div>第一行包含整数&nbsp;N<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>，(1≦N≦1000)(1≦<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>≦1000)；<br>接下来&nbsp;N<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>&nbsp;行，每行包含字符串&nbsp;s<span style=""font-style: italic;"">s</span>&nbsp;和三个整数&nbsp;c1,c2,c3<span style=""font-style: italic;"">c</span>1​,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">c</span>2​,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">c</span>3​，依次表示学生姓名及三门成绩。<br></div><h3>输出描述：</h3><div>输出姓名&nbsp;s<span style=""font-style: italic;"">s</span>&nbsp;及对应成绩&nbsp;c1,c2,c3<span style=""font-style: italic;"">c</span>1​,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">c</span>2​,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">c</span>3​，以空格分隔。<br></div></div><div><h2>示例1</h2><div><div>输入：<pre>4
alice 100 90 80
david 90 100 80
mary 80 80 100
bob 100 90 80</pre>复制</div><div>输出：<pre>alice 100 90 80</pre>复制</div><div>说明：</div></div></div><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">样例中，alice 与 bob 总分均为 270270，顺序提前者 alice 为答案。<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">struct</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Student</span> {
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> name;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> c1,c2,c3;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> total;
};
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n;
    cin&gt;&gt;n;

    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Student</span> best;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> maxTotal =-<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i =<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;i&lt;n;i++){
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> currentName;
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> g1,g2,g3;
        cin&gt;&gt;currentName&gt;&gt;g1&gt;&gt;g2&gt;&gt;g3;

        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> currentTotal = g1 +g2+g3;

        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span>(currentTotal&gt;maxTotal){
            maxTotal = currentTotal;
            best.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">name</span> = currentName;
            best.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">c1</span> = g1;
            best.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">c2</span> = g2;
            best.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">c3</span> = g3;
        }
    }
    cout&lt;&lt;best.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">name</span>&lt;&lt;<span style=""color:#CE9178"">"" ""</span>&lt;&lt;best.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">c1</span>&lt;&lt;<span style=""color:#CE9178"">"" ""</span>&lt;&lt;best.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">c2</span>&lt;&lt;<span style=""color:#CE9178"">"" ""</span>&lt;&lt;best.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">c3</span>&lt;&lt;endl;

}

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#569CD6""><br></span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><div><h2>描述</h2><div>你需要实现一个函数，给定平面上的点&nbsp;(a,b)(<span style=""font-style: italic;"">a</span>,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">b</span>)，以及一条由另外两个点&nbsp;(x1,y1)(<span style=""font-style: italic;"">x</span>1​,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">y</span>1​)&nbsp;和&nbsp;(x2,y2)(<span style=""font-style: italic;"">x</span>2​,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">y</span>2​)&nbsp;确定的直线&nbsp;L<span style=""font-style: italic;"">L</span>，求点&nbsp;(a,b)(<span style=""font-style: italic;"">a</span>,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">b</span>)&nbsp;到直线&nbsp;L<span style=""font-style: italic;"">L</span>&nbsp;的距离。<br></div><h3>输入描述：</h3><div>共&nbsp;22&nbsp;行。<br>第一行是两个空格隔开的整数&nbsp;a,b<span style=""font-style: italic;"">a</span>,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">b</span>。<br>第二行是四个空格隔开的整数&nbsp;x1,y1,x2,y2<span style=""font-style: italic;"">x</span>1​,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">y</span>1​,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">x</span>2​,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">y</span>2​。</div><h3>输出描述：</h3><div>共一行，一个实数，表示点&nbsp;(a,b)(<span style=""font-style: italic;"">a</span>,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">b</span>)&nbsp;到直线&nbsp;L<span style=""font-style: italic;"">L</span>&nbsp;的距离，保留两位小数。</div></div><div><h2>示例1</h2><div><div>输入：<pre>0 0
-1 1 1 1</pre>复制</div><div>输出：<pre>1.00</pre>复制</div></div></div><div><h2>备注：</h2></div><div style=""color: rgb(255, 255, 255); white-space-collapse: collapse; background-color: rgb(54, 54, 54);""><span style=""white-space-collapse: preserve; font-family: inherit; background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212);"">&nbsp;</span><span style=""white-space-collapse: preserve; font-family: inherit; background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212);"">1≤a,b,x1,y1,x2,y2&lt;231</span><span style=""white-space-collapse: preserve; font-family: inherit; background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212);"">1</span><span style=""white-space-collapse: preserve; font-family: inherit; background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212);"">≤</span><span style=""white-space-collapse: preserve; font-family: inherit; background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); font-style: italic;"">a</span><span style=""white-space-collapse: preserve; font-family: inherit; background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212);"">,</span><span style=""white-space-collapse: preserve; font-family: inherit; background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); font-style: italic;"">b</span><span style=""white-space-collapse: preserve; font-family: inherit; background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212);"">,</span><span style=""white-space-collapse: preserve; font-family: inherit; background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); font-style: italic;"">x</span><span style=""white-space-collapse: preserve; font-family: inherit; background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212);"">1</span><span style=""white-space-collapse: preserve; font-family: inherit; background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212);"">​</span><span style=""white-space-collapse: preserve; font-family: inherit; background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212);"">,</span><span style=""white-space-collapse: preserve; font-family: inherit; background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); font-style: italic;"">y</span><span style=""white-space-collapse: preserve; font-family: inherit; background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212);"">1</span><span style=""white-space-collapse: preserve; font-family: inherit; background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212);"">​</span><span style=""white-space-collapse: preserve; font-family: inherit; background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212);"">,</span><span style=""white-space-collapse: preserve; font-family: inherit; background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); font-style: italic;"">x</span><span style=""white-space-collapse: preserve; font-family: inherit; background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212);"">2</span><span style=""white-space-collapse: preserve; font-family: inherit; background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212);"">​</span><span style=""white-space-collapse: preserve; font-family: inherit; background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212);"">,</span><span style=""white-space-collapse: preserve; font-family: inherit; background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); font-style: italic;"">y</span><span style=""white-space-collapse: preserve; font-family: inherit; background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212);"">2</span><span style=""white-space-collapse: preserve; font-family: inherit; background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212);"">​</span><span style=""white-space-collapse: preserve; font-family: inherit; background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212);"">&lt;</span><span style=""white-space-collapse: preserve; font-family: inherit; background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212);"">2</span><span style=""white-space-collapse: preserve; font-family: inherit; background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212);"">3</span><span style=""white-space-collapse: preserve; font-family: inherit; background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212);"">1</span><span style=""white-space-collapse: preserve; font-family: inherit; background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212);"">。</span>在几何学中，如果我们有两个向量 U 和 V，它们之间的夹角为 theta，那么以它们为邻边的平行四边形面积公式是：</div><div style=""color: rgb(255, 255, 255); white-space-collapse: collapse; background-color: rgb(54, 54, 54);""><strong>面积 = |U| * |V| * sin(theta)</strong></div></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#569CD6"">double</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">getDistance</span>(point <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">P</span>, line <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">L</span>){
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// TODO: 计算点P到直线L的距离</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">auto</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">A</span>=<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">L</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">point_A</span>;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">auto</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">B</span>=<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">L</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">point_B</span>;
    point <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">AB</span>=<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">point</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">B</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">x</span>-<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">A</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">x</span>,<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">B</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">y</span>-<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">A</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">y</span>);
    point <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">AP</span>=<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">point</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">P</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">x</span>-<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">A</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">x</span>,<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">P</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">y</span>-<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">A</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">y</span>);
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">auto</span> dist=[&amp;](point a, point b)-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">double</span>{
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">sqrt</span>(<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">pow</span>(a.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">x</span>-b.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">x</span>,<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>)+<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">pow</span>(a.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">y</span>-b.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">y</span>,<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>));
    };
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">auto</span> cross=[&amp;](point a,point b)-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">double</span>{

    };
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">abs</span>(<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">cross</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">AB</span>,<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">AP</span>)/(<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">dist</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">A</span>,<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">B</span>)));

            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><div><div>一路地铁依次经过&nbsp;n<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>&nbsp;个站点，编号依次为&nbsp;1∼n1∼<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>。地铁从第&nbsp;i<span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>&nbsp;个站点到第&nbsp;i+1<span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>+1&nbsp;个站点需要用&nbsp;ti<span italic;"">s</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>​&nbsp;秒。<br>旺仔哥哥想从第&nbsp;x<span style=""font-style: italic;"">x</span>&nbsp;站坐地铁到第&nbsp;y<span style=""font-style: italic;"">y</span>&nbsp;站。那么他在地铁上的最长时间是多少？<br>注：最长时间，即地铁刚到第&nbsp;x<span style=""font-style: italic;"">x</span>&nbsp;站就上地铁，地铁即将离开第&nbsp;y<span style=""font-style: italic;"">y</span>&nbsp;站才下地铁的情况下，旺仔哥哥在地铁上的时间。单位为秒。<br><br>你需要实现一个函数，接受的参数有四个，分别是：<br>∙ ∙序列&nbsp;t1,t2,…,tn−1(1≦ti≦103)<span style=""font-style: italic;"">t</span>1​,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">t</span>2​,…,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">t</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>−1​(1≦<span style=""font-style: italic;"">t</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>​≦103)，表示地铁在相邻两站之间的用时。<br>∙ ∙序列&nbsp;s1,s2,…,sn(1≦ti≦103)<span style=""font-style: italic;"">s</span>1​,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">s</span>2​,…,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">s</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>​(1≦<span style=""font-style: italic;"">t</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>​≦103)，表示地铁在每一站的停靠时间。<br>∙ ∙两个正整数&nbsp;x,y(1≦x≦y≦103)<span style=""font-style: italic;"">x</span>,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">y</span>(1≦<span style=""font-style: italic;"">x</span>≦<span style=""font-style: italic;"">y</span>≦103)，表示旺仔哥哥想从第&nbsp;x<span style=""font-style: italic;"">x</span>&nbsp;站坐到第&nbsp;y<span style=""font-style: italic;"">y</span>&nbsp;站。<br><br>返回值为一个正整数，即旺仔哥哥在地铁上的最长时间，单位为秒。<br></div></div><div><h2>示例1</h2><div><div>输入：<pre>[150,180,170],[35,32,33,34],2,4</pre>复制</div><div>返回值：<pre>449</pre>复制</div><div>说明：<pre>旺仔哥哥在地铁刚到第&nbsp;22&nbsp;站就上了地铁，接下来地铁经过如下流程：<br><br>- 先在第&nbsp;22&nbsp;站停靠&nbsp;3232&nbsp;秒。<br>- 然后用&nbsp;180180&nbsp;秒开到第&nbsp;33&nbsp;站。<br>- 在第&nbsp;33&nbsp;站停靠&nbsp;3333&nbsp;秒。<br>- 然后用&nbsp;170170&nbsp;秒开到第&nbsp;44&nbsp;站。<br>- 最后在第&nbsp;44&nbsp;站停靠&nbsp;3434&nbsp;秒。<br><br>然后旺仔哥哥下车。在地铁上的总时间是&nbsp;32+180+33+170+34=44932+180+33+170+34=449&nbsp;秒。</pre></div></div></div></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">countLongestSubwayTime</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span             <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><a href=""https://www.nowcoder.com/share/jump/716254661768987390092"">https://www.nowcoder.com/share/jump/716254661768987390092</a><span style=""color:#C586C0""><br></span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">栈的贪心排序</pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;bits/stdc++.h&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n;
    cin&gt;&gt;n;

    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">a</span>(n+<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);

    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">affter_max</span>(n+<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>,<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>);
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i =n;i&gt;=<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;--i){

    }
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">stack</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; s;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i =<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> ;i&lt;=n;++i){

        }
    }
    cout&lt;&lt;endl;

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><div><div>给定长度为&nbsp;n<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>&nbsp;的入栈序列pushedpushed&nbsp;和长度为&nbsp;n<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>&nbsp;的出栈序列&nbsp;poppedpopped，两者均为&nbsp;1∼n1∼<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>&nbsp;的排列。初始时栈为空，只允许在栈顶进行插入（入栈）和删除（出栈）操作；若可通过若干操作使出栈顺序等于&nbsp;poppedpopped，则称&nbsp;poppedpopped&nbsp;为合法出栈序列。<br><br>现有&nbsp;q<span style=""font-style: italic;"">q</span>&nbsp;组测试，每组给定对应序列，判断&nbsp;poppedpopped&nbsp;是否为合法出栈序列。<br><br>【名词解释】<br>【排列】长度为&nbsp;n<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>&nbsp;的&nbsp;<u>排列</u>&nbsp;是由&nbsp;1∼n1∼<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>&nbsp;的&nbsp;n<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>&nbsp;个整数按任意顺序组成的序列，其中每个整数恰好出现一次。<br></div><h3>输入描述：</h3><div>第一行输入整数&nbsp;q&nbsp;(1≦q≦5)<span style=""font-style: italic;"">q</span>&nbsp;(1≦<span style=""font-style: italic;"">q</span>≦5)，表示测试组数。<br>接下来对于每组测试，依次输入：<br>1.1.​一行整数&nbsp;n&nbsp;(1≦n≦105)<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>&nbsp;(1≦<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>≦105)，表示序列长度；<br>2.2.​一行&nbsp;n<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>&nbsp;个整数，为入栈序列&nbsp;pushed1,…,pushednpushed1​,…,pushed<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>​；<br>3.3.​一行&nbsp;n<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>&nbsp;个整数，为出栈序列&nbsp;popped1,…,poppednpopped1​,…,popped<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>​。<br></div><h3>输出描述：</h3><div>对于每组测试，输出一行，如果&nbsp;poppedpopped&nbsp;为合法出栈序列，则输出&nbsp;YesYes；否则输出&nbsp;NoNo。<br></div></div><div><h2>示例1</h2><div><div>输入：<pre>2
5
1 2 3 4 5
2 5 4 1 3
5
1 2 3 4 5
2 5 4 3 1</pre>复制</div><div>输出：<pre>No
Yes</pre><br>
</div></div></div></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;stack&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> q;
    cin &gt;&gt; q;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; i &lt; q; i++) {
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n; cin &gt;&gt; n;
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; pushed, poped;
        pushed.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">resize</span>(n);
        poped.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">resize</span>(n);
        
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> j = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; j &lt; n; j++) cin &gt;&gt; pushed[j];
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> k = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; k &lt; n; k++) cin &gt;&gt; poped[k];

        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">stack</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; s;
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> idx = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;

        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 修改点 1：把逻辑简化，每个数先老老实实入栈</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> j = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; j &lt; pushed.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>(); j++) {
            s.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">push</span>(pushed[j]);
            
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 修改点 2：【核心】每入一个，就尝试连环弹出</span>
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 这里不能写 idx++ 在括号里，必须对上了才能加</span>
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (!s.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">empty</span>() &amp;&amp; s.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">top</span>() == poped[idx]) { 
                s.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">pop</span>();
                idx++; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 修改点 3：只有匹配成功，才让指针后移</span>
            }
        } <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 修改点 4：补上 for 循环的右括号</span>

        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 此时，那个最后的 while(1) 已经不需要了，因为上面已经弹干净了</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (!s.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">empty</span>()) cout &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""No""</span> &lt;&lt; endl;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> cout &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""Yes""</span> &lt;&lt; endl;
    }
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}

  这个更好          <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">stopAtWho</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&amp; a, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> m) {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n = a.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>();

<div><span style=""font-family: inherit;"">        </span>有&nbsp;n<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>&nbsp;个小朋友排成一圈，按照<strong>顺时针顺序</strong>依次被编号为&nbsp;1∼n1∼<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>，每个小朋友衣服上都有一个数字，第&nbsp;i<span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>&nbsp;个小朋友的数字是&nbsp;ai<span style=""font-style: italic;"">a</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>​。<br><br><div>旺仔哥哥想要选出一个小朋友，于是他先站在&nbsp;11&nbsp;号小朋友旁边，然后以如下方式移动&nbsp;m<span style=""font-style: italic;"">m</span>&nbsp;次：</div><blockquote>逆时针走过「当前小朋友衣服上的数字」数量个小朋友。</blockquote>旺仔哥哥想知道，他最后会站在哪位小朋友旁边。<br><br><div>你需要实现一个函数，包含以下两个参数：</div><div>∙ ∙一个序列&nbsp;a<span style=""font-style: italic;"">a</span>，第&nbsp;i<span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>&nbsp;个小朋友的数字是&nbsp;ai<span style=""font-style: italic;"">a</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>​。</div><div>∙ ∙一个正整数&nbsp;m<span style=""font-style: italic;"">m</span>，表示旺仔哥哥的移动次数。</div>你需要计算出旺仔哥哥最后会站在哪位小朋友旁边，并将这个结果作为该函数的返回值。<br></div></div><div><h2>示例1</h2><div><div>输入：<pre>[2,1,4,5,2,3],3</pre>复制</div><div>返回值：<pre>5</pre>复制</div><div>说明：<pre>初始时，旺仔哥哥站在&nbsp;11&nbsp;号小朋友旁边。<br><br><div>第 1 次移动前，11&nbsp;号小朋友衣服上的数字&nbsp;a1=2<span style=""font-style: italic;"">a</span>1​=2，因此旺仔哥哥需要逆时针走过&nbsp;22&nbsp;个小朋友。旺仔哥哥走到&nbsp;55&nbsp;号小朋友旁边。</div><div><br></div><div>第 2 次移动前，55&nbsp;号小朋友衣服上的数字&nbsp;a5=2<span style=""font-style: italic;"">a</span>5​=2，因此旺仔哥哥需要逆时针走过&nbsp;22&nbsp;个小朋友。旺仔哥哥走到&nbsp;33&nbsp;号小朋友旁边。</div><div><br></div>第 3 次移动前，33&nbsp;号小朋友衣服上的数字&nbsp;a3=4<span style=""font-style: italic;"">a</span>3​=4，因此旺仔哥哥需要逆时针走过&nbsp;44&nbsp;个小朋友。旺仔哥哥走到&nbsp;55&nbsp;号小朋友旁边。<br><br><div>最终旺仔哥哥站在&nbsp;55&nbsp;号小朋友旁边。</div></pre></div></div></div></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#569CD6"">class</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Solution</span> {
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">/**
     * 代码中的类名、方法名、参数名已经指定，请勿修改，直接返回方法规定的值即可
     *
     * 计算出旺仔哥哥最后会站在哪位小朋友旁边
     * @param a int整型vector 第 i 个小朋友的数字是 a_i
     * @param m int整型 表示旺仔哥哥的移动次数
     * @return int整型
     */</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">stopAtWho</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&amp; a, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> m) {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// write code here</span>
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> idx = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;i&lt;m;i++){
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> k = a[idx];
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span>(idx-k&lt;<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>){
                idx+=a.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>();
            }
            idx=(idx-k+a.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>())%a.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>();
        }
        idx++;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> idx;
    }

    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">calculate</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span>&amp; s,<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&amp; index){

            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span>(c == <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'('</span>){

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><div><div>给定长度为&nbsp;n<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>&nbsp;的字符串&nbsp;s<span style=""font-style: italic;"">s</span>，其字符&nbsp;si∈{R,D}<span style=""font-style: italic;"">s</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>​∈{R,D}&nbsp;表示第&nbsp;i<span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>&nbsp;位参议员的阵营。其中 R 代表红帮，D 代表黑帮。<br>参议员按照索引&nbsp;11&nbsp;到&nbsp;n<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>&nbsp;的顺序循环行动。若剩余<strong>有行动权的</strong>参议员均属于同一阵营，则该阵营获胜并结束流程；否则，当前参<br>议员可选择：<br>1.1.​&nbsp;弹劾一名仍可行动的参议员，使其在后续轮次中失去行动权。<br>2.2.​&nbsp;（仅当剩余参议员同阵营时）直接宣布胜利。<br><div>你需要实现一个函数，求出所有参议员均采用最优策略时，最终获胜的阵营的名称。</div><div><br></div>函数接受的参数为一个字符串&nbsp;s<span style=""font-style: italic;"">s</span>，长度&nbsp;n<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>&nbsp;(1≦n≦104)(1≦<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>≦104)，且&nbsp;si∈{R,D}<span style=""font-style: italic;"">s</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>​∈{R,D}。<br>函数的返回值为一个字符串 `Red` 或 `Dark`，分别表示红帮或黑帮获胜。<br></div></div><div><h2>示例1</h2><div><div>输入：<pre>""DR""</pre>复制</div><div>返回值：<pre>""Dark""</pre>复制</div><div>说明：<pre>第 1 轮时，第一个参议员来自 Dark 阵营，他可以使用第一项权利禁止第二个参议员的权利<br>这样第二个参议员就无法使用任何权利了。<br>第 2 轮时，第一个参议员可以宣布胜利，因为他是唯一一个有投票权的人。</pre></div></div></div><div><h2>示例2</h2><div><div>输入：<pre>""DRR""</pre>复制</div><div>返回值：<pre>""Red""</pre>复制</div><div>说明：<pre>第 1 轮时，第一个来自 Dark 阵营的参议员可以使用第一项权利禁止第二个参议员的权利<br>第 2 轮时，第三个来自 Red 阵营的参议员可以使用他的第一项权利禁止第一个参议员的权利<br>这样在第 3 轮只剩下第三个参议员拥有投票的权利，于是他可以宣布胜利。</pre></div></div></div></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;string&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;queue&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">class</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Solution</span> {
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">predictPartyVictory</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> s) {
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n = s.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">length</span>();
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 定义两个队列，分别存放红帮 (Red) 和黑帮 (Dark) 的参议员索引</span>
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">queue</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; red;
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">queue</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; dark;

        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 初始化队列</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; i &lt; n; ++i) {
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (s[i] == <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'R'</span>) {
                red.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">push</span>(i);
            } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
                dark.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">push</span>(i);
            }
        }

        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 模拟对决</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (!red.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">empty</span>() &amp;&amp; !dark.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">empty</span>()) {
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> r_idx = red.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">front</span>();
            red.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">pop</span>();
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> d_idx = dark.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">front</span>();
            dark.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">pop</span>();

            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 索引小的人先行使权力，弹劾对方</span>
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (r_idx &lt; d_idx) {
                <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 红帮获胜，将其索引 + n 重新加入队列，代表进入下一轮</span>
                red.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">push</span>(r_idx + n);
            } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
                <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 黑帮获胜，将其索引 + n 重新加入队列</span>
                dark.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">push</span>(d_idx + n);
            }
        }

        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 返回最终获胜阵营</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> red.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">empty</span>() ? <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""Dark""</span> : <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""Red""</span>;
    }
};

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 简单的测试主函数</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Solution</span> sol;
    cout &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""示例1 (DR): ""</span> &lt;&lt; sol.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">predictPartyVictory</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""DR""</span>) &lt;&lt; endl;    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 输出: Dark</span>
    cout &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""示例2 (DRR): ""</span> &lt;&lt; sol.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">predictPartyVictory</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""DRR""</span>) &lt;&lt; endl;  <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 输出: Red</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}
</pre>

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><div><div>给定整数序列&nbsp;a1,a2,…,aN<span style=""font-style: italic;"">a</span>1​,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">a</span>2​,…,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">a</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>​&nbsp;和常数&nbsp;C<span style=""font-style: italic;"">C</span>，统计序列中有多少有序数对&nbsp;(i,j)(<span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">j</span>)&nbsp;满足&nbsp;1≦i,j≦N1≦<span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">j</span>≦<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>&nbsp;且&nbsp;ai−aj=C<span style=""font-style: italic;"">a</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>​−<span style=""font-style: italic;"">a</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">j</span>​=<span style=""font-style: italic;"">C</span>。<br></div><h3>输入描述：</h3><div><div>第一行输入两个整数&nbsp;N,C&nbsp;(1≦N≦2×105,&nbsp;0≦C&lt;230)<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">C</span>&nbsp;(1≦<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>≦2×105,&nbsp;0≦<span style=""font-style: italic;"">C</span>&lt;230)；<br>第二行输入&nbsp;N<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>&nbsp;个整数&nbsp;a1,a2,…,aN&nbsp;(0≦ai&lt;230)<span style=""font-style: italic;"">a</span>1​,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">a</span>2​,…,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">a</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>​&nbsp;(0≦<span style=""font-style: italic;"">a</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>​&lt;230)。<br></div></div><h3>输出描述：</h3><div>输出一个整数，表示满足条件的有序数对数量。</div></div><div><h2>示例1</h2><div><div>输入：<pre>5 2
1 3 3 4 5</pre>复制</div><div>输出：<pre>4</pre>复制</div><div>说明：<pre>在此样例中，满足条件的有序数对有 (3,1),(4,1),(4,2),(5,3)(3,1),(4,1),(4,2),(5,3)，共 44 对。</pre></div></div></div></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;map&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 优化输入输出效率</span>
    ios::<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">sync_with_stdio</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">false</span>);
    cin.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">tie</span>(<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>);

    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">N</span>;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">C</span>;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (!(cin &gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">N</span> &gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">C</span>)) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;

    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span>&gt; <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">a</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">N</span>);
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">map</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span>, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span>&gt; counts;

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 读取数据并统计每个数字出现的频率</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; i &lt; <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">N</span>; ++i) {
        cin &gt;&gt; a[i];
        counts[a[i]]++;
    }

    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> total_pairs = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 遍历 map，寻找满足条件的 val + C</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 遍历每一个出现过的数字作为 aj</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">auto</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span>&amp; [val, count] : counts) {
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> target = val + <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">C</span>;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (counts.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">count</span>(target)) {
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 如果存在 ai = aj + C</span>
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 数对数量 = (aj出现的次数) * (ai出现的次数)</span>
            total_pairs += count * counts[target];
        }
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 输出最终结果</span>
    cout &lt;&lt; total_pairs &lt;&lt; endl;

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}

            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><div><div><div>给定一个正整数，请你判断这个数是不是快乐数。</div><div>快乐数：对于一个正整数，每次把他替换为他每个位置上的数字的平方和，如果这个数能变为 1 则是快乐数，如果不可能变成 1 则不是快乐数。</div><div>例如：正整数 19</div><div>转换过程为 1*1+9*9=82 , 8*8+2*2=68，6*6+8*8=100，1*1+0*0+0*0=1 ，所以他是快乐数。</div><div><br></div><div>数据范围：输入的正整数满足&nbsp;1≤n≤109&nbsp;1≤<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>≤109&nbsp;</div></div></div><div><h2>示例1</h2><div><div>输入：<pre>19</pre>复制</div><div>返回值：<pre>true
</pre>复制</div></div></div><div><h2>示例2</h2><div><div>输入：<pre>111</pre>复制</div><div>返回值：<pre>false
</pre><br>
</div></div></div></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#569CD6"">class</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Solution</span> {

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">/**
     * 代码中的类名、方法名、参数名已经指定，请勿修改，直接返回方法规定的值即可
     *
     * 
     * @param n int整型 
     * @return bool布尔型
     */</span>
     
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">getNext</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n){
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> totalSum = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span>(n&gt;<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>){
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> d = n%<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">10</span>;
            totalSum += d*d;
            n/=<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">10</span>;

        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> totalSum;

    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">bool</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">happynum</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n) {

        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span>(n!=<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> &amp;&amp; seen.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">find</span>(n) == seen.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">end</span>()){
            seen.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">insert</span>(n);
            n = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">getNext</span>(n);
        }
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> n==<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
    }

"<img src=""paste-8b4cde99bdd1b415bd6f27cccecfaeae3cf90a44.jpg""><br>set和multiset不能用地址直接减，必须要索引<br>"	
"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><img src=""paste-f73ca353fdf2de950173a1768e52bd6c5db7b063.jpg""><span style=""color:#6A9955""><br></span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><img src=""paste-01e2ac5f4da2d0b0514ea517cc5b7197ec57fb00.jpg""><br></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">/**
 * struct ListNode {
 *     int val;
 *     struct ListNode *next;
 *     ListNode(int x) : val(x), next(nullptr) {}
 * };
 */</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">class</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Solution</span> {
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span>* <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">swapPairs</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span>* head) {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 创建虚拟头节点，简化头部的交换逻辑</span>
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span>* dummy = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">new</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span>(<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>);
        dummy-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span> = head;
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span>* cur = dummy;

        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 只有当后面至少有两个节点时，才需要交换</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span> != <span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span> &amp;&amp; cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span> != <span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>) {
            <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span>* node1 = cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>;      <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 第一个节点</span>
            <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span>* node2 = cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 第二个节点</span>

            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// --- 开始三步交换逻辑 ---</span>
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 步骤一：cur 指向 node2</span>
            cur-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span> = node2;
            
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 步骤二：node1 指向 node2 的后面（防止链表断裂）</span>
            node1-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span> = node2-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>;
            
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 步骤三：node2 指向 node1</span>
            node2-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span> = node1;

            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 将指针移动到交换后的第二个节点（即 node1），准备下一对交换</span>
            cur = node1;
        }

        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">ListNode</span>* res = dummy-&gt;<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">next</span>;
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">delete</span> dummy; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 释放虚拟头节点</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> res;
    }
};</pre>

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><div>
        <div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;string&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;list&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;unordered_map&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">solve_list</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n, m;
    cin &gt;&gt; n &gt;&gt; m;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">list</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span>&gt; q;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">unordered_map</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span>, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">list</span>::iterator&gt; pos;

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; i &lt; n; ++i) {
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> s;
        cin &gt;&gt; s;
        q.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">push_back</span>(s);
        pos[s] = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">prev</span>(q.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">end</span>());
    }

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; i &lt; m; ++i) {
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> x, y;
        cin &gt;&gt; x &gt;&gt; y;
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 从原位置移除</span>
        q.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">erase</span>(pos[x]);
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 插入到 y 的前面</span>
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">auto</span> it_y = pos[y];
        pos[x] = q.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">insert</span>(it_y, x);
    }

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">auto</span> it = q.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">begin</span>(); it != q.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">end</span>(); ++it) {
        cout &lt;&lt; *it &lt;&lt; (<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">next</span>(it) == q.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">end</span>() ? <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""""</span> : <span style=""color:#CE9178"">"" ""</span>);
    }
    cout &lt;&lt; endl;
}</pre>
        </div>
        <br>
<div><span style=""font-family: inherit;"">        </span>在熙熙攘攘的商业街区，一家人气爆棚的网红奶茶店前总是大排长龙。然而，在这有序的队伍中，偶尔也会出现不和谐的插队行为——插队不仅破坏公平排队的秩序，也引发其他顾客的不满与抱怨。<br><br>假设店前有&nbsp;n<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>&nbsp;位顾客按从前到后依次排队，初始队列为&nbsp;s1,s2,…,sn<span style=""font-style: italic;"">s</span>1​,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">s</span>2​,…,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">s</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>​。随后发生&nbsp;m<span style=""font-style: italic;"">m</span>&nbsp;次插队事件。在第&nbsp;i<span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>&nbsp;次事件中，名为&nbsp;xi<span style=""font-style: italic;"">x</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>​&nbsp;的顾客会移动到名为&nbsp;yi<span style=""font-style: italic;"">y</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>​&nbsp;的顾客前面。<br><br>请你模拟所有插队事件，输出最终队列中顾客的排队顺序。<br></div><h3>输入描述：</h3><div>第一行输入两个整数&nbsp;n,m<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">m</span>，用空格隔开，表示顾客人数和插队事件次数，满足<br>&nbsp;2≦n≦2×105,1≦m≦2×1052≦<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>≦2×105,1≦<span style=""font-style: italic;"">m</span>≦2×105。<br>第二行输入&nbsp;n<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>&nbsp;个字符串&nbsp;s1,s2,…,sn<span style=""font-style: italic;"">s</span>1​,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">s</span>2​,…,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">s</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>​，用空格隔开，表示初始排队顺序。每个字符串长度&nbsp;1≦∣si∣≦101≦∣<span style=""font-style: italic;"">s</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>​∣≦10，仅由小写字母组成；所有字符串两两互不相同。<br><br>接下来&nbsp;m<span style=""font-style: italic;"">m</span>&nbsp;行，每行输入两个字符串&nbsp;xi,yi<span style=""font-style: italic;"">x</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>​,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">y</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>​，用空格隔开，表示第&nbsp;i<span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>&nbsp;次插队事件中，名为&nbsp;xi<span style=""font-style: italic;"">x</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>​&nbsp;的顾客插入到名为&nbsp;yi<span style=""font-style: italic;"">y</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>​&nbsp;的顾客前。保证&nbsp;xi,yi<span style=""font-style: italic;"">x</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>​,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">y</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>​&nbsp;均在初始队列中出现，且&nbsp;xi≠yi<span style=""font-style: italic;"">x</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>​​=<span style=""font-style: italic;"">y</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>​。<br></div><h3>输出描述：</h3><div>输出一行&nbsp;n<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>&nbsp;个字符串，用空格隔开，表示所有插队事件结束后队列中顾客的顺序。<br></div></div><div><h2>示例1</h2><div><div>输入：<pre>4 6
alpha bravo charlie delta
bravo alpha
charlie alpha
delta alpha
charlie bravo
delta bravo
charlie delta</pre>复制</div><div>输出：<pre>charlie delta bravo alpha</pre>复制</div><div>说明：<pre>初始队列：alpha bravo charlie delta <br>事件 1：bravo alpha charlie delta <br>事件 2：bravo charlie alpha delta <br>事件 3：bravo charlie delta alpha <br>事件 4：charlie bravo delta alpha <br>事件 5：charlie delta bravo alpha <br>事件 6：charlie delta bravo alpha</pre></div></div></div></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><br></pre></div>"	
"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><div><div>给定一个整数序列&nbsp;a=[a1,a2,…,an]<span style=""font-style: italic;"">a</span>=[<span style=""font-style: italic;"">a</span>1​,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">a</span>2​,…,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">a</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>​]&nbsp;和目标整数&nbsp;T<span style=""font-style: italic;"">T</span>，寻找一对下标&nbsp;(i,j)(<span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">j</span>)&nbsp;满足&nbsp;1≦i&lt;j≦n1≦<span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>&lt;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">j</span>≦<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>&nbsp;且&nbsp;ai+aj=T<span style=""font-style: italic;"">a</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>​+<span style=""font-style: italic;"">a</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">j</span>​=<span style=""font-style: italic;"">T</span>。<br>测试数据保证恰有一组解，你需要求出对应的下标对&nbsp;(i,j)(<span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">j</span>)&nbsp;作为序列并返回。<br><br>传入参数：<br>∙ ∙整数序列&nbsp;a<span style=""font-style: italic;"">a</span>，长度满足&nbsp;2≦n≦1052≦<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>≦105&nbsp;且&nbsp;0≦ai≦1090≦<span style=""font-style: italic;"">a</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>​≦109；<br><div>∙ ∙目标整数&nbsp;T<span style=""font-style: italic;"">T</span>，满足&nbsp;0≦T≦1090≦<span style=""font-style: italic;"">T</span>≦109。</div><div><br></div><div>返回值：<br>一对整数下标&nbsp;(i,j)(<span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">j</span>)&nbsp;构成的序列，满足&nbsp;ai+aj=T<span style=""font-style: italic;"">a</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>​+<span style=""font-style: italic;"">a</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">j</span>​=<span style=""font-style: italic;"">T</span>。<br></div></div></div><div><h2>示例1</h2><div><div>输入：<pre>[0,7,2,1],9</pre>复制</div><div>返回值：<pre>[2,3]</pre>复制</div><div>说明：<pre>a2+a3=7+2=9<span style=""font-style: italic;"">a</span>2​+<span style=""font-style: italic;"">a</span>3​=7+2=9。</pre></div></div></div></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#569CD6"">class</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Solution</span> {
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">/**
     * @param nums int整型vector 
     * @param target int整型 
     * @return int整型vector
     */</span>
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">twoSum</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&amp; nums, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> target) {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// key: 数值, value: 在原数组中的 1-based 下标</span>
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">unordered_map</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; mp;
        
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; i &lt; nums.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>(); i++) {
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> complement = target - nums[i];
            
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 如果在 map 中找到了需要的补数</span>
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (mp.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">find</span>(complement) != mp.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">end</span>()) {
                <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 返回之前的下标和当前下标 (都要 +1 转换成 1-based)</span>
                <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 题目要求 i &lt; j，mp[complement] 存储的是之前出现的，所以它一定更小</span>
                <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> {mp[complement], i + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>};
            }
            
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 存入当前数值及其 1-based 下标</span>
            mp[nums[i]] = i + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
        }
        
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> {}; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 理论上不会执行</span>
    }
};

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><div><div>现有&nbsp;N<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>&nbsp;篇文档，每篇文档由若干小写字母单词组成。记第&nbsp;i<span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>&nbsp;篇文档的单词集合为&nbsp;Si<span style=""font-style: italic;"">S</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>​。现给定&nbsp;M<span style=""font-style: italic;"">M</span>&nbsp;个查询单词&nbsp;w1,w2,…,wM<span style=""font-style: italic;"">w</span>1​,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">w</span>2​,…,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">w</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">M</span>​，请分别求出每个&nbsp;wj<span style=""font-style: italic;"">w</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>≦103)。<br><div>接下来&nbsp;N<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>&nbsp;行，第&nbsp;i<span style=""font-style: italic;"">L</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>​,&nbsp;∑<span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>=1<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>​<span style=""font-style: italic;"">L</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>​≦5×105)，随后给出&nbsp;Li<span style=""font-style: italic;"">L</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>​&nbsp;个由小写字母组成的单词，单词间以空格分隔。</div><div>接着一行一个整数&nbsp;M&nbsp;(&nbsp;1≦M≦104)<span style=""font-style: italic;"">M</span>&nbsp;(&nbsp;1≦<span style=""font-style: italic;"">M</span>≦104)。<br></div>随后&nbsp;M<span style=""font-style: italic;"">M</span>&nbsp;行，每行包含一个由小写字母组成的查询单词&nbsp;wj<span style=""font-style: italic;"">w</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">j</span>​。<br></div><h3>输出描述：</h3><div>对于每个查询单词&nbsp;wj<span style=""font-style: italic;"">w</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">j</span>​，输出一行，按升序列出所有满足&nbsp;wj∈Si<span style=""font-style: italic;"">w</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">j</span>​∈<span style=""font-style: italic;"">S</span><span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>​&nbsp;的文档编号&nbsp;i<span style=""font-style: italic;"">i</span>，编号间以空格分隔；若对应集合为空，则输出空行。<br></div></div><div><h2>示例1</h2><div><div>输入：<pre>3

3 a b a
2 x y
2
b
z</pre>复制</div><div>输出：<pre>1</pre></div></div></div></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;bits/stdc++.h&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n;cin&gt;&gt;n;

    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">map</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span>, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">set</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&gt; invertedIndex;

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;i&lt;=n;++i){
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Li</span>;
        cin&gt;&gt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Li</span>;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Li</span>--){
            <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> word;cin&gt;&gt;word;
            invertedIndex[word].<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">insert</span>(i);
        }
    }
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> m;
    cin&gt;&gt;m;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span>(m--){
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> query;cin&gt;&gt;query;

        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span>(invertedIndex.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">count</span>(query)){
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">set</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&amp; docIds = invertedIndex[query];
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">auto</span> it = docIds.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">begin</span>();it != docIds.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">end</span>();++it){
                cout&lt;&lt;(it == docIds.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">begin</span>() ? <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""""</span>:<span style=""color:#CE9178"">"" ""</span>)&lt;&lt;*it;
            }
        }
        cout&lt;&lt;endl;
    }
}
