"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><img src=""paste-51ef3869a13e7d4434a670c8f362c2d6cfab9056.jpg""><span style=""color:#C586C0""><br></span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><div><h2>描述</h2><div><div>您需要动态地维护一个初始为空的集合&nbsp;M<span style=""font-style: italic;"">M</span>，并且支持以下操作：</div><div><br></div>∙ ∙操作&nbsp;11：向集合&nbsp;M<span style=""font-style: italic;"">M</span>&nbsp;中插入一个数&nbsp;x<span style=""font-style: italic;"">x</span>，如果&nbsp;x<span style=""font-style: italic;"">x</span>&nbsp;在集合&nbsp;M<span style=""font-style: italic;"">M</span>&nbsp;中已经存在，则忽略本次操作。<br>∙ ∙操作&nbsp;22：从集合&nbsp;M<span style=""font-style: italic;"">M</span>&nbsp;中删除一个数&nbsp;x<span style=""font-style: italic;"">x</span>，如果&nbsp;x<span style=""font-style: italic;"">x</span>&nbsp;不在集合&nbsp;M<span style=""font-style: italic;"">M</span>&nbsp;中，则忽略本次操作。<br>∙ ∙操作&nbsp;33：查询一个数&nbsp;x<span style=""font-style: italic;"">x</span>&nbsp;是否在集合&nbsp;M<span style=""font-style: italic;"">M</span>&nbsp;中。如果存在，输出&nbsp;YESYES；否则输出&nbsp;NONO。<br>∙ ∙操作&nbsp;44：查询集合&nbsp;M<span style=""font-style: italic;"">M</span>&nbsp;中元素的个数，即集合&nbsp;M<span style=""font-style: italic;"">M</span>&nbsp;的大小。<br>∙ ∙操作&nbsp;55：查询集合&nbsp;M<span style=""font-style: italic;"">M</span>&nbsp;中&nbsp;x<span style=""font-style: italic;"">x</span>&nbsp;的前驱（前驱定义为小于&nbsp;x<span style=""font-style: italic;"">x</span>&nbsp;且最大的数），如果前驱不存在，则输出&nbsp;−1−1。<br>∙ ∙操作&nbsp;66：查询集合&nbsp;M<span style=""font-style: italic;"">M</span>&nbsp;中&nbsp;x<span style=""font-style: italic;"">x</span>&nbsp;的后继（后继定义为大于&nbsp;x<span style=""font-style: italic;"">x</span>&nbsp;且最小的数），如果后继不存在，则输出&nbsp;−1−1。<br></div><h3>输入描述：</h3><div>第一行输入一个整数&nbsp;n<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>（1≦n≦1051≦<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>≦105），表示操作的个数。<br>接下来&nbsp;n<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>&nbsp;行，每行表示一次操作。对于操作&nbsp;1、2、3、5、61、2、3、5、6，输入两个整数&nbsp;optopt&nbsp;和&nbsp;x<span style=""font-style: italic;"">x</span>（1≦opt≦61≦opt≦6，0≦x≦1060≦<span style=""font-style: italic;"">x</span>≦106），分别表示操作类型和操作的参数；对于操作&nbsp;44，输入两个整数&nbsp;optopt&nbsp;，表示操作类型。<br></div><h3>输出描述：</h3><div>对于操作类型为&nbsp;3、4、5、63、4、5、6&nbsp;的每次操作，按照题意输出对应的查询结果，每个结果占一行。<br></div></div><div><h2>示例1</h2><div><div>输入：<pre>4
1 4
4
2 4
3 4</pre>复制</div><div>输出：<pre>1
NO</pre>复制</div><div>说明：<pre><div>第一步插入操作向集合 M<span style=""font-style: italic;"">M</span> 中插入了元素 44；</div><div>第二步查询操作类型为 44，查询集合大小，当前集合中只有元素 44，大小为 11，因此输出 11；</div><div>第三步删除了集合&nbsp;M<span style=""font-style: italic;"">M</span>&nbsp;中的元素&nbsp;44；</div><div>第四步查询元素&nbsp;44&nbsp;是否在集合&nbsp;M<span style=""font-style: italic;"">M</span>&nbsp;中，不在，故输出&nbsp;NONO。</div></pre></div></div></div><div><h2>示例2</h2><div><div>输入：<pre>5
1 5
1 10
1 20
5 15
6 15</pre>复制</div><div>输出：<pre>10
20</pre>复制</div><div>说明：<pre><div>前三步插入操作使集合 M={5,10,20}<span style=""font-style: italic;"">M</span>={5,10,20}；</div><div>第四步操作类型为 55，查询前驱，数字 1515 在集合中前驱为 1010，输出 1010；</div><div>第五步操作类型为 66，查询后继，数字 1515 在集合中后继为 2020，输出 2020。</div></pre></div></div></div></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include</span>&lt;bits/stdc++.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">h</span>&gt;
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">set</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">M</span>;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">insertValue</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> x){
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">M</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">insert</span>(x); <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// set 自动处理重复元素</span>
}

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">eraseValue</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> x){
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">M</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">erase</span>(x); <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 如果不存在则不执行任何操作</span>
}

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">xInSet</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> x){
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">M</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">count</span>(x); <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 返回 1 表示存在，0 表示不存在</span>
}

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">sizeOfSet</span>(){
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">M</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>();
}

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">getPre</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> x){
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">auto</span> it = <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">M</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">lower_bound</span>(x); <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 找到第一个 &gt;= x 的位置</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (it == <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">M</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">begin</span>()) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> -<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 没有比它小的数</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> *(--it); <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 向前移动一位即为前驱</span>
}

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">getBack</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> x){
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">auto</span> it = <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">M</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">upper_bound</span>(x); <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 找到第一个 &gt; x 的位置</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (it == <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">M</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">end</span>()) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> -<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 没有比它大的数</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> *it;
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// main 函数保持不变即可运行</span></pre>
        </div>
        <br>"	
"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><div><div>Farmer John 有若干头奶牛。为了训练奶牛们的智力，他在谷仓的墙上放了一张美国地图。地图上标明了每个城市及其所在州的代码（前两位大写字母）。<br><br>奶牛们注意到，如果城市&nbsp;A<span style=""font-style: italic;"">A</span>&nbsp;的名称前两位字母等于城市&nbsp;B<span style=""font-style: italic;"">B</span>&nbsp;所在州代码，且城市&nbsp;B<span style=""font-style: italic;"">B</span>&nbsp;的名称前两位字母等于城市&nbsp;A<span style=""font-style: italic;"">A</span>&nbsp;所在州代码，并且&nbsp;A,B<span style=""font-style: italic;"">A</span>,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">B</span>&nbsp;来自不同的州，则称&nbsp;{A,B}{<span style=""font-style: italic;"">A</span>,<span style=""font-style: italic;"">B</span>}&nbsp;是一对<u>特殊</u>城市。<br><br>现有&nbsp;N<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>&nbsp;座城市，请你计算共有多少对特殊城市。<br></div><h3>输入描述：</h3><div>第一行输入一个整数&nbsp;N<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>（1≦N≦2×1051≦<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>≦2×105），表示城市数量。<br><br>接下来&nbsp;N<span style=""font-style: italic;"">N</span>&nbsp;行，每行输入两个字符串：城市名称&nbsp;S<span style=""font-style: italic;"">S</span>（由&nbsp;2∼102∼10&nbsp;个大写字母组成）和所在州代码&nbsp;C<span style=""font-style: italic;"">C</span>（由&nbsp;22&nbsp;个大写字母组成），用空格隔开。保证同一州内城市名称互不相同。<br></div><h3>输出描述：</h3><div>输出一个整数，表示特殊城市对的数量。<br></div></div><div><h2>示例1</h2><div><div>输入：<pre>6
MIAMI FL
DALLAS TX
FLINT MI
CLEMSON SC
BOSTON MA
ORLANDO FL</pre>复制</div><div>输出：<pre>1</pre>复制</div><div>说明：<pre>MIAMI 位于州 FL，且 FLINT 的名称前两位字母为 FL；FLINT 位于州 MI，且 MIAMI 的名称前两位字母为 MI。其他城市不满足此条件，因此共有 1 对特殊城市。</pre></div></div></div></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;string&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;map&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    ios::<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">sync_with_stdio</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">false</span>);
    cin.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">tie</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>);

    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n;
    cin &gt;&gt; n;

    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">map</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span>, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; counts;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> ans = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; i &lt; n; ++i) {
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> cityName, stateCode;
        cin &gt;&gt; cityName &gt;&gt; stateCode;
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> cityCode = cityName.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">substr</span>(<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>);

        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 核心：只有当城市前两位和州代码不同时，才可能和“不同州”的城市配对</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (cityCode != stateCode) {
            <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> target = stateCode + cityCode;
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (counts.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">count</span>(target)) {
                ans += counts[target];
            }
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 记录当前组合</span>
            counts[cityCode + stateCode]++;
        }
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 如果 cityCode == stateCode，它永远无法满足“不同州”的配对要求，直接无视即可</span>
    }

    cout &lt;&lt; ans &lt;&lt; endl;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>
        </div>
        <br>"	
"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 110 线段树</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 线段树维护区间增加、区间查询累加和 (add, query)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 懒更新信息下发与汇总 (down, up)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 懒更新任务具体执行 (lazy)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 4. 递归建树 (build)</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;cstdio&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> class110 {

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">class</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Code01_SegmentTreeAddQuerySum</span> {
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">static</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span> = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">100005</span>;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> arr[<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span>];
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> sum[<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span> &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>];
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> add_tag[<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span> &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>];

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 建树</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// l~r 是当前节点管辖范围，i 是数组下标</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> r, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i) {
        add_tag[i] = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (l == r) {
            sum[i] = arr[l];
        } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> mid = (l + r) &gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>(l, mid, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>(mid + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, r, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">up</span>(i);
        }
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 范围修改</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// jobl ~ jobr 范围上每个数字增加 jobv</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">add</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobl, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobr, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> jobv, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> r, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobl &lt;= l &amp;&amp; r &lt;= jobr) {
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">lazy</span>(i, jobv, r - l + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> mid = (l + r) &gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">down</span>(i, mid - l + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, r - mid);
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobl &lt;= mid) {
                <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">add</span>(jobl, jobr, jobv, l, mid, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
            }
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobr &gt; mid) {
                <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">add</span>(jobl, jobr, jobv, mid + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, r, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
            }
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">up</span>(i);
        }
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 查询累加和</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// jobl ~ jobr 范围上的数字总和</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">query</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobl, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobr, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> r, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobl &lt;= l &amp;&amp; r &lt;= jobr) {
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> sum[i];
        }
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> mid = (l + r) &gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">down</span>(i, mid - l + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, r - mid);
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> ans = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobl &lt;= mid) {
            ans += <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">query</span>(jobl, jobr, l, mid, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        }
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobr &gt; mid) {
            ans += <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">query</span>(jobl, jobr, mid + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, r, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        }
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> ans;
    }

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">private</span>:
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 4. 累加和信息的汇总</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">up</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i) {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 父范围的累加和 = 左范围累加和 + 右范围累加和</span>
        sum[i] = sum[i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>] + sum[i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>];
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 5. 懒信息的下发</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">down</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> ln, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> rn) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (add_tag[i] != <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>) {
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 发左</span>
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">lazy</span>(i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, add_tag[i], ln);
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 发右</span>
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">lazy</span>(i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, add_tag[i], rn);
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 父范围懒信息清空</span>
            add_tag[i] = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
        }
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 6. 懒更新任务的具体执行</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 把线段树当前范围的 sum 数组和 add 数组调整好，不再继续往下发</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">lazy</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> v, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n) {
        sum[i] += v * n;
        add_tag[i] += v;
    }
};

} <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// namespace class110</span>

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 实例化线段树（静态全局分配空间，防止栈溢出）</span>
class110::<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Code01_SegmentTreeAddQuerySum</span> st;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n, m;
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 使用高效的 scanf 处理输入，对标 Java 的 StreamTokenizer</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">scanf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""%d %d""</span>, &amp;n, &amp;m) != <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">EOF</span>) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &lt;= n; i++) {
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">scanf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""%lld""</span>, &amp;st.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">arr</span>[i]);
        }
        
        st.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">build</span>(<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, n, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> op, l, r;
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> v;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; i &lt; m; i++) {
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">scanf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""%d""</span>, &amp;op);
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (op == <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>) {
                <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">scanf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""%d %d %lld""</span>, &amp;l, &amp;r, &amp;v);
                st.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">add</span>(l, r, v, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, n, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
            } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
                <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">scanf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""%d %d""</span>, &amp;l, &amp;r);
                <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""%lld\n""</span>, st.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">query</span>(l, r, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, n, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>));
            }
        }
    }
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 110 线段树支持范围增加、范围查询</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 累加和信息的汇总 (up)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 懒信息的下发 (down)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 懒更新任务的具体执行 (lazy)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 4. 建树 (build)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 5. 范围修改 (add)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 6. 查询累加和 (query)</span>

<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;cstdio&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;algorithm&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 使用常数定义最大范围</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span> = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">100005</span>;

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 全局静态数组，long long 处理，防止溢出</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> arr[<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span>];
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> sum_tree[<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span> &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>];
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> add_tag[<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span> &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>];

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 累加和信息的汇总</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">up</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i) {
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 父范围的累加和 = 左范围累加和 + 右范围累加和</span>
    sum_tree[i] = sum_tree[i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>] + sum_tree[i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>];
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 懒更新任务的具体执行</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 把线段树当前范围的 sum 数组和 add 数组调整好</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">lazy</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> v, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n) {
    sum_tree[i] += v * n;
    add_tag[i] += v;
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 懒信息的下发</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">down</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> ln, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> rn) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (add_tag[i] != <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>) {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 发左</span>
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">lazy</span>(i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, add_tag[i], ln);
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 发右</span>
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">lazy</span>(i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, add_tag[i], rn);
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 父范围懒信息清空</span>
        add_tag[i] = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    }
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 4. 建树</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> r, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i) {
    add_tag[i] = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (l == r) {
        sum_tree[i] = arr[l];
    } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> mid = (l + r) &gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>(l, mid, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>(mid + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, r, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">up</span>(i);
    }
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 5. 范围修改</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// jobl ~ jobr 范围上每个数字增加 jobv</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">add</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobl, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobr, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> jobv, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> r, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobl &lt;= l &amp;&amp; r &lt;= jobr) {
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">lazy</span>(i, jobv, r - l + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
    } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> mid = (l + r) &gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">down</span>(i, mid - l + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, r - mid);
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobl &lt;= mid) {
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">add</span>(jobl, jobr, jobv, l, mid, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        }
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobr &gt; mid) {
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">add</span>(jobl, jobr, jobv, mid + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, r, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        }
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">up</span>(i);
    }
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 6. 查询累加和</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">query</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobl, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobr, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> r, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobl &lt;= l &amp;&amp; r &lt;= jobr) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> sum_tree[i];
    }
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> mid = (l + r) &gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">down</span>(i, mid - l + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, r - mid);
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> ans = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobl &lt;= mid) {
        ans += <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">query</span>(jobl, jobr, l, mid, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
    }
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobr &gt; mid) {
        ans += <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">query</span>(jobl, jobr, mid + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, r, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
    }
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> ans;
}

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n, m;
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 使用 scanf 提升大量数据的输入效率</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">scanf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""%d %d""</span>, &amp;n, &amp;m) != <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">EOF</span>) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &lt;= n; i++) {
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">scanf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""%lld""</span>, &amp;arr[i]);
        }
        
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>(<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, n, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> op, jobl, jobr;
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> jobv;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &lt;= m; i++) {
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">scanf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""%d""</span>, &amp;op);
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (op == <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>) {
                <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">scanf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""%d %d %lld""</span>, &amp;jobl, &amp;jobr, &amp;jobv);
                <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">add</span>(jobl, jobr, jobv, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, n, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
            } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
                <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">scanf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""%d %d""</span>, &amp;jobl, &amp;jobr);
                <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""%lld\n""</span>, <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">query</span>(jobl, jobr, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, n, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>));
            }
        }
    }
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
