"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 110 线段树支持范围重置、范围查询</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 累加和信息的汇总 (up)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 懒信息的下发 (down)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 懒更新任务的具体执行 (lazy)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 4. 建树 (build)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 5. 范围重置 (update)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 6. 查询累加和 (query)</span>

<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;algorithm&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;cstdio&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 基础常量定义</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span> = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">100005</span>;

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 全局静态数组，防止栈溢出</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> arr[<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span>];
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> sum_tree[<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span> &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>];
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> change[<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span> &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>];
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">bool</span> update_tag[<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span> &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>];

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 累加和信息的汇总</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">up</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i) {
    sum_tree[i] = sum_tree[i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>] + sum_tree[i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>];
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 懒更新任务的具体执行</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 范围重置操作：当前范围所有数字变为 v</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">lazy</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> v, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n) {
    sum_tree[i] = v * n;
    change[i] = v;
    update_tag[i] = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">true</span>;
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 懒信息的下发</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">down</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> ln, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> rn) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (update_tag[i]) {
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">lazy</span>(i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, change[i], ln);
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">lazy</span>(i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, change[i], rn);
        update_tag[i] = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">false</span>;
    }
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 4. 建树</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> r, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (l == r) {
        sum_tree[i] = arr[l];
    } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> mid = (l + r) &gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>(l, mid, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>(mid + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, r, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">up</span>(i);
    }
    change[i] = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    update_tag[i] = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">false</span>;
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 5. 范围重置</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// jobl ~ jobr 范围上每个数字重置为 jobv</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">update</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobl, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobr, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> jobv, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> r, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobl &lt;= l &amp;&amp; r &lt;= jobr) {
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">lazy</span>(i, jobv, r - l + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
    } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> mid = (l + r) &gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">down</span>(i, mid - l + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, r - mid);
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobl &lt;= mid) {
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">update</span>(jobl, jobr, jobv, l, mid, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        }
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobr &gt; mid) {
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">update</span>(jobl, jobr, jobv, mid + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, r, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        }
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">up</span>(i);
    }
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 6. 查询累加和</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">query</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobl, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobr, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> r, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobl &lt;= l &amp;&amp; r &lt;= jobr) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> sum_tree[i];
    }
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> mid = (l + r) &gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">down</span>(i, mid - l + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, r - mid);
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> ans = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobl &lt;= mid) {
        ans += <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">query</span>(jobl, jobr, l, mid, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
    }
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobr &gt; mid) {
        ans += <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">query</span>(jobl, jobr, mid + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, r, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
    }
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> ans;
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 对数器使用的暴力验证逻辑</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">checkUpdate</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span>&gt;&amp; check, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobl, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobr, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> jobv) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = jobl; i &lt;= jobr; i++) {
        check[i] = jobv;
    }
}

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">checkQuery</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span>&gt;&amp; check, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobl, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobr) {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> ans = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = jobl; i &lt;= jobr; i++) {
        ans += check[i];
    }
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> ans;
}

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 模拟对数器验证</span>
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""测试开始\n""</span>);
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1000</span>;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> v = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2000</span>;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> t = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1000000</span>;
    
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 初始化随机数组</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &lt;= n; i++) {
        arr[i] = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">rand</span>() % v;
    }
    
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>(<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, n, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
    
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span>&gt; <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">check</span>(n + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &lt;= n; i++) {
        check[i] = arr[i];
    }
    
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &lt;= t; i++) {
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> op = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">rand</span>() % <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>;
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> a = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">rand</span>() % n + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> b = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">rand</span>() % n + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobl = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">min</span>(a, b);
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobr = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">max</span>(a, b);
        
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (op == <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>) {
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> jobv = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">rand</span>() % (v * <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>) - v;
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">update</span>(jobl, jobr, jobv, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, n, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">checkUpdate</span>(check, jobl, jobr, jobv);
        } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> ans1 = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">query</span>(jobl, jobr, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, n, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> ans2 = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">checkQuery</span>(check, jobl, jobr);
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (ans1 != ans2) {
                <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""出错了!\n""</span>);
                <span style=""color:#C586C0"">break</span>;
            }
        }
    }
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""测试结束\n""</span>);
    
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>
        </div>
        <br>"	
"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 110 Code03 线段树支持范围增加、范围查询最大值</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 最大值信息的汇总 (up)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 懒信息的下发 (down)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 懒更新任务的具体执行 (lazy)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 4. 建树 (build)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 5. 范围增加 (add)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 6. 查询最大值 (query)</span>

<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;algorithm&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;cstdio&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;climits&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;ctime&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 基础常量定义</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span> = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">100005</span>;

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 全局静态数组，long long 处理，防止溢出</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> arr[<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span>];
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> max_tree[<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span> &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>];
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> add_tag[<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span> &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>];

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 最大值信息的汇总</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">up</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i) {
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 父范围的最大值 = max(左子范围最大值, 右子范围最大值)</span>
    max_tree[i] = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">max</span>(max_tree[i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>], max_tree[i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>]);
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 懒更新任务的具体执行</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 范围增加操作：当前范围所有数字增加 v</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">lazy</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> v) {
    max_tree[i] += v;
    add_tag[i] += v;
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 懒信息的下发</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">down</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (add_tag[i] != <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>) {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 向左孩子发懒信息</span>
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">lazy</span>(i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, add_tag[i]);
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 向右孩子发懒信息</span>
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">lazy</span>(i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, add_tag[i]);
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 父范围懒信息清空</span>
        add_tag[i] = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    }
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 4. 建树</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> r, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (l == r) {
        max_tree[i] = arr[l];
    } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> mid = (l + r) &gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>(l, mid, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>(mid + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, r, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">up</span>(i);
    }
    add_tag[i] = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 5. 范围增加</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// jobl ~ jobr 范围上每个数字增加 jobv</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">add</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobl, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobr, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> jobv, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> r, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobl &lt;= l &amp;&amp; r &lt;= jobr) {
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">lazy</span>(i, jobv);
    } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">down</span>(i);
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> mid = (l + r) &gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobl &lt;= mid) {
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">add</span>(jobl, jobr, jobv, l, mid, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        }
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobr &gt; mid) {
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">add</span>(jobl, jobr, jobv, mid + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, r, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        }
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">up</span>(i);
    }
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 6. 查询最大值</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 查询 jobl ~ jobr 范围内的最大值</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">query</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobl, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobr, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> r, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobl &lt;= l &amp;&amp; r &lt;= jobr) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> max_tree[i];
    }
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">down</span>(i);
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> mid = (l + r) &gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> ans = <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">LLONG_MIN</span>;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobl &lt;= mid) {
        ans = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">max</span>(ans, <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">query</span>(jobl, jobr, l, mid, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>));
    }
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobr &gt; mid) {
        ans = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">max</span>(ans, <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">query</span>(jobl, jobr, mid + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, r, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>));
    }
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> ans;
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 验证结构的增加（暴力）</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">checkAdd</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span>&gt;&amp; check, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobl, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobr, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> jobv) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = jobl; i &lt;= jobr; i++) {
        check[i] += jobv;
    }
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 验证结构的查询（暴力）</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">checkQuery</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span>&gt;&amp; check, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobl, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobr) {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> ans = <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">LLONG_MIN</span>;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = jobl; i &lt;= jobr; i++) {
        ans = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">max</span>(ans, check[i]);
    }
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> ans;
}

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">srand</span>(<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">time</span>(<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>));
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""测试开始\n""</span>);
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1000</span>;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> v = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2000</span>;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> t = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1000000</span>;
    
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 初始化随机数组</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &lt;= n; i++) {
        arr[i] = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">rand</span>() % v;
    }
    
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 建立线段树</span>
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>(<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, n, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
    
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 建立对数器验证结构</span>
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span>&gt; <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">check</span>(n + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &lt;= n; i++) {
        check[i] = arr[i];
    }
    
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &lt;= t; i++) {
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> op = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">rand</span>() % <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>;
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> a = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">rand</span>() % n + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> b = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">rand</span>() % n + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobl = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">min</span>(a, b);
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobr = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">max</span>(a, b);
        
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (op == <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>) {
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> jobv = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">rand</span>() % (v * <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>) - v;
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">add</span>(jobl, jobr, jobv, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, n, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">checkAdd</span>(check, jobl, jobr, jobv);
        } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> ans1 = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">query</span>(jobl, jobr, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, n, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> ans2 = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">checkQuery</span>(check, jobl, jobr);
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (ans1 != ans2) {
                <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""出错了!\n""</span>);
                <span style=""color:#C586C0"">break</span>;
            }
        }
    }
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""测试结束\n""</span>);
    
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>
        </div>
        <br>"	
"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 110 Code04 线段树支持范围重置、范围查询最大值</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 最大值信息的汇总 (up)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 懒信息的下发 (down)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 懒更新任务的具体执行 (lazy)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 4. 建树 (build)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 5. 范围重置 (update)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 6. 查询最大值 (query)</span>

<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;algorithm&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;cstdio&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;climits&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;ctime&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 基础常量定义</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span> = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">100005</span>;

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 全局静态数组，防止栈溢出</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> arr[<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span>];
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> max_tree[<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span> &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>];
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> change[<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span> &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>];
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">bool</span> update_tag[<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span> &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>];

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 最大值信息的汇总</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">up</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i) {
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 父范围的最大值 = max(左孩子最大值, 右孩子最大值)</span>
    max_tree[i] = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">max</span>(max_tree[i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>], max_tree[i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>]);
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 懒更新任务的具体执行</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 范围重置操作：当前范围所有数字重置为 v</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">lazy</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> v) {
    max_tree[i] = v;
    change[i] = v;
    update_tag[i] = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">true</span>;
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 懒信息的下发</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">down</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (update_tag[i]) {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 向左孩子发懒信息</span>
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">lazy</span>(i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, change[i]);
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 向右孩子发懒信息</span>
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">lazy</span>(i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, change[i]);
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 标记重置</span>
        update_tag[i] = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">false</span>;
    }
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 4. 建树</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> r, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (l == r) {
        max_tree[i] = arr[l];
    } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> mid = (l + r) &gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>(l, mid, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>(mid + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, r, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">up</span>(i);
    }
    change[i] = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    update_tag[i] = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">false</span>;
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 5. 范围重置</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// jobl ~ jobr 范围上每个数字重置为 jobv</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">update</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobl, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobr, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> jobv, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> r, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobl &lt;= l &amp;&amp; r &lt;= jobr) {
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">lazy</span>(i, jobv);
    } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">down</span>(i);
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> mid = (l + r) &gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobl &lt;= mid) {
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">update</span>(jobl, jobr, jobv, l, mid, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        }
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobr &gt; mid) {
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">update</span>(jobl, jobr, jobv, mid + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, r, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        }
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">up</span>(i);
    }
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 6. 查询最大值</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 查询 jobl ~ jobr 范围内的最大值</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">query</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobl, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobr, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> r, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobl &lt;= l &amp;&amp; r &lt;= jobr) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> max_tree[i];
    }
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">down</span>(i);
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> mid = (l + r) &gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> ans = <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">LLONG_MIN</span>;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobl &lt;= mid) {
        ans = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">max</span>(ans, <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">query</span>(jobl, jobr, l, mid, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>));
    }
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobr &gt; mid) {
        ans = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">max</span>(ans, <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">query</span>(jobl, jobr, mid + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, r, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>));
    }
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> ans;
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 验证结构的更新（对数器暴力逻辑）</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">checkUpdate</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span>&gt;&amp; check, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobl, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobr, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> jobv) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = jobl; i &lt;= jobr; i++) {
        check[i] = jobv;
    }
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 验证结构的查询（对数器暴力逻辑）</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">checkQuery</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span>&gt;&amp; check, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobl, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobr) {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> ans = <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">LLONG_MIN</span>;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = jobl; i &lt;= jobr; i++) {
        ans = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">max</span>(ans, check[i]);
    }
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> ans;
}

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">srand</span>(<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">time</span>(<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>));
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""测试开始\n""</span>);
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1000</span>;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> v = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2000</span>;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> t = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1000000</span>;
    
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 生成随机数组</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &lt;= n; i++) {
        arr[i] = (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span>)(<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">rand</span>() % v);
    }
    
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 建立线段树</span>
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>(<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, n, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
    
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 建立验证数组</span>
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span>&gt; <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">check</span>(n + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &lt;= n; i++) {
        check[i] = arr[i];
    }
    
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &lt;= t; i++) {
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> op = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">rand</span>() % <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>;
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> a = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">rand</span>() % n + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> b = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">rand</span>() % n + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobl = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">min</span>(a, b);
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobr = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">max</span>(a, b);
        
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (op == <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>) {
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> jobv = (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span>)(<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">rand</span>() % (v * <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>) - v);
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">update</span>(jobl, jobr, jobv, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, n, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">checkUpdate</span>(check, jobl, jobr, jobv);
        } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> ans1 = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">query</span>(jobl, jobr, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, n, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> ans2 = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">checkQuery</span>(check, jobl, jobr);
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (ans1 != ans2) {
                <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""出错了!\n""</span>);
                <span style=""color:#C586C0"">break</span>;
            }
        }
    }
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""测试结束\n""</span>);
    
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>
        </div>
        <br>"	
"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 110 Code05 线段树同时支持范围重置、范围增加、范围查询</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 累加和信息的汇总 (up)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 懒信息的下发 (down)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 范围重置懒更新任务执行 (updateLazy)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 4. 范围增加懒更新任务执行 (addLazy)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 5. 建树 (build)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 6. 范围重置修改 (update)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 7. 范围增加修改 (add)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 8. 范围查询累加和 (query)</span>

<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;algorithm&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;cstdio&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;ctime&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 基础常量定义</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span> = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1000001</span>;

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 全局静态数组，防止栈溢出</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> arr[<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span>];
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> sum_tree[<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span> &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>];
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> add_tag[<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span> &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>];
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> change_tag[<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span> &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>];
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">bool</span> update_tag[<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span> &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>];

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 累加和信息的汇总</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">up</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i) {
    sum_tree[i] = sum_tree[i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>] + sum_tree[i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>];
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 范围重置懒更新任务执行</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 重置操作优先级高于增加操作，一旦重置，之前的增加标记清空</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">updateLazy</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> v, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n) {
    sum_tree[i] = v * n;
    change_tag[i] = v;
    add_tag[i] = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 关键：重置后之前的增加标记失效</span>
    update_tag[i] = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">true</span>;
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 4. 范围增加懒更新任务执行</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">addLazy</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> v, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n) {
    sum_tree[i] += v * n;
    add_tag[i] += v;
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 懒信息的下发</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 先发重置标记，再发增加标记</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">down</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> ln, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> rn) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (update_tag[i]) {
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">updateLazy</span>(i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, change_tag[i], ln);
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">updateLazy</span>(i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, change_tag[i], rn);
        update_tag[i] = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">false</span>;
    }
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (add_tag[i] != <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>) {
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">addLazy</span>(i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, add_tag[i], ln);
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">addLazy</span>(i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, add_tag[i], rn);
        add_tag[i] = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    }
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 5. 建树</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> r, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (l == r) {
        sum_tree[i] = arr[l];
    } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> mid = (l + r) &gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>(l, mid, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>(mid + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, r, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">up</span>(i);
    }
    add_tag[i] = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    change_tag[i] = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    update_tag[i] = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">false</span>;
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 6. 范围重置修改</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">update</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobl, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobr, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> jobv, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> r, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobl &lt;= l &amp;&amp; r &lt;= jobr) {
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">updateLazy</span>(i, jobv, r - l + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
    } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> mid = (l + r) &gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">down</span>(i, mid - l + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, r - mid);
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobl &lt;= mid) {
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">update</span>(jobl, jobr, jobv, l, mid, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        }
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobr &gt; mid) {
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">update</span>(jobl, jobr, jobv, mid + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, r, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        }
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">up</span>(i);
    }
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 7. 范围增加修改</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">add</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobl, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobr, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> jobv, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> r, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobl &lt;= l &amp;&amp; r &lt;= jobr) {
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">addLazy</span>(i, jobv, r - l + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
    } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> mid = (l + r) &gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">down</span>(i, mid - l + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, r - mid);
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobl &lt;= mid) {
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">add</span>(jobl, jobr, jobv, l, mid, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        }
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobr &gt; mid) {
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">add</span>(jobl, jobr, jobv, mid + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, r, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        }
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">up</span>(i);
    }
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 8. 范围查询累加和</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">query</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobl, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobr, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> r, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobl &lt;= l &amp;&amp; r &lt;= jobr) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> sum_tree[i];
    }
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> mid = (l + r) &gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">down</span>(i, mid - l + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, r - mid);
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> ans = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobl &lt;= mid) {
        ans += <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">query</span>(jobl, jobr, l, mid, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
    }
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobr &gt; mid) {
        ans += <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">query</span>(jobl, jobr, mid + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, r, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
    }
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> ans;
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 对数器暴力验证逻辑</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">checkAdd</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span>&gt;&amp; check, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobl, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobr, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> jobv) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = jobl; i &lt;= jobr; i++) check[i] += jobv;
}

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">checkUpdate</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span>&gt;&amp; check, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobl, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobr, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> jobv) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = jobl; i &lt;= jobr; i++) check[i] = jobv;
}

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">checkQuery</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span>&gt;&amp; check, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobl, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobr) {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> ans = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = jobl; i &lt;= jobr; i++) ans += check[i];
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> ans;
}

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">srand</span>(<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">time</span>(<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>));
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""测试开始\n""</span>);
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1000</span>;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> v = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2000</span>;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> t = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1000000</span>;
    
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &lt;= n; i++) arr[i] = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">rand</span>() % v;
    
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>(<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, n, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
    
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span>&gt; <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">check</span>(n + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &lt;= n; i++) check[i] = arr[i];
    
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &lt;= t; i++) {
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> op = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">rand</span>() % <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">3</span>;
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> a = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">rand</span>() % n + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, b = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">rand</span>() % n + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobl = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">min</span>(a, b), jobr = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">max</span>(a, b);
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> jobv = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">rand</span>() % (v * <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>) - v;
        
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (op == <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>) {
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">add</span>(jobl, jobr, jobv, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, n, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">checkAdd</span>(check, jobl, jobr, jobv);
        } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (op == <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>) {
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">update</span>(jobl, jobr, jobv, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, n, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">checkUpdate</span>(check, jobl, jobr, jobv);
        } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">query</span>(jobl, jobr, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, n, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>) != <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">checkQuery</span>(check, jobl, jobr)) {
                <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""出错了!\n""</span>);
                <span style=""color:#C586C0"">break</span>;
            }
        }
    }
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""测试结束\n""</span>);
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>
        </div>
        <br>"	
"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 110 Code06 线段树同时支持范围重置、范围增加、范围查询最大值</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 最大值信息的汇总 (up)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 懒信息的下发 (down)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 范围重置懒更新任务执行 (updateLazy)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 4. 范围增加懒更新任务执行 (addLazy)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 5. 建树 (build)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 6. 范围重置修改 (update)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 7. 范围增加修改 (add)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 8. 范围查询最大值 (query)</span>

<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;cstdio&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;algorithm&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;climits&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 基础常量定义，MAXN 为 1,000,001</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span> = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1000001</span>;

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 全局静态数组，long long 处理，防止溢出</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> arr[<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span>];
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> max_tree[<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span> &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>];
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> add_tag[<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span> &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>];
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> change_tag[<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span> &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>];
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">bool</span> update_tag[<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span> &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>];

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 最大值信息的汇总</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">up</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i) {
    max_tree[i] = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">max</span>(max_tree[i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>], max_tree[i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>]);
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 范围重置懒更新任务执行</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 优先级：重置操作会覆盖掉之前的增加操作</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">updateLazy</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> v) {
    max_tree[i] = v;
    add_tag[i] = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    change_tag[i] = v;
    update_tag[i] = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">true</span>;
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 4. 范围增加懒更新任务执行</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">addLazy</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> v) {
    max_tree[i] += v;
    add_tag[i] += v;
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 懒信息的下发</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 遵循先处理重置(Update)，再处理增加(Add)的原则</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">down</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (update_tag[i]) {
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">updateLazy</span>(i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, change_tag[i]);
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">updateLazy</span>(i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, change_tag[i]);
        update_tag[i] = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">false</span>;
    }
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (add_tag[i] != <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>) {
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">addLazy</span>(i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, add_tag[i]);
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">addLazy</span>(i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, add_tag[i]);
        add_tag[i] = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    }
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 5. 建树</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> r, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (l == r) {
        max_tree[i] = arr[l];
    } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> mid = (l + r) &gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>(l, mid, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>(mid + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, r, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">up</span>(i);
    }
    add_tag[i] = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    change_tag[i] = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    update_tag[i] = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">false</span>;
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 6. 范围重置修改</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">update</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobl, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobr, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> jobv, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> r, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobl &lt;= l &amp;&amp; r &lt;= jobr) {
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">updateLazy</span>(i, jobv);
    } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> mid = (l + r) &gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">down</span>(i);
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobl &lt;= mid) {
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">update</span>(jobl, jobr, jobv, l, mid, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        }
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobr &gt; mid) {
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">update</span>(jobl, jobr, jobv, mid + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, r, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        }
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">up</span>(i);
    }
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 7. 范围增加修改</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">add</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobl, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobr, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> jobv, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> r, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobl &lt;= l &amp;&amp; r &lt;= jobr) {
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">addLazy</span>(i, jobv);
    } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> mid = (l + r) &gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">down</span>(i);
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobl &lt;= mid) {
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">add</span>(jobl, jobr, jobv, l, mid, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        }
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobr &gt; mid) {
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">add</span>(jobl, jobr, jobv, mid + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, r, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        }
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">up</span>(i);
    }
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 8. 范围查询最大值</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">query</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobl, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> jobr, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> r, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobl &lt;= l &amp;&amp; r &lt;= jobr) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> max_tree[i];
    }
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> mid = (l + r) &gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">down</span>(i);
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> ans = <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">LLONG_MIN</span>;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobl &lt;= mid) {
        ans = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">max</span>(ans, <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">query</span>(jobl, jobr, l, mid, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>));
    }
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (jobr &gt; mid) {
        ans = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">max</span>(ans, <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">query</span>(jobl, jobr, mid + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, r, i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>));
    }
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> ans;
}

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n, m;
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 使用 scanf/printf 以匹配 Java 中 StreamTokenizer 的高效 IO</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">scanf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""%d %d""</span>, &amp;n, &amp;m) != <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">EOF</span>) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &lt;= n; i++) {
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">scanf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""%lld""</span>, &amp;arr[i]);
        }
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>(<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, n, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> op, jobl, jobr;
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> jobv;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &lt;= m; i++) {
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">scanf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""%d""</span>, &amp;op);
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (op == <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>) {
                <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">scanf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""%d %d %lld""</span>, &amp;jobl, &amp;jobr, &amp;jobv);
                <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">update</span>(jobl, jobr, jobv, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, n, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
            } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (op == <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>) {
                <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">scanf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""%d %d %lld""</span>, &amp;jobl, &amp;jobr, &amp;jobv);
                <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">add</span>(jobl, jobr, jobv, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, n, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
            } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
                <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">scanf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""%d %d""</span>, &amp;jobl, &amp;jobr);
                <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""%lld\n""</span>, <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">query</span>(jobl, jobr, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, n, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>));
            }
        }
    }
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>
        </div>
        <br>"	
"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">        <div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">typedef</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> ll; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 必须用 long long 避坑</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span> = 1e5 + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">5</span>;
ll tree[<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span> &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>], lazy[<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span> &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>], a[<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span>];

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 向上更新父节点</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">push_up</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> rt) {
    tree[rt] = tree[rt &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>] + tree[rt &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>];
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 向下传递懒标记</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">push_down</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> rt, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> r) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (lazy[rt]) {
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> mid = (l + r) &gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 左子树更新</span>
        lazy[rt &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>] += lazy[rt];
        tree[rt &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>] += lazy[rt] * (mid - l + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 右子树更新</span>
        lazy[rt &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>] += lazy[rt];
        tree[rt &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>] += lazy[rt] * (r - mid);
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 清空当前标记</span>
        lazy[rt] = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    }
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 建树</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> rt, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> r) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (l == r) {
        tree[rt] = a[l];
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span>;
    }
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> mid = (l + r) &gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>(rt &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, l, mid);
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>(rt &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, mid + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, r);
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">push_up</span>(rt);
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 区间修改 [L, R] 加上 k</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">update</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> rt, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> r, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">L</span>, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">R</span>, ll k) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">L</span> &lt;= l &amp;&amp; r &lt;= <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">R</span>) {
        tree[rt] += k * (r - l + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        lazy[rt] += k;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span>;
    }
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">push_down</span>(rt, l, r);
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> mid = (l + r) &gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">L</span> &lt;= mid) <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">update</span>(rt &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, l, mid, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">L</span>, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">R</span>, k);
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">R</span> &gt; mid) <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">update</span>(rt &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, mid + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, r, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">L</span>, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">R</span>, k);
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">push_up</span>(rt);
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 区间查询 [L, R]</span>
ll <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">query</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> rt, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> r, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">L</span>, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">R</span>) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">L</span> &lt;= l &amp;&amp; r &lt;= <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">R</span>) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> tree[rt];
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">push_down</span>(rt, l, r);
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> mid = (l + r) &gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
    ll res = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">L</span> &lt;= mid) res += <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">query</span>(rt &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, l, mid, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">L</span>, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">R</span>);
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">R</span> &gt; mid) res += <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">query</span>(rt &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> | <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, mid + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, r, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">L</span>, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">R</span>);
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> res;
}

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n, m;
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">scanf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""%d %d""</span>, &amp;n, &amp;m);
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &lt;= n; i++) <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">scanf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""%lld""</span>, &amp;a[i]);
    
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>(<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, n);
    
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (m--) {
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> opt, x, y;
        ll k;
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">scanf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""%d""</span>, &amp;opt);
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (opt == <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>) {
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">scanf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""%d %d %lld""</span>, &amp;x, &amp;y, &amp;k);
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">update</span>(<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, n, x, y, k);
        } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">scanf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""%d %d""</span>, &amp;x, &amp;y);
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""%lld\n""</span>, <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">query</span>(<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, n, x, y));
        }
    }
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>
