"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><div><div><div>液晶屏上，每个阿拉伯数字都是可以显示成&nbsp;3×5&nbsp;的点阵的（其中&nbsp;<code>X</code>&nbsp;表示亮点，<code>.</code>&nbsp;表示暗点）。现在给出数字位数（不超过&nbsp;100）和一串数字，要求输出这些数字在显示屏上的效果。数字的显示方式如同样例输出，注意每个数字之间都有一列间隔。</div></div></div><h2>输入格式</h2><div><div><div>第一行输入一个正整数&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>，表示数字的位数。</div><div>第二行输入一个长度为&nbsp;<span style=""font-style: italic;"">n</span>&nbsp;的自然数。</div></div></div><h2>输出格式</h2><div><div><div>输出五行，表示显示屏上的数字。</div></div></div><h2>输入输出样例</h2><div><div><div><b>输入 #1</b>复制</div><pre>10
0123456789
</pre></div><div><div><b>输出 #1</b>复制</div><pre>XXX...X.XXX.XXX.X.X.XXX.XXX.XXX.XXX.XXX
X.X...X...X...X.X.X.X...X.....X.X.X.X.X
X.X...X.XXX.XXX.XXX.XXX.XXX...X.XXX.XXX
X.X...X.X.....X...X...X.X.X...X.X.X...X
XXX...X.XXX.XXX...X.XXX.XXX...X.XXX.XXX</pre></div></div></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;bits/stdc++.h&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>(){

    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> model[<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">10</span>][<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">5</span>] = {
    {<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""XXX""</span>, <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""X.X""</span>, <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""X.X""</span>, <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""X.X""</span>, <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""XXX""</span>}, <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 0</span>
    {<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""..X""</span>, <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""..X""</span>, <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""..X""</span>, <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""..X""</span>, <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""..X""</span>}, <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1</span>
    {<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""XXX""</span>, <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""..X""</span>, <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""XXX""</span>, <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""X..""</span>, <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""XXX""</span>}, <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2</span>
    {<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""XXX""</span>, <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""..X""</span>, <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""XXX""</span>, <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""..X""</span>, <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""XXX""</span>}, <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3</span>
    {<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""X.X""</span>, <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""X.X""</span>, <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""XXX""</span>, <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""..X""</span>, <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""..X""</span>}, <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 4</span>
    {<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""XXX""</span>, <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""X..""</span>, <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""XXX""</span>, <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""..X""</span>, <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""XXX""</span>}, <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 5</span>
    {<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""XXX""</span>, <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""X..""</span>, <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""XXX""</span>, <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""X.X""</span>, <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""XXX""</span>}, <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 6</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>(){
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n,m;cin&gt;&gt;n&gt;&gt;m;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span>(m==<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>){

        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    }

    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">s</span>(n+<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>,<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>);
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i =<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;i&lt;=n;i++){
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> a;cin&gt;&gt;a;
        s[i] = s[i-<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>] +a;

    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> min_sum = s[m] -s[<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>];

    cout&lt;&lt;min_sum&lt;&lt;endl;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""># P1789 【Mc生存】插火把<br><br>## 题目描述<br><br>话说有一天，linyorson 在“我的世界”中开了一个 $n \times n$ 的方阵。现在他有 $m$ 个火把和 $k$ 个萤石，分别放在 $(x_1, y_1) \sim (x_m, y_m)$ 和 $(o_1, p_1) \sim (o_k, p_k)$ 的位置。已知没有光并且没放东西的地方会生成怪物，请问在这个方阵中有几个点会生成怪物？<br><br>**注意，在本题中火把与萤石的照明范围与原版 Minecraft（我的世界）不尽相同，请以本题中的描述为准。**<br><br>火把的照亮范围是：<br><br>|暗|暗|光|暗|暗|<br>|:-:|:-:|:-:|:-:|:-:|<br>|**暗**|**光**|**光**|**光**|**暗**|<br>|**光**|**光**|**火把**|**光**|**光**|<br>|**暗**|**光**|**光**|**光**|**暗**|<br>|**暗**|**暗**|**光**|**暗**|**暗**|<br><br>萤石是：<br><br>|**光**|**光**|**光**|**光**|**光**|<br>|:-:|:-:|:-:|:-:|:-:|<br>|**光**|**光**|**光**|**光**|**光**|<br>|**光**|**光**|**萤石**|**光**|**光**|<br>|**光**|**光**|**光**|**光**|**光**|<br>|**光**|**光**|**光**|**光**|**光**|<br><br>## 输入格式<br><br>输入共 $m + k + 1$ 行。<br><br>第一行为两个正整数 $n, m$ 和一个非负整数 $k$。&nbsp; <br>第二到第 $m + 1$ 行每行两个正整数 $x_i, y_i$，表示各个火把的位置。&nbsp; <br>第 $m + 2$ 到第 $m + k + 1$ 行每行两个正整数 $o_i, p_i$，表示各个萤石的位置。<br><br>数据中可能没有萤石，但一定有火把。<br><br>## 输出格式<br><br>有几个点会生出怪物。<br><br>## 输入输出样例 #1<br><br>### 输入 #1<br><br>```<br>5 1 0<br>3 3<br><br>```<br><br>### 输出 #1<br><br>```<br>12<br><br>```<br><br>## 说明/提示<br><br>数据保证 $1 \le n \le 100$，$1 \leq m+k \leq 25$，$1 \leq m \leq 25$，$0 \leq k \leq 5$。<span style=""color:#C586C0""><br></span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0""><br></span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">通过i和m 还有距离区分火把和萤石</span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0""><br></span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;bits/stdc++.h&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n,m,k,a,b,ans;
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> s[<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">101</span>][<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">101</span>];
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">bool</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">valid</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> x,<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> y){
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span>(x&lt;<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>||y&lt;<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>||x&gt;n||y&gt;n) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
}

    
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>(){
    cin&gt;&gt;n&gt;&gt;m&gt;&gt;k;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i= <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;i&lt;=m+k;i++){
        cin&gt;&gt;a&gt;&gt;b;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> x=-<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>;x&lt;=<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>;x++)
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> y = -<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>;y&lt;=<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>;y++)

                s[x+a][b+y]++;
    }

        ans+=s[i][j] == <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
        cout&lt;&lt;ans;

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 038 Code01 字符串的全部子序列（去重版）</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 递归决策：每个位置的字符选或者不选</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 使用 set 进行结果去重</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 两种实现：string 动态拼接与 char 数组下标控制</span>

<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;string&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;unordered_set&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;algorithm&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 解法一：使用 string 模拟路径（对应 Java 的 StringBuilder）</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f1</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span>&amp; s, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span>&amp; path, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">unordered_set</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span>&gt;&amp; res) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (i == s.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">length</span>()) {
        res.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">insert</span>(path);
    } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 决策1：要当前字符</span>
        path.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">push_back</span>(s[i]);
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f1</span>(s, i + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, path, res);
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 回溯：弹出当前字符</span>
        path.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">pop_back</span>();
        
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 决策2：不要当前字符</span>
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f1</span>(s, i + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, path, res);
    }
}

<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span>&gt; <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">generatePermutation1</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> str) {
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">unordered_set</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span>&gt; <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">set</span>;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> path = <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""""</span>;
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f1</span>(str, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, path, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">set</span>);
    
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span>&gt; ans;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span>&amp; s : <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">set</span>) {
        ans.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">push_back</span>(s);
    }
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> ans;
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 解法二：使用字符数组覆盖更新，靠 size 维护逻辑长度（效率更高）</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f2</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span>&amp; s, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">char</span>&gt;&amp; path, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> size, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">unordered_set</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span>&gt;&amp; res) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (i == s.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">length</span>()) {
        res.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">insert</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span>(path.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">begin</span>(), path.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">begin</span>() + size));
    } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 决策1：要当前字符，填入 path[size]</span>
        path[size] = s[i];
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f2</span>(s, i + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, path, size + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, res);
        
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 决策2：不要当前字符，直接传 size</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 这里不需要清理 path[size]，因为逻辑长度 size 没变</span>
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f2</span>(s, i + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, path, size, res);
    }
}

<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span>&gt; <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">generatePermutation2</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> str) {
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">unordered_set</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span>&gt; <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">set</span>;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">char</span>&gt; <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">path</span>(str.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">length</span>());
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f2</span>(str, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, path, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">set</span>);
    
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span>&gt; ans;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span>&amp; s : <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">set</span>) {
        ans.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">push_back</span>(s);
    }
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> ans;
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 简单测试</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> test = <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""acc""</span>;
    
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""测试开始 (字符串: %s)\n""</span>, test.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">c_str</span>());
    
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span>&gt; result = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">generatePermutation2</span>(test);
    
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""去重后的子序列有:\n""</span>);
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span>&amp; s : result) {
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""\""%s\""\n""</span>, s.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">c_str</span>());
    }
    
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>
        </div>
        <br>"	
"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 038 Code02 含有重复元素数组的所有不重复组合</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 核心思路：排序后，将相同的数字看作一组</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 递归决策：对于每一组相同的数字，决定选 0 个, 1 个, 2 个... 直到该组上限</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 这种方法天然避开了重复组合，无需使用 Set 集合</span>

<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;algorithm&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">/**
 * 辅助递归函数
 * @param nums  原始数组（已排序）
 * @param i     当前处理到的下标位置
 * @param path  路径数组，模拟栈
 * @param size  当前路径的有效长度
 * @param ans   结果集
 */</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&amp; nums, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> path[], <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> size, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&gt;&amp; ans) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (i == nums.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>()) {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 收集结果</span>
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; cur;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> j = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; j &lt; size; j++) {
            cur.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">push_back</span>(path[j]);
        }
        ans.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">push_back</span>(cur);
    } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 找到当前组的边界：找出下一组第一个数的位置 j</span>
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> j = i + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (j &lt; nums.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>() &amp;&amp; nums[i] == nums[j]) {
            j++;
        }

        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 决策：当前数字 nums[i] 选 0 个</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 直接跳到下一组数字的位置 j</span>
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f</span>(nums, j, path, size, ans);

        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 决策：当前数字 nums[i] 选 1个、2个...k个</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 这里的 i 是当前组内元素的移动下标，j 是下一组的起点</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (; i &lt; j; i++) {
            path[size++] = nums[i]; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 每选一个，size 增加</span>
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f</span>(nums, j, path, size, ans);
        }
    }
}

<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">subsetsWithDup</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&amp; nums) {
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&gt; ans;
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 必须排序，让相同的数聚在一起</span>
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">sort</span>(nums.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">begin</span>(), nums.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">end</span>());
    
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 使用静态数组或 vector 模拟 path，这里用动态分配模拟 Java 的 int[] path</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>* path = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">new</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>[nums.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>()];
    
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f</span>(nums, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, path, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, ans);
    
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">delete</span>[] path; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 释放内存</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> ans;
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 简单验证逻辑</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; nums = {<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>};
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&gt; result = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">subsetsWithDup</span>(nums);

    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""nums = [1, 2, 2] 的不重复组合:\n""</span>);
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">auto</span>&amp; subset : result) {
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""[ ""</span>);
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> x : subset) <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""%d ""</span>, x);
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""]\n""</span>);
    }

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>
        </div>
        <br>"	
"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 038 Code03 没有重复项数字的全排列</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 核心思路：i 之前的数字已经确定，i 之后的数字（包括 i）都可以交换到 i 位置上来尝试</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 递归深度：每一层递归确定一个位置上的数字</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 回溯恢复：交换过去之后，递归回来必须交换回来，确保上一层决策时的现场不被破坏</span>

<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;algorithm&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 交换函数</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">swap</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&amp; nums, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> j) {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> tmp = nums[i];
    nums[i] = nums[j];
    nums[j] = tmp;
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">/**
 * 递归函数
 * @param nums 原始数组
 * @param i    当前来到哪个位置做选择
 * @param ans  收集结果
 */</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&amp; nums, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&gt;&amp; ans) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (i == nums.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>()) {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 到底了，收集当前数组的快照</span>
        ans.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">push_back</span>(nums);
    } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> j = i; j &lt; nums.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>(); j++) {
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 把 j 位置的数换到 i 位置来</span>
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">swap</span>(nums, i, j);
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 去填充下一个位置</span>
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f</span>(nums, i + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, ans);
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 特别重要：递归回来，必须换回来（回溯）</span>
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">swap</span>(nums, i, j);
        }
    }
}

<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">permute</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&amp; nums) {
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&gt; ans;
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f</span>(nums, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, ans);
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> ans;
}

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; nums = {<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">3</span>};
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&gt; ans = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">permute</span>(nums);
    
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""数组 [1, 2, 3] 的全排列结果：\n""</span>);
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">auto</span>&amp; <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">list</span> : ans) {
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""[ ""</span>);
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> num : <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">list</span>) {
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""%d ""</span>, num);
        }
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""]\n""</span>);
    }
    
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>
        </div>
        <br>"	
"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 038 Code04 有重复项数组的去重全排列</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 核心思路：在 Code03 交换全排列的基础上，增加“同层去重”</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 剪枝逻辑：在当前位置 i 尝试交换 j 位置的数时，如果 nums[j] 这个数值在当前层已经交换过一次了，则不再尝试</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 空间优化：在 C++ 中，如果数值范围有限，可以用 boolean 数组代替 unordered_set</span>

<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;unordered_set&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;algorithm&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 交换函数</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">swap</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&amp; nums, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> j) {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> tmp = nums[i];
    nums[i] = nums[j];
    nums[j] = tmp;
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">/**
 * 递归函数
 * @param nums 数组
 * @param i    当前来到哪个位置做选择
 * @param ans  收集结果
 */</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&amp; nums, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&gt;&amp; ans) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (i == nums.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>()) {
        ans.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">push_back</span>(nums);
    } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 关键点：set 是局部变量，每一层递归都有自己的 set</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 它记录了当前 i 位置已经尝试过哪些数值了</span>
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">unordered_set</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; visited;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> j = i; j &lt; nums.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>(); j++) {
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 如果 nums[j] 之前没有在这个位置（i位置）出现过，才进行交换尝试</span>
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (visited.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">find</span>(nums[j]) == visited.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">end</span>()) {
                visited.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">insert</span>(nums[j]);
                <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">swap</span>(nums, i, j);
                <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f</span>(nums, i + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, ans);
                <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">swap</span>(nums, i, j); <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 恢复现场</span>
            }
        }
    }
}

<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&gt; <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">permuteUnique</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&amp; nums) {
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&gt; ans;
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 交换全排列不强制要求排序，但排序能让结果更有序</span>
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f</span>(nums, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, ans);
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> ans;
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 简单测试</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; nums = {<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>};
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&gt; result = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">permuteUnique</span>(nums);
    
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""数组 [1, 1, 2] 的去重全排列结果：\n""</span>);
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">auto</span>&amp; <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">list</span> : result) {
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""[ ""</span>);
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> num : <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">list</span>) <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""%d ""</span>, num);
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""]\n""</span>);
    }
    
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>
        </div>

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">// 038 Code07 </pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">打印 n 层汉诺塔问题的最优移动轨迹</pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">// 核心思路：把 n 个盘子的移动拆解为三步</pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">// 1. 将前 n-1 个盘子从 from 移动到 other (利用 to 作为辅助)</pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">// 2. 将第 n 个盘子从 from 移动到 to</pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">// 3. 将前 n-1 个盘子从 other 移动到 to (利用 from 作为辅助)<span style=""color:#C586C0""><br></span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;string&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">/**
 * 汉诺塔递归函数
 */</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> from, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> to, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> other) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (i == <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>) {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 使用 cout 输出，直接插入变量，无需 .c_str()</span>
        cout &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""移动圆盘 1 从 ""</span> &lt;&lt; from &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#CE9178"">"" 到 ""</span> &lt;&lt; to &lt;&lt; endl;
    } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f</span>(i - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, from, other, to);
        
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// endl 相当于 \n 并刷新缓冲区</span>
        cout &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""移动圆盘 ""</span> &lt;&lt; i &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#CE9178"">"" 从 ""</span> &lt;&lt; from &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#CE9178"">"" 到 ""</span> &lt;&lt; to &lt;&lt; endl;
        
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f</span>(i - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, other, to, from);
    }
}

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">hanoi</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (n &gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>) {
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f</span>(n, <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""左""</span>, <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""右""</span>, <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""中""</span>);
    }
}

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {

    ios::<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">sync_with_stdio</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">false</span>);
    cin.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">tie</span>(<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>);

    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">3</span>;
    cout &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""--- ""</span> &lt;&lt; n &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#CE9178"">"" 层汉诺塔移动轨迹 ---""</span> &lt;&lt; endl;
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">hanoi</span>(n);

            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""># P5015 [NOIP 2018 普及组] 标题统计<br><br>## 题目背景<br><br>NOIP2018 普及组 T1<br><br>## 题目描述<br><br>凯凯刚写了一篇美妙的作文，请问这篇作文的标题中有多少个字符？ 注意：标题中可能包含大、小写英文字母、数字字符、空格和换行符。统计标题字符数时，空格和换行符不计算在内。<br><br>## 输入格式<br><br>输入文件只有一行，一个字符串 $s$。<br><br>## 输出格式<br><br>输出文件只有一行，包含一个整数，即作文标题的字符数（不含空格和换行符）。<br><br>## 输入输出样例 #1<br><br>### 输入 #1<br><br>```<br>234 <br>```<br><br>### 输出 #1<br><br>```<br>3<br>```<br><br>## 输入输出样例 #2<br><br>### 输入 #2<br><br>```<br>Ca 45 <br>```<br><br>### 输出 #2<br><br>```<br>4<br>```<br><br>## 说明/提示<br><br>**样例 1 说明**&nbsp;&nbsp; <br><br>标题中共有 3 个字符，这 3 个字符都是数字字符。&nbsp;&nbsp; <br><br>**样例 2 说明**<br><br>标题中共有 $ 5$ 个字符，包括 $1$ 个大写英文字母， $1$ 个小写英文字母和 $2$ 个数字字符， 还有 $1$ 个空格。由于空格不计入结果中，故标题的有效字符数为 $4$ 个。 <br><br>**数据规模与约定**<br><br>规定 $|s|$ 表示字符串 $s$ 的长度（即字符串中的字符和空格数）。&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <br>对于 $40\%$ 的数据，$1 ≤ |s| ≤ 5$，保证输入为数字字符及行末换行符。&nbsp;&nbsp; <br>对于 $80\%$ 的数据，$1 ≤ |s| ≤ 5$，输入只可能包含大、小写英文字母、数字字符及行末换行符。&nbsp;&nbsp; <br>对于 $100\%$ 的数据，$1 ≤ |s| ≤ 5$，输入可能包含大、小写英文字母、数字字符、空格和行末换行符。<span style=""color:#C586C0""><br></span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;string&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> s;
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">getline</span>(cin, s); <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 读入整行，包括空格</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> count = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">char</span> c : s) {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 只有当字符不是空格且不是换行时才计数</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 注意：getline 会去掉行末换行符，所以这里主要判断空格</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (c != <span style=""color:#CE9178"">' '</span> &amp;&amp; c != <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'\n'</span> &amp;&amp; c != <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'\r'</span>) {
            count++;
        }
    }
    cout &lt;&lt; count &lt;&lt; endl;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>

        <br><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">char</span> c;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> count = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// cin &gt;&gt; c 只要能读到非空白字符就会返回 true</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (cin &gt;&gt; c) {
        count++;
    }
    cout &lt;&lt; count &lt;&lt; endl;

            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""># P1308 [NOIP 2011 普及组] 统计单词数<br><br>## 题目描述<br><br>一般的文本编辑器都有查找单词的功能，该功能可以快速定位特定单词在文章中的位置，有的还能统计出特定单词在文章中出现的次数。<br><br>现在，请你编程实现这一功能，具体要求是：给定一个单词，请你输出它在给定的文章中出现的次数和第一次出现的位置。注意：匹配单词时，不区分大小写，但要求完全匹配，即给定单词必须与文章中的某一独立单词在不区分大小写的情况下完全相同（参见样例 1），如果给定单词仅是文章中某一单词的一部分则不算匹配（参见样例 2）。<br><br>## 输入格式<br><br>共 $2$ 行。<br><br>第 $1$ 行为一个字符串，其中只含字母，表示给定单词；<br><br>第 $2$ 行为一个字符串，其中只可能包含字母和空格，表示给定的文章。<br><br>## 输出格式<br><br>一行，如果在文章中找到给定单词则输出两个整数，两个整数之间用一个空格隔开，分别是单词在文章中出现的次数和第一次出现的位置（即在文章中第一次出现时，单词首字母在文章中的位置，位置从 $0$ 开始）；如果单词在文章中没有出现，则直接输出一个整数 $-1$。<br><br>注意：空格占一个字母位<br><br>## 输入输出样例 #1<br><br>### 输入 #1<br><br>```<br>To<br>to be or not to be is a question<br><br>```<br><br>### 输出 #1<br><br>```<br>2 0<br><br><br>```<br><br>## 输入输出样例 #2<br><br>### 输入 #2<br><br>```<br>to<br>Did the Ottoman Empire lose its power at that time<br>```<br><br>### 输出 #2<br><br>```<br>-1<br>```<br><br>## 说明/提示<br><br>数据范围<br><br>$1\leq $ 第一行单词长度 $\leq10$。<br><br>$1\leq $ 文章长度 $\leq10^6$。<br><br>noip2011 普及组第 2 题<span style=""color:#C586C0""><br></span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;string&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;algorithm&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> word, text;
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">getline</span>(cin, word);
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">getline</span>(cin, text);

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 全部转小写</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">char</span> &amp;c : word) c = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">tolower</span>(c);
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">char</span> &amp;c : text) c = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">tolower</span>(c);

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 核心技巧：前后加空格，确保“全字匹配”</span>
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> target = <span style=""color:#CE9178"">"" ""</span> + word + <span style=""color:#CE9178"">"" ""</span>;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> body = <span style=""color:#CE9178"">"" ""</span> + text + <span style=""color:#CE9178"">"" ""</span>;

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 查找第一次出现的位置</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">size_t</span> pos = body.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">find</span>(target);
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (pos == <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span>::npos) {
        cout &lt;&lt; -<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> &lt;&lt; endl;
    } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> first_pos = pos; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 此时的pos正好对应原text中单词的起始位置</span>
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> count = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
        
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 4. 统计出现次数</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (pos != <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span>::npos) {
            count++;
            pos = body.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">find</span>(target, pos + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        }
        cout &lt;&lt; count &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#CE9178"">"" ""</span> &lt;&lt; first_pos &lt;&lt; endl;
    }

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""># P1553 数字反转（升级版）<br><br>## 题目背景<br><br>**以下为原题面，仅供参考:**<br><br>给定一个数，请将该数各个位上数字反转得到一个新数。<br><br>这次与 NOIp2011 普及组第一题不同的是：这个数可以是小数，分数，百分数，整数。整数反转是将所有数位对调；小数反转是把整数部分的数反转，再将小数部分的数反转，不交换整数部分与小数部分；分数反转是把分母的数反转，再把分子的数反转，不交换分子与分母；百分数的分子一定是整数，百分数只改变数字部分。整数新数也应满足整数的常见形式，即除非给定的原数为零，否则反转后得到的新数的最高位数字不应为零；小数新数的末尾不为 $0$（除非小数部分除了 $0$ 没有别的数，那么只保留1个 $0$）；分数不约分，分子和分母都不是小数（约分滴童鞋抱歉了，不能过哦。输入数据保证分母不为 $0$），本次没有负数。<br><br>## 题目描述<br><br>给定一个数，请将该数各个位上数字反转得到一个新数。<br><br>这次与 NOIp2011 普及组第一题不同的是：这个数可以是小数，分数，百分数，整数。<br><br>- 整数反转是将所有数位对调。<br><br>- 小数反转是把整数部分的数反转，再将小数部分的数反转，不交换整数部分与小数部分。<br><br>- 分数反转是把分母的数反转，再把分子的数反转，不交换分子与分母。<br><br>- 百分数的分子一定是整数，百分数只改变数字部分。<br><br>## 输入格式<br><br>一个实数 $s$<br><br>## 输出格式<br><br>一个实数，即 $s$ 的反转数<br><br>## 输入输出样例 #1<br><br>### 输入 #1<br><br>```<br>5087462<br>```<br><br>### 输出 #1<br><br>```<br>2647805<br>```<br><br>## 输入输出样例 #2<br><br>### 输入 #2<br><br>```<br>600.084<br>```<br><br>### 输出 #2<br><br>```<br>6.48<br>```<br><br>## 输入输出样例 #3<br><br>### 输入 #3<br><br>```<br>700/27<br>```<br><br>### 输出 #3<br><br>```<br>7/72<br>```<br><br>## 输入输出样例 #4<br><br>### 输入 #4<br><br>```<br>8670%<br>```<br><br>### 输出 #4<br><br>```<br>768%<br>```<br><br>## 说明/提示<br><br>**【数据范围】**<br><br>- 对于 $25\%$ 的数据，$s$ 是整数，不大于 $20$ 位；<br>- 对于 $25\%$ 的数据，$s$ 是小数，整数部分和小数部分均不大于 $10$ 位；<br>- 对于 $25\%$ 的数据，$s$ 是分数，分子和分母均不大于 $10$ 位；<br>- 对于 $25\%$ 的数据，$s$ 是百分数，分子不大于 $19$ 位。<br><br>**【数据保证】**<br><br>- 对于整数翻转而言，整数原数和整数新数满足整数的常见形式，即除非给定的原数为零，否则反转后得到的新数和原来的数字的最高位数字不应为零。<br><br>- 对于小数翻转而言，其小数点前面部分同上，小数点后面部分的形式，保证满足小数的常见形式，也就是末尾没有多余的 $0$（小数部分除了 $0$ 没有别的数，那么只保留 $1$ 个 $0$。若反转之后末尾数字出现 $0$，请省略多余的 $0$）<br><br>- 对于分数翻转而言，分数不约分，分子和分母都不是小数。输入的分母不为 $0$。与整数翻转相关规定见上。<br><br>- 对于百分数翻转而言，见与整数翻转相关内容。<br><br>数据不存在负数。<span style=""color:#C586C0""><br></span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;bits/stdc++.h&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">rev</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> s,<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> mode){
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">reverse</span>(s.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">begin</span>(),s.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">end</span>());
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span>(s==<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""0""</span>) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""0""</span>;

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span>(mode == <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>){
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">size_t</span> first = s.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">find_first_not_of</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">'0'</span>);
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span>(first == <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span>::npos) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""0""</span>;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> s.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">substr</span>(first);
    }
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span>{
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">size_t</span> last = s.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">find_last_not_of</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">'0'</span>);
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span>(last == <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span>::npos) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""0""</span>;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> s.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">substr</span>(<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>,last+<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
    }
}

    
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>(){
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> s;cin&gt;&gt;s;

    }<span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span>{

            <pre style=""color: rgb(212, 212, 212); margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""># P1603 斯诺登的密码<br><br>## 题目背景<br><br>根据斯诺登事件出的一道水题<br><br>// 数据已经修正 By absi2011 如果还有问题请联系我<br><br>## 题目描述<br><br>2013 年 X 月 X 日，俄罗斯办理了斯诺登的护照，于是他混迹于一架开往委内瑞拉的飞机。但是，这件事情太不周密了，因为 FBI 的间谍早已获悉他的具体位置——但这不是最重要的——最重要的是如果要去委内瑞拉，那么就要经过古巴，而经过古巴的路在美国的掌控之中。<br><br>丧心病狂的奥巴马迫降斯诺登的飞机，搜查时却发现，斯诺登杳无踪迹。但是，在据说是斯诺登的座位上，发现了一张纸条。纸条由纯英文构成：`Obama is a two five zero.`（以 `.` 结束输出，只有 $6$ 个单词 + 一个句号，句子开头如没有大写亦为合法）这句话虽然有点无厘头，但是警官陈珺骛发现这是一条极其重要的线索。他在斯诺登截获的一台笔记本中找到了一个 C++ 程序，输入这条句子后立马给出了相对应的密码。陈珺鹜高兴得晕了过去，身为警官的你把字条和程序带上了飞机，准备飞往曼哈顿国际机场，但是在飞机上检查的时候发现——程序被粉碎了！飞机抵达华盛顿只剩 $5$ 分钟，你必须在这 $5$ 分钟内编写（杜撰）一个程序，免受上司的 $10000000000 \bmod 10$ 大板。破译密码的步骤如下：<br><br>1. 找出句子中所有用英文表示的数字 $(\leq 20)$，列举在下：<br>&nbsp; - 正规：`zero one two three four five six seven eight nine ten eleven twelve thirteen fourteen fifteen sixteen seventeen eighteen nineteen twenty`<br>&nbsp; - 非正规：`a both another first second third`<br>&nbsp; - 为避免造成歧义，`another` 算作 $1$ 处理。<br>2. 将这些数字平方后对 $100$ 取模，如 $0 \to 0 \to 00$，$5 \to 25 \to 25$，$19 \to 361 \to 61$。<br>3. 把这些两位数（按任意顺序）按数位排成一行，组成一个新数，如果开头为 $0$，就去 $0$，如 $\{00,25,61\} \to 2561$。<br>4. 找出所有排列方法中最小的一个数，即为密码。<br><br>## 输入格式<br><br>一个含有 $6$ 个单词的句子。<br><br>保证整个句子的字符个数（包括空格）不超过 $1000$。<br><br>## 输出格式<br><br>一个整型变量（密码）。如果没有符合要求的数字出现，则输出 $0$。<br><br>## 输入输出样例 #1<br><br>### 输入 #1<br><br>```<br>Black Obama is two five zero .<br>```<br><br>### 输出 #1<br><br>```<br>425<br>```<span style=""color:#C586C0""><br></span></pre><pre style=""color: rgb(212, 212, 212); margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;bits/stdc++.h&gt;</span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">using</span><font color=""#d4d4d4""> </font><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">namespace</span><font color=""#d4d4d4""> std;

</font><span style=""color: rgb(86, 156, 214);"">int</span><font color=""#d4d4d4""> </font><span style=""color: rgb(220, 220, 170);"">main</span><font color=""#d4d4d4"">(){

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""># P5461 赦免战俘<br><br>## 题目背景<br><br>借助反作弊系统，一些在月赛有抄袭作弊行为的选手被抓出来了！<br><br>## 题目描述<br><br>现有 $2^n\times 2^n (n\le10)$ 名作弊者站成一个正方形方阵等候 kkksc03 的发落。kkksc03 决定赦免一些作弊者。他将正方形矩阵均分为 $4$ 个更小的正方形矩阵，每个更小的矩阵的边长是原矩阵的一半。其中左上角那一个矩阵的所有作弊者都将得到赦免，剩下 $3$ 个小矩阵中，每一个矩阵继续分为 $4$ 个更小的矩阵，然后通过同样的方式赦免作弊者……直到矩阵无法再分下去为止。所有没有被赦免的作弊者都将被处以棕名处罚。<br><br>给出 $n$，请输出每名作弊者的命运，其中 $0$ 代表被赦免，$1$ 代表不被赦免。<br><br>## 输入格式<br><br>一个整数 $n$。<br><br>## 输出格式<br><br>$2^n \times 2^n$ 的 01 矩阵，代表每个人是否被赦免。数字之间有一个空格。<br><br>## 输入输出样例 #1<br><br>### 输入 #1<br><br>```<br>3<br>```<br><br>### 输出 #1<br><br>```<br>0 0 0 0 0 0 0 1<br>0 0 0 0 0 0 1 1<br>0 0 0 0 0 1 0 1<br>0 0 0 0 1 1 1 1<br>0 0 0 1 0 0 0 1<br>0 0 1 1 0 0 1 1<br>0 1 0 1 0 1 0 1<br>1 1 1 1 1 1 1 1<br>```<span style=""color:#C586C0""><br></span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;bits/stdc++.h&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> a[<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1025</span>][<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1025</span>];
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">solve</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> x,<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> y,<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n){
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span>(n==<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span>;

    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> len = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>&lt;&lt;n;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> half = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>&lt;&lt;(n-<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i =x;i&lt;x+half;i++){
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> j =y;j&lt;y +half;j++){
            a[i][j] = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
        }
    }

    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">solve</span>(x,y+half,n-<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">solve</span>(x+half,y,n-<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">solve</span>(x+half,y+half,n-<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
}

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>(){
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n;cin&gt;&gt;n;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> size = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>&lt;&lt;n;

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i =<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;i&lt;size;i++)
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> j =<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;j&lt;size;j++)
            a[i][j] = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;

    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">solve</span>(<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>,<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>,n);

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i =<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;i&lt;size;i++){
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> j =<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;j&lt;size;j++){
            cout&lt;&lt;a[i][j] &lt;&lt;(j == size -<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>?<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""""</span>:<span style=""color:#CE9178"">"" ""</span>);
        }
        cout&lt;&lt;endl;
    }
    
}</pre>
        </div>
        <br>"	
"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 039 Code01 含有嵌套的表达式求值</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 递归思路：遇到左括号 '(' 就开启下一层递归，遇到右括号 ')' 就结算并跳回</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 乘除优先：通过 push 函数，遇到 * / 立即计算，保证 numbers 内部只有加减关系</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 全局指针：使用 static 变量 where 记录递归处理到的位置</span>

<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;string&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 全局变量，记录递归计算到了哪个位置</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">static</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> where = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 辅助函数：负责执行乘除合并逻辑</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">push</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&amp; numbers, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">char</span>&gt;&amp; ops, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> cur, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">char</span> op) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (numbers.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">empty</span>() || (ops.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">back</span>() == <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'+'</span> || ops.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">back</span>() == <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'-'</span>)) {
        numbers.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">push_back</span>(cur);
        ops.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">push_back</span>(op);
    } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> topNumber = numbers.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">back</span>();
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">char</span> topOp = ops.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">back</span>();
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (topOp == <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'*'</span>) {
            numbers.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">back</span>() = topNumber * cur;
        } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
            numbers.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">back</span>() = topNumber / cur;
        }
        ops.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">back</span>() = op;
    }
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 辅助函数：计算最终的加减序列</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">compute</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&amp; numbers, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">char</span>&gt;&amp; ops) {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n = numbers.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>();
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> ans = numbers[<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>];
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &lt; n; i++) {
        ans += (ops[i - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>] == <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'+'</span> ? numbers[i] : -numbers[i]);
    }
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> ans;
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 核心递归函数</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span>&amp; s, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i) {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> cur = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; numbers;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">char</span>&gt; ops;

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (i &lt; s.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">length</span>() &amp;&amp; s[i] != <span style=""color:#CE9178"">')'</span>) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (s[i] &gt;= <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'0'</span> &amp;&amp; s[i] &lt;= <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'9'</span>) {
            cur = cur * <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">10</span> + (s[i++] - <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'0'</span>);
        } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (s[i] != <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'('</span>) {
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 遇到运算符 + - * /</span>
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">push</span>(numbers, ops, cur, s[i++]);
            cur = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
        } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 遇到左括号，递归进去拿结果</span>
            cur = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f</span>(s, i + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
            i = where + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 从递归结算出来的右括号后面继续</span>
        }
    }
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 最后补上一个加号，收尾结算</span>
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">push</span>(numbers, ops, cur, <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'+'</span>);
    where = i; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 汇报当前位置</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">compute</span>(numbers, ops);
}

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">calculate</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> str) {
    where = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f</span>(str, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>);
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 简单测试</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> exp = <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""1+(2*(3+4)/2)-5""</span>; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1 + 7 - 5 = 3</span>
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""表达式 %s 的计算结果为: %d\n""</span>, exp.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">c_str</span>(), <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">calculate</span>(exp));
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 039 Code02 含有嵌套的字符串解码</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 核心思路：将字符串解码看作是另一种形式的“表达式计算”</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 嵌套处理：遇到 '[' 开启递归 f，遇到 ']' 或结尾停止并汇报全局位置 where</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 结果合并：通过 get 函数（或简单的循环）将递归回来的子串按 cnt 倍数翻倍</span>

<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;string&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 全局变量记录递归位置</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">static</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> where = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">/**
 * 辅助函数：将字符串 str 重复 cnt 次
 */</span>
<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">get</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> cnt, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> str) {
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> res = <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""""</span>;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; i &lt; cnt; i++) {
        res += str;
    }
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> res;
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">/**
 * 核心递归函数
 * @param s 原始字符数组
 * @param i 当前处理起始位置
 */</span>
<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span>&amp; s, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i) {
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> path = <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""""</span>;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> cnt = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (i &lt; s.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">length</span>() &amp;&amp; s[i] != <span style=""color:#CE9178"">']'</span>) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> ((s[i] &gt;= <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'a'</span> &amp;&amp; s[i] &lt;= <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'z'</span>) || (s[i] &gt;= <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'A'</span> &amp;&amp; s[i] &lt;= <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'Z'</span>)) {
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 情况1：遇到普通字母</span>
            path += s[i++];
        } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (s[i] &gt;= <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'0'</span> &amp;&amp; s[i] &lt;= <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'9'</span>) {
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 情况2：遇到数字，累加倍数</span>
            cnt = cnt * <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">10</span> + (s[i++] - <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'0'</span>);
        } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 情况3：遇到 '['，递归去拿括号内部解码后的结果</span>
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 注意：此时 cnt 已经存好了，比如 3[...</span>
            path += <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">get</span>(cnt, <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f</span>(s, i + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>));
            i = where + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 更新 i，跳过刚才递归处理完的那个 ']'</span>
            cnt = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;       <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 倍数归零，迎接下一组</span>
        }
    }
    where = i; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 汇报当前处理到的下标</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> path;
}

<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">decodeString</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> str) {
    where = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f</span>(str, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>);
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 简单验证</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> s = <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""3[a2[c]]""</span>; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// a cc a cc a cc -&gt; accaccacc</span>
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""输入: %s\n""</span>, s.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">c_str</span>());
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""结果: %s\n""</span>, <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">decodeString</span>(s).<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">c_str</span>());
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 039 Code01 含有嵌套的表达式求值</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 测试链接 : https://leetcode.cn/problems/basic-calculator-iii/</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 测试链接 : https://www.nowcoder.com/practice/c215ba61c8b1443b996351df929dc4d4</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 核心思路：递归处理括号 + 栈/列表处理乘除优先级</span>

<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;string&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">class</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Solution</span> {
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> where = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;

    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">calculate</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> s) {
        where = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f</span>(s, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>);
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// f(s, i) 返回从 s[i...] 开始计算的结果</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span>&amp; s, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i) {
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> cur = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; numbers;
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">char</span>&gt; ops;

        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (i &lt; s.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">length</span>() &amp;&amp; s[i] != <span style=""color:#CE9178"">')'</span>) {
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">isdigit</span>(s[i])) {
                cur = cur * <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">10</span> + (s[i++] - <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'0'</span>);
            } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (s[i] != <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'('</span>) {
                <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 遇到运算符 + - * /</span>
                <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">push</span>(numbers, ops, (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>)cur, s[i++]);
                cur = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
            } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
                <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 遇到左括号，递归进去拿结果</span>
                cur = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">f</span>(s, i + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
                i = where + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
            }
        }
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 最后一个数字或括号结果压入</span>
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">push</span>(numbers, ops, (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>)cur, <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'+'</span>);
        where = i;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">compute</span>(numbers, ops);
    }

    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">push</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&amp; numbers, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">char</span>&gt;&amp; ops, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> cur, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">char</span> op) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (numbers.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">empty</span>() || (ops.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">back</span>() != <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'*'</span> &amp;&amp; ops.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">back</span>() != <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'/'</span>)) {
            numbers.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">push_back</span>(cur);
            ops.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">push_back</span>(op);
        } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> topNum = numbers.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">back</span>();
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">char</span> topOp = ops.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">back</span>();
            numbers.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">pop_back</span>();
            ops.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">pop_back</span>();
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (topOp == <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'*'</span>) {
                numbers.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">push_back</span>(topNum * cur);
            } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
                numbers.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">push_back</span>(topNum / cur);
            }
            ops.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">push_back</span>(op);
        }
    }

    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">compute</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&amp; numbers, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">char</span>&gt;&amp; ops) {
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> ans = numbers[<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>];
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &lt; numbers.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>(); i++) {
            ans += (ops[i - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>] == <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'+'</span>) ? numbers[i] : -numbers[i];
        }
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> ans;
    }
};

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Solution</span> sol;

            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""># P5741 【深基7.例10】旗鼓相当的对手 - 加强版<br><br>## 题目描述<br><br>现有 $N(N\le 1000)$ 名同学参加了期末考试，并且获得了每名同学的信息：姓名（不超过 $8$ 个字符的字符串，没有空格）、语文、数学、英语成绩（均为不超过 $150$ 的自然数）。如果某对学生 $\text{&lt;}i,j\text{&gt;}$ 的每一科成绩的分差都不大于 $5$，且总分分差不大于 $10$，那么这对学生就是“旗鼓相当的对手”。现在我们想知道这些同学中，哪些是“旗鼓相当的对手”？请输出他们的姓名。<br><br>所有人的姓名是按照字典序给出的，输出时也应该按照字典序输出所有对手组合。也就是说，这对组合的第一个名字的字典序应该小于第二个；如果两个组合中第一个名字不一样，则第一个名字字典序小的先输出；如果两个组合的第一个名字一样但第二个名字不同，则第二个名字字典序小的先输出。<br><br>## 输入格式<br><br>第一行输入一个正整数 $N$，表示学生个数。<br><br>第二行开始，往下 $N$ 行，对于每一行首先先输入一个字符串表示学生姓名，再输入三个自然数表示语文、数学、英语的成绩。均用空格相隔。<br><br>## 输出格式<br><br>输出若干行，每行两个以空格隔开的字符串，表示一组旗鼓相当的对手。注意题目描述中的输出格式。<br><br>## 输入输出样例 #1<br><br>### 输入 #1<br><br>```<br>3<br>fafa 90 90 90<br>lxl 95 85 90<br>senpai 100 80 91<br>```<br><br>### 输出 #1<br><br>```<br>fafa lxl<br>lxl senpai<br><br>```<br><br>## 说明/提示<br><br>数据保证，$1 \leq N \leq 1000$，姓名为长度不超过 $8$ 的字符串，语文、数学、英语成绩均为不超过 $150$ 的自然数。<span style=""color:#C586C0""><br></span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;bits/stdc++.h&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">struct</span> student{
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> name;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> g1,g2,g3,total;

    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">bool</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">isMatch</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span> student&amp; other) <span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span>{
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">abs</span>(g1 - other.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">g1</span>) &lt;=<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">5</span>&amp;&amp; 
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">abs</span>(g2 - other.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">g2</span>) &lt;=<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">5</span> &amp;&amp;
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">abs</span>(g3 - other.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">g3</span>)&lt;=<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">5</span> &amp;&amp;
            <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">abs</span>(total - other.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">total</span>) &lt;=<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">10</span>;
    }
};


<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>(){
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n;cin&gt;&gt;n;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;student&gt; <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">v</span>(n);
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i =<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;i&lt;n;i++){
        cin&gt;&gt;v[i].<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">name</span>&gt;&gt;v[i].<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">g1</span>&gt;&gt;v[i].<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">g2</span>&gt;&gt;v[i].<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">g3</span>;
        v[i].<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">total</span> = v[i].<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">g1</span> + v[i].<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">g2</span> + v[i].<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">g3</span>;
    }

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i =<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;i&lt;n;i++){
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> j =i+<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;j&lt;n;j++){
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span>(v[i].<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">isMatch</span>(v[j])){
                cout&lt;&lt;v[i].<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">name</span> &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#CE9178"">"" ""</span> &lt;&lt;v[j].<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">name</span> &lt;&lt;endl;
            }
        }
    }
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>

            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""># P2415 集合求和<br><br>## 题目描述<br><br>给定一个集合 $s$（集合元素数量 $\le 30$），求出此集合所有子集元素之和。<br><br>## 输入格式<br><br>集合中的元素（元素 $\le 1000$）<br><br>## 输出格式<br><br>$s$ 所有子集元素之和。<br><br>## 输入输出样例 #1<br><br>### 输入 #1<br><br>```<br>2 3<br><br>```<br><br>### 输出 #1<br><br>```<br>10<br><br>```<br><br>## 说明/提示<br><br>**【样例解释】**<br><br>子集为：$\varnothing, \{ 2 \}, \{ 3 \}, \{ 2, 3 \}$，和为 $2 + 3 + 2 + 3 = 10$。<br><br>----<br><br>**【数据范围】**<br><br>对于 $100 \%$ 的数据，$1 \le \lvert s \rvert \le 30$，$1 \le s_i \le 1000$，$s$ 所有子集元素之和 $\le {10}^{18}$。<br></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;cmath&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> val, sum = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, count = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 题目没有给出 N，需要循环读取直到文件结束</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (cin &gt;&gt; val) {
        sum += val;
        count++;
    }
    
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 使用位运算 1LL &lt;&lt; (count - 1) 代替 pow，效率更高且避免精度问题</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 注意题目要求结果可能达到 10^18，必须用 long long</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> result = sum * (1LL &lt;&lt; (count - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>));
    
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 特殊情况处理：如果集合为空，和为 0</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (count == <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>) cout &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span> &lt;&lt; endl;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> cout &lt;&lt; result &lt;&lt; endl;
    
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>

            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""># P5743 【深基7.习8】猴子吃桃<br><br>## 题目描述<br><br>一只小猴买了若干个桃子。第一天他刚好吃了这些桃子的一半，又贪嘴多吃了一个；接下来的每一天它都会吃剩余的桃子的一半外加一个。第 $n$ 天早上起来一看，只剩下 $1$ 个桃子了。请问小猴买了几个桃子？<br><br>## 输入格式<br><br>输入一个正整数 $n$，表示天数。<br><br>## 输出格式<br><br>输出小猴买了多少个桃子。<br><br>## 输入输出样例 #1<br><br>### 输入 #1<br><br>```<br>4<br>```<br><br>### 输出 #1<br><br>```<br>22<br><br>```<br><br>## 说明/提示<br><br>数据保证，$1\le n\le20$。<span style=""color:#C586C0""><br></span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
