            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""># P2670 [NOIP 2015 普及组] 扫雷游戏<br><br>## 题目背景<br><br>NOIP2015 普及组 T2<br><br>## 题目描述<br><br>扫雷游戏是一款十分经典的单机小游戏。在 $n$ 行 $m$ 列的雷区中有一些格子含有地雷（称之为地雷格），其他格子不含地雷（称之为非地雷格）。玩家翻开一个非地雷格时，该格将会出现一个数字——提示周围格子中有多少个是地雷格。游戏的目标是在不翻出任何地雷格的条件下，找出所有的非地雷格。<br><br>现在给出 $n$ 行 $m$ 列的雷区中的地雷分布，要求计算出每个非地雷格周围的地雷格数。<br><br>注：一个格子的周围格子包括其上、下、左、右、左上、右上、左下、右下八个方向上与之直接相邻的格子。<br><br>## 输入格式<br><br>第一行是用一个空格隔开的两个整数 $n$ 和 $m$，分别表示雷区的行数和列数。<br><br>接下来 $n$ 行，每行 $m$ 个字符，描述了雷区中的地雷分布情况。字符 $\texttt{*}$ 表示相应格子是地雷格，字符 $\texttt{?}$ 表示相应格子是非地雷格。相邻字符之间无分隔符。<br><br>## 输出格式<br><br>输出文件包含 $n$ 行，每行 $m$ 个字符，描述整个雷区。用 $\texttt{*}$ 表示地雷格，用周围的地雷个数表示非地雷格。相邻字符之间无分隔符。<br><br>## 输入输出样例 #1<br><br>### 输入 #1<br><br>```<br>3 3<br>*??<br>???<br>?*?<br><br>```<br><br>### 输出 #1<br><br>```<br>*10<br>221<br>1*1<br>```<br><br>## 输入输出样例 #2<br><br>### 输入 #2<br><br>```<br>2 3<br>?*?<br>*??<br>```<br><br>### 输出 #2<br><br>```<br>2*1<br>*21<br>```<br><br>## 说明/提示<br><br>对于 $100\%$的数据，$1≤n≤100, 1≤m≤100$。<span style=""color:#C586C0""><br></span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;bits/stdc++.h&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> a[] = {<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>,<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>,<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>,-<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>,<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>,-<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>,-<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>,<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>};
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> b[] = {<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>,<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>,<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>,<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>,-<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>,-<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>,<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>,-<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>};
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> res[<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">105</span>][<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">105</span>];

                    res[i+a[k]][j+b[k]]++;

        }

            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""># P1563 [NOIP 2016 提高组] 玩具谜题<br><br>## 题目背景<br><br>NOIP2016 提高组 D1T1<br><br>## 题目描述<br><br>小南有一套可爱的玩具小人，它们各有不同的职业。<br><br>有一天，这些玩具小人把小南的眼镜藏了起来。小南发现玩具小人们围成了一个圈，它们有的面朝圈内，有的面朝圈外。如下图：<br><br>![](https://cdn.luogu.com.cn/upload/image_hosting/0u7em9pi.png) <br><br>这时 singer 告诉小南一个谜题：“眼镜藏在我左数第 $3$ 个玩具小人的右数第 $1$ 个玩具小人的左数第 $2$ 个玩具小人那里。”<br><br>小南发现，这个谜题中玩具小人的朝向非常关键，因为朝内和朝外的玩具小人的左右方向是相反的：面朝圈内的玩具小人，它的左边是顺时针方向，右边是逆时针方向；而面向圈外的玩具小人，它的左边是逆时针方向，右边是顺时针方向。<br><br>小南一边艰难地辨认着玩具小人，一边数着:<br><br>singer 朝内，左数第 $3$ 个是 archer。<br><br>archer 朝外，右数第 $1$ 个是 thinker。<br><br>thinker 朝外，左数第 $2$ 个是 writer。<br><br>所以眼镜藏在 writer 这里！<br><br>虽然成功找回了眼镜，但小南并没有放心。如果下次有更多的玩具小人藏他的眼镜，或是谜题的长度更长，他可能就无法找到眼镜了。所以小南希望你写程序帮他解决类似的谜题。这样的谜题具体可以描述为：<br><br>有 $n$ 个玩具小人围成一圈，已知它们的职业和朝向。现在第 $1$ 个玩具小人告诉小南一个包含 $m$ 条指令的谜题，其中第 $z$ 条指令形如“向左数/右数第 $s$ 个玩具小人”。你需要输出依次数完这些指令后，到达的玩具小人的职业。<br><br>## 输入格式<br><br>输入的第一行包含两个正整数 $n,m$，表示玩具小人的个数和指令的条数。<br><br>接下来 $n$ 行，每行包含一个整数和一个字符串，以逆时针为顺序给出每个玩具小人的朝向和职业。其中 $0$ 表示朝向圈内，$1$ 表示朝向圈外。保证不会出现其他的数。字符串长度不超过 $10$ 且仅由英文字母构成，字符串不为空，并且字符串两两不同。整数和字符串之间用一个空格隔开。<br><br>接下来 $m$ 行，其中第 $i$ 行包含两个整数 $a_i,s_i$，表示第 $i$ 条指令。若 $a_i=0$，表示向左数 $s_i$ 个人；若 $a_i=1$，表示向右数 $s_i$ 个人。 保证 $a_i$ 不会出现其他的数，$1 \le s_i &lt; n$。<br><br>## 输出格式<br><br>输出一个字符串，表示从第一个读入的小人开始，依次数完 $m$ 条指令后到达的小人的职业。<br><br>## 输入输出样例 #1<br><br>### 输入 #1<br><br>```<br>7 3<br>0 singer<br>0 reader<br>0 mengbier <br>1 thinker<br>1 archer<br>0 writer<br>1 mogician <br>0 3<br>1 1<br>0 2<br>```<br><br>### 输出 #1<br><br>```<br>writer<br>```<br><br>## 输入输出样例 #2<br><br>### 输入 #2<br><br>```<br>10 10<br>1 C<br>0 r<br>0 P<br>1 d<br>1 e<br>1 m<br>1 t<br>1 y<br>1 u<br>0 V<br>1 7<br>1 1<br>1 4<br>0 5<br>0 3<br>0 1<br>1 6<br>1 2<br>0 8<br>0 4<br>```<br><br>### 输出 #2<br><br>```<br>y<br>```<br><br>## 说明/提示<br><br>**样例 1 说明**<br><br>这组数据就是【题目描述】中提到的例子。<br><br><br>**子任务**<br><br>子任务会给出部分测试数据的特点。如果你在解决题目中遇到了困难，可以尝试只解决一部分测试数据。<br><br>每个测试点的数据规模及特点如下表:<br><br>::cute-table{tuack}<br><br>| 测试点 | $n$ | $m$ | 全朝内 | 全左数 | $s_i=1$ | 职业长度为 $1$ |<br>|:-:|:-:|:-:|:-:|:-:|:-:|:-:|<br>| $1$ | $20$ | $1000$ | $\surd$ | $\surd$ | $\surd$ | $\surd$ |<br>| $2$ | ^ | ^ | $\times$ | ^ | ^ | ^ |<br>| $3$ | ^ | ^ | $\surd$ | $\times$ | ^ | ^ |<br>| $4$ | ^ | ^ | $\times$ | ^ | ^ | ^ |<br>| $5$ | ^ | ^ | $\surd$ | $\surd$ | $\times$ | ^ |<br>| $6$ | ^ | ^ | $\times$ | ^ | ^ | ^ |<br>| $7$ | ^ | ^ | $\surd$ | $\times$ | ^ | ^ |<br>| $8$ | ^ | ^ | $\times$ | ^ | ^ | ^ |<br>| $9$ | ^ | ^ | $\surd$ | $\surd$ | $\surd$ | $\times$ |<br>| $10$ | ^ | ^ | $\times$ | ^ | ^ | ^ |<br>| $11$ | ^ | ^ | $\surd$ | $\times$ | ^ | ^ |<br>| $12$ | ^ | ^ | $\times$ | ^ | ^ | ^ |<br>| $13$ | ^ | ^ | $\surd$ | $\surd$ | $\times$ | ^ |<br>| $14$ | ^ | ^ | $\times$ | ^ | ^ | ^ |<br>| $15$ | ^ | ^ | $\surd$ | $\times$ | ^ | ^ |<br>| $16$ | ^ | ^ | $\times$ | ^ | ^ | ^ |<br>| $17$ | $10^5$ | $10^5$ | $\surd$ | $\surd$ | ^ | ^ |<br>| $18$ | ^ | ^ | $\times$ | ^ | ^ | ^ |<br>| $19$ | ^ | ^ | $\surd$ | $\times$ | ^ | ^ |<br>| $20$ | ^ | ^ | $\times$ | ^ | ^ | ^ |<br><br>其中一些简写的列意义如下:<br><br>- 全朝内：若为 $\surd$，表示该测试点保证所有的玩具小人都朝向圈内；<br><br>- 全左数：若为 $\surd$，表示该测试点保证所有的指令都向左数，即对任意的 $1\leq z\leq m, a_i=0$；<br><br>- $s=1$：若为 $\surd$，表示该测试点保证所有的指令都只数 $1$ 个，即对任意的 $1\leq z\leq m,s_i=1$；<br><br>职业长度为 $1$：若为 $\surd$，表示该测试点保证所有玩具小人的职业一定是一个长度为 $1$ 的字符串。<span style=""color:#C586C0""><br></span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;bits/stdc++.h&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n, m; cin &gt;&gt; n &gt;&gt; m;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">face</span>(n);
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span>&gt; <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">name</span>(n);
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; i &lt; n; i++) cin &gt;&gt; face[i] &gt;&gt; name[i];

    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> cur = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 当前位置</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; i &lt; m; i++) {
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> a, s; cin &gt;&gt; a &gt;&gt; s;
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 如果朝向和指令方向相同(0,0 或 1,1)，则顺时针减</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 如果不同(0,1 或 1,0)，则逆时针加</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (face[cur] == a) 
            cur = (cur - s % n + n) % n;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> 
            cur = (cur + s % n) % n;
    }
    cout &lt;&lt; name[cur] &lt;&lt; endl;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;i&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">A</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>() || i&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">B</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>();i++){
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span>(i&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">A</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>()) t+=<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">A</span>[i];
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span>(i&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">B</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>()) t+=<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">B</span>[i];
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">C</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">push_back</span>(t%<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">10</span>);
        t/=<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">10</span>;
    }
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span>(t) <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">C</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">push_back</span>(t);

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i =<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">C</span>.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>() -<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;i&gt;=<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;i--) cout&lt;&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">C</span>[i];

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">高精度乘法</span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0""><br></span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;bits/stdc++.h&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>(){
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> s1,s2;
    cin&gt;&gt;s1&gt;&gt;s2;

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span>(s1 == <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""0""</span> || s2==<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""0""</span>){
        cout&lt;&lt;<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>&lt;&lt;endl;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    }

    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n = s1.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>();
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> m = s2.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>();

    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">C</span>(n+m,<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>);

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;i&lt;n;i++){
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> x = s1[n-<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>-i] -<span style=""color:#CE9178"">'0'</span>;
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> carry = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;

        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> j = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;j&lt;m;j++){
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> y = s2[m-<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>-j] - <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'0'</span>;

            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> cur = <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">C</span>[i+j] + x* y+carry;
            <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">C</span>[i+j] = cur%<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">10</span>;
            carry = cur/=<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">10</span>;
        }

        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span>(carry) {
            <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">C</span>[i+m] += carry;
        }
    }

    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> k = n+m-<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span>(k&gt;<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span> &amp;&amp; <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">C</span>[k] == <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>) k--;

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(;k&gt;=<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;k--){
        cout&lt;&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">C</span>[k];
    }
    cout&lt;&lt;endl;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;bits/stdc++.h&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> g[<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">505</span>][<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">505</span>];
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">magicRotato</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> x, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> y, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> r, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> z) {
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 确定魔法影响的整块区域的四个极端边界</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> areaTop = x - r;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> areaBottom = x + r;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> areaLeft = y - r;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> areaRight = y + r;

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 剥洋葱：从最外层往中心收缩（layer 决定当前在转哪一圈）</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> layer = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; layer &lt; r; layer++) {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 计算当前这一圈（层）的具体边界</span>
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> currTop = areaTop + layer;
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> currBottom = areaBottom - layer;
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> currLeft = areaLeft + layer;
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> currRight = areaRight - layer;

        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 偏移量 offset：在当前层的一条边上，我们要转动多少组“四个角”</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 每一层的边长在缩短，所以 offset 的上限也在减小</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> offset = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; offset &lt; (currRight - currLeft); offset++) {
            
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (z == <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>) { <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 顺时针旋转：左下 -&gt; 左上 -&gt; 右上 -&gt; 右下 -&gt; 左下</span>
                <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> temp = g[currTop][currLeft + offset]; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 暂存左上</span>
                
                <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 核心：用坐标移动的方向来命名</span>
                g[currTop][currLeft + offset] = g[currBottom - offset][currLeft];   <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 左下 填到 左上</span>
                g[currBottom - offset][currLeft] = g[currBottom][currRight - offset]; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 右下 填到 左下</span>
                g[currBottom][currRight - offset] = g[currTop + offset][currRight];   <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 右上 填到 右下</span>
                g[currTop + offset][currRight] = temp;                                <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 暂存的左上 填到 右上</span>
                
            } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> { <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 逆时针旋转：右上 -&gt; 左上 -&gt; 左下 -&gt; 右下 -&gt; 右上</span>
                <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> temp = g[currTop][currLeft + offset]; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 暂存左上</span>
                
                g[currTop][currLeft + offset] = g[currTop + offset][currRight];    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 右上 填到 左上</span>
                g[currTop + offset][currRight] = g[currBottom][currRight - offset]; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 右下 填到 右上</span>
                g[currBottom][currRight - offset] = g[currBottom - offset][currLeft]; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 左下 填到 右下</span>
                g[currBottom - offset][currLeft] = temp;                             <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 暂存的左上 填到 左下</span>
            }
        }
    }
}

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>(){
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n,m;cin&gt;&gt;n&gt;&gt;m;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> cnt = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i =<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;i&lt;=n;i++){
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> j =<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;j&lt;=n;j++){
            g[i][j] = cnt++;
        }
    }

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span>(m--){
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> x,y,r,z;
        cin&gt;&gt;x&gt;&gt;y&gt;&gt;r&gt;&gt;z;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span>(r==<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">continue</span>;
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">magicRotato</span>(x,y,r,z);
    }

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;i&lt;=n;i++){
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> j = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;j&lt;=n;j++){
            cout&lt;&lt;g[i][j]&lt;&lt;(j==n ?<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""""</span>:<span style=""color:#CE9178"">"" ""</span>);
        }
        cout&lt;&lt;endl;
    }

}

        </div>
        <pre><img src=""paste-2a44279f2c0b5e4fafd13ce28a241e68c39b353c.jpg""></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""># P4924 [1007] 魔法少女小Scarlet<br><br>## 题目描述<br><br>Scarlet 最近学会了一个数组魔法，她会在 $n\times n$ 二维数组上将一个奇数阶方阵按照顺时针或者逆时针旋转 $90^\circ$。<br><br>首先，Scarlet 会把 $1$ 到 $n^2$ 的正整数按照从左往右，从上至下的顺序填入初始的二维数组中，然后她会施放一些简易的魔法。<br><br>Scarlet 既不会什么分块特技，也不会什么 Splay 套 Splay，她现在提供给你她的魔法执行顺序，想让你来告诉她魔法按次执行完毕后的二维数组。<br><br>## 输入格式<br><br>第一行两个整数 $n,m$，表示方阵大小和魔法施放次数。<br><br>接下来 $m$ 行，每行 $4$ 个整数 $x,y,r,z$，表示在这次魔法中，Scarlet 会把以第 $x$ 行第 $y$ 列为中心的 $2r+1$ 阶矩阵按照某种时针方向旋转，其中 $z=0$ 表示顺时针，$z=1$ 表示逆时针。<br><br>## 输出格式<br><br>输出 $n$ 行，每行 $n$ 个用空格隔开的数，表示最终所得的矩阵。<br><br>## 输入输出样例 #1<br><br>### 输入 #1<br><br>```<br>5 4<br>2 2 1 0<br>3 3 1 1<br>4 4 1 0<br>3 3 2 1<br>```<br><br>### 输出 #1<br><br>```<br>5 10 3 18 15<br>4 19 8 17 20<br>1 14 23 24 25<br>6 9 2 7 22<br>11 12 13 16 21<br>```<br><br>## 说明/提示<br><br>对于 $50\%$ 的数据，满足 $r=1$；<br><br>对于 $100\%$ 的数据，满足 $1\leq n,m\leq500$，$1\leq x-r\leq x+r\leq n$，$1\leq y-r\leq y+r\leq n$。<span style=""color:#C586C0""><br></span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><br></pre></div>"	
"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><img src=""paste-965b7b1b84b7404464404b0474363b1726728760.jpg""><br></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">也可以用胜利的组来判断</pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""># P1328 [NOIP 2014 提高组] 生活大爆炸版石头剪刀布<br><br>## 题目背景<br><br>NOIP2014 提高组 D1T1<br><br>## 题目描述<br><br>石头剪刀布是常见的猜拳游戏：石头胜剪刀，剪刀胜布，布胜石头。如果两个人出拳一样，则不分胜负。在《生活大爆炸》第二季第 8 集中出现了一种石头剪刀布的升级版游戏。<br><br>升级版游戏在传统的石头剪刀布游戏的基础上，增加了两个新手势：<br><br>斯波克:《星际迷航》主角之一。<br><br>蜥蜴人:《星际迷航》中的反面角色。<br><br>这五种手势的胜负关系如表一所示,表中列出的是甲对乙的游戏结果。<br><br>![](https://cdn.luogu.com.cn/upload/pic/1346.png)<br><br>现在，小 A 和小 B 尝试玩这种升级版的猜拳游戏。已知他们的出拳都是有周期性规律的，但周期长度不一定相等。例如：如果小 A 以 `石头-布-石头-剪刀-蜥蜴人-斯波克` 长度为 $6$ 的周期出拳,那么他的出拳序列就是 `石头-布-石头-剪刀-蜥蜴人-斯波克-石头-布-石头-剪刀-蜥蜴人-斯波克-...`，而如果小 B 以 `剪刀-石头-布-斯波克-蜥蜴人` 长度为 $5$ 的周期出拳,那么他出拳的序列就是 `剪刀-石头-布-斯波克-蜥蜴人-剪刀-石头-布-斯波克-蜥蜴人-...`。<br><br>已知小 A 和小 B 一共进行 $N$ 次猜拳。每一次赢的人得 $1$ 分，输的得 $0$ 分；平局两人都得 $0$ 分。现请你统计 $N$ 次猜拳结束之后两人的得分。<br><br>## 输入格式<br><br>第一行包含三个整数：$N,N_A,N_B$，分别表示共进行 $N$ 次猜拳、小 A 出拳的周期长度，小 B 出拳的周期长度。数与数之间以一个空格分隔。<br><br>第二行包含 $N_A$ 个整数,表示小 A 出拳的规律,第三行包含 $N_B$ 个整数，表示小 B 出拳的规律。其中，$0$ 表示 `剪刀`，$1$ 表示 `石头`，$2$ 表示 `布`，$3$ 表示 `蜥蜴人`，$4$ 表示 `斯波克`。数与数之间以一个空格分隔。<br><br>## 输出格式<br><br>输出一行，包含两个整数，以一个空格分隔，分别表示小 A、小 B 的得分。<br><br>## 输入输出样例 #1<br><br>### 输入 #1<br><br>```<br>10 5 6<br>0 1 2 3 4<br>0 3 4 2 1 0<br><br>```<br><br>### 输出 #1<br><br>```<br>6 2<br><br>```<br><br>## 输入输出样例 #2<br><br>### 输入 #2<br><br>```<br>9 5 5<br>0 1 2 3 4<br>1 0 3 2 4<br><br>```<br><br>### 输出 #2<br><br>```<br>4 4<br>```<br><br>## 说明/提示<br><br>对于 $100\%$ 的数据，$0 &lt; N \leq 200, 0 &lt; N_A \leq 200, 0 &lt; N_B \leq 200$ 。<span style=""color:#C586C0""><br></span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;bits/stdc++.h&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;


<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>(){
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n,na,nb;
    cin&gt;&gt;n&gt;&gt;na&gt;&gt;nb;

    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">a</span>(na),<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">b</span>(nb);
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i =<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;i&lt;na;i++) cin&gt;&gt;a[i];
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i =<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;i&lt;nb;i++) cin&gt;&gt;b[i];

    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> vs[<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">5</span>][<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">5</span>] = {
        {<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>},
        {<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>},
        {<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>},
        {<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>},
        {<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>}
    };

    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> scoreA = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>,scoreB = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i =<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;i&lt;n;i++){
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> choiceA = a[i% na];
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> choiceB = b[i% nb];
        scoreA += vs[choiceA][choiceB];
        scoreB += vs[choiceB][choiceA];
    }
    cout&lt;&lt;scoreA&lt;&lt;<span style=""color:#CE9178"">"" ""</span>&lt;&lt;scoreB&lt;&lt;endl;
        
}</pre>

            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""># P1518 [USACO2.4] 两只塔姆沃斯牛 The Tamworth Two<br><br>## 题目描述<br><br>两只牛逃跑到了森林里。Farmer John 开始用他的专家技术追捕这两头牛。你的任务是模拟他们的行为（牛和 John）。<br><br>追击在 $10 \times 10$ 的平面网格内进行。一个格子可以是：一个障碍物，两头牛（它们总在一起），或者 Farmer John。两头牛和 Farmer John 可以在同一个格子内（当他们相遇时），但是他们都不能进入有障碍的格子。<br><br>一个格子可以是：<br>- `.` 空地；<br>- `*` 障碍物；<br>- `C` 两头牛；<br>- `F` Farmer John。<br><br>这里有一个地图的例子：<br><br>```plain<br>*...*.....<br>......*...<br>...*...*..<br>..........<br>...*.F....<br>*.....*...<br>...*......<br>..C......*<br>...*.*....<br>.*.*......<br>```<br><br>牛在地图里以固定的方式游荡。每分钟，它们可以向前移动或是转弯。如果前方无障碍（地图边沿也是障碍），它们会按照原来的方向前进一步。否则它们会用这一分钟顺时针转 $90$ 度。 同时，它们不会离开地图。<br><br>Farmer John 深知牛的移动方法，他也这么移动。<br><br>每次（每分钟）Farmer John 和两头牛的移动是同时的。如果他们在移动的时候穿过对方，但是没有在同一格相遇，我们不认为他们相遇了。当他们在某分钟末在某格子相遇，那么追捕结束。<br><br>读入十行表示地图。每行都只包含 $10$ 个字符，表示的含义和上面所说的相同。保证地图中只有一个 `F` 和一个 `C`。`F` 和 `C` 一开始不会处于同一个格子中。<br><br>计算 Farmer John 需要多少分钟来抓住他的牛，假设牛和 Farmer John 一开始的行动方向都是正北（即上）。 如果 John 和牛永远不会相遇，输出 $0$。<br><br>## 输入格式<br><br>输入共十行，每行 $10$ 个字符，表示如上文描述的地图。<br><br>## 输出格式<br><br>输出一个数字，表示 John 需要多少时间才能抓住牛们。如果 John 无法抓住牛，则输出 $0$。<br><br>## 输入输出样例 #1<br><br>### 输入 #1<br><br>```<br>*...*.....<br>......*...<br>...*...*..<br>..........<br>...*.F....<br>*.....*...<br>...*......<br>..C......*<br>...*.*....<br>.*.*......<br>```<br><br>### 输出 #1<br><br>```<br>49<br>```<br><br>## 说明/提示<br><br>翻译来自NOCOW<br><br>USACO 2.4<span style=""color:#C586C0""><br></span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;bits/stdc++.h&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">char</span> grid[<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">12</span>][<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">12</span>];
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> dx[] = {-<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>,<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>,<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>,<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>},dy[] = {<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>,<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>,<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>,-<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>};
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">struct</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Entity</span>{
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> x,y,dir;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">move</span>(){
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> nx = x+dx[dir] ,ny = y+dy[dir];
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span>(nx&lt;<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span> || nx&gt;=<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">10</span> || ny &lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>||ny&gt;=<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">10</span>||grid[nx][ny] == <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'*'</span>){
            dir = (dir+<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>) %<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">4</span>;
        }<span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span>{
            x = nx;y = ny;
        }
    }
};

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>(){
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Entity</span> f,c;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;i&lt;<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">10</span>;i++){
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> j =<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;j&lt;<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">10</span>;j++){
            cin&gt;&gt;grid[i][j];
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span>(grid[i][j] ==<span style=""color:#CE9178"">'F'</span>) f = {i,j,<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>};
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span>(grid[i][j] ==<span style=""color:#CE9178"">'C'</span>) c = {i,j,<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>};
        }
    }

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> t =<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; t&lt;=<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1000000</span>;t++){
        f.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">move</span>();
        c.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">move</span>();
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span>(f.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">x</span>==c.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">x</span> &amp;&amp; f.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">y</span> ==c.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">y</span>){
            cout&lt;&lt;t&lt;&lt;endl;
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
        }
    }
    cout&lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span> &lt;&lt;endl;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;

}</pre>

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 047 Code01 航班预订统计</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 核心思想：一维差分</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 建立一个长度为 n+2 的数组 cnt（为了处理 R+1 越界问题）</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 差分操作：对于 [L, R, V]，执行 cnt[L]+=V, cnt[R+1]-=V</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 前缀和还原：cnt[i] = cnt[i] + cnt[i-1]</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 4. 复杂度：时间 O(N+M)，空间 O(N)</span>

<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">corpFlightBookings</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&gt;&amp; bookings, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n) {
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 为什么要 n + 2？</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 因为航班编号是 1~n，R+1 最大可能是 n+1</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 为了防止下标越界且逻辑清晰，开到 n+2</span>
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">cnt</span>(n + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>);

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 设置差分数组</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">auto</span>&amp; book : bookings) {
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> first = book[<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>];
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> last = book[<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>];
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> seats = book[<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>];
        
        cnt[first] += seats;
        cnt[last + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>] -= seats;
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 加工前缀和</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 此时 cnt[i] 存的是与前一个位置的差值</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 累加后，cnt[i] 就变成了第 i 个航班的总座位数</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &lt;= n; i++) {
        cnt[i] += cnt[i - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>];
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 结果平移到 0 下标起始的 vector</span>
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">ans</span>(n);
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; i &lt; n; i++) {
        ans[i] = cnt[i + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>];
    }

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> ans;
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 简单测试</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&gt; bookings = {{<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">10</span>}, {<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">3</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">20</span>}, {<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">5</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">25</span>}};
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">5</span>;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; result = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">corpFlightBookings</span>(bookings, n);
    
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""各航班预订座位总数: ""</span>);
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> x : result) <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""%d ""</span>, x);
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""\n""</span>); <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 预期输出: 10 55 45 25 25</span>
    
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>
        </div>
        <br>"	
"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 047 Code02 等差数列差分</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 核心：二阶差分</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 设置四个点：l, l+1, r+1, r+2</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 两次前缀和加工</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 注意 long long 防止溢出，以及大数据量的快读处理</span>

<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;algorithm&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 10^7 + 5 的范围，必须开在全局存储区</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span> = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">10000005</span>;
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> arr[<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span>]; 
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n, m;

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 二阶差分设置函数</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">set</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> r, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> s, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> e, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> d) {
    arr[l] += s;
    arr[l + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>] += (d - s);
    arr[r + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>] -= (d + e);
    arr[r + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>] += e;
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 两次前缀和还原</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 第一次加工：还原成一阶差分数组</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &lt;= n; i++) {
        arr[i] += arr[i - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>];
    }
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 第二次加工：还原成原始数值数组</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &lt;= n; i++) {
        arr[i] += arr[i - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>];
    }
}

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 优化 C++ 输入输出效率</span>
    ios::<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">sync_with_stdio</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">false</span>);
    cin.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">tie</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>);

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (!(cin &gt;&gt; n &gt;&gt; m)) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; i &lt; m; i++) {
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l, r;
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> s, e;
        cin &gt;&gt; l &gt;&gt; r &gt;&gt; s &gt;&gt; e;
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 计算公差 d</span>
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> d = (e - s) / (r - l == <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span> ? <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> : (r - l)); 
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 实际上题目保证了 r &gt;= l，当 r == l 时 d 并不重要，因为 l+1 和 r+1 会抵消</span>
        <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">set</span>(l, r, s, e, (r == l) ? <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span> : d);
    }

    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>();

    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> max_val = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> xor_sum = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &lt;= n; i++) {
        max_val = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">max</span>(max_val, arr[i]);
        xor_sum ^= arr[i];
    }

    cout &lt;&lt; xor_sum &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#CE9178"">"" ""</span> &lt;&lt; max_val &lt;&lt; endl;

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>

        <br>"	
"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 047 Code04 二维差分：地毯问题</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 测试链接 : https://www.luogu.com.cn/problem/P3397</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 核心思路：</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 差分操作：add(x1, y1, x2, y2, V)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 还原操作：二维前缀和 s[i][j] = s[i-1][j] + s[i][j-1] - s[i-1][j-1] + diff[i][j]</span>

<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span> = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1005</span>;
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> diff[<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span>][<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span>];
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n, m;

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 二维差分：对子矩阵进行 O(1) 修改</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">add</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> x1, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> y1, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> x2, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> y2, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> v) {
    diff[x1][y1] += v;
    diff[x1][y2 + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>] -= v;
    diff[x2 + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>][y1] -= v;
    diff[x2 + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>][y2 + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>] += v;
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 二维前缀和还原</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &lt;= n; i++) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> j = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; j &lt;= n; j++) {
            diff[i][j] += diff[i - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>][j] + diff[i][j - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>] - diff[i - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>][j - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>];
        }
    }
}

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    ios::<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">sync_with_stdio</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">false</span>);
    cin.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">tie</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">nullptr</span>);

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (!(cin &gt;&gt; n &gt;&gt; m)) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; i &lt; m; i++) {
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> x1, y1, x2, y2;
        cin &gt;&gt; x1 &gt;&gt; y1 &gt;&gt; x2 &gt;&gt; y2;
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">add</span>(x1, y1, x2, y2, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
    }

    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">build</span>();

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &lt;= n; i++) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> j = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; j &lt;= n; j++) {
            cout &lt;&lt; diff[i][j] &lt;&lt; (j == n ? <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""""</span> : <span style=""color:#CE9178"">"" ""</span>);
        }
        cout &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""\n""</span>;
    }

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>
        </div>

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""># P1098 [NOIP 2007 提高组] 字符串的展开<br><br>## 题目描述<br><br>在初赛普及组的“阅读程序写结果”的问题中，我们曾给出一个字符串展开的例子：如果在输入的字符串中，含有类似于 `d-h` 或者 `4-8` 的字串，我们就把它当作一种简写，输出时，用连续递增的字母或数字串替代其中的减号，即，将上面两个子串分别输出为 `defgh` 和 `45678`。在本题中，我们通过增加一些参数的设置，使字符串的展开更为灵活。具体约定如下：<br><br>1. 遇到下面的情况需要做字符串的展开。在输入的字符串中，出现了减号 `-`，减号两侧同为小写字母或同为数字，且按照 ASCII 码的顺序，减号右边的字符严格大于左边的字符。<br><br>2. 参数 $p_1$：展开方式。$p_1=1$ 时，对于字母子串，填充小写字母；$p_1=2$ 时，对于字母子串，填充大写字母。这两种情况下数字子串的填充方式相同；$p_1=3$ 时，不论是字母子串还是数字字串，都用与要填充的字母个数相同的星号 `*` 来填充。<br><br>3. 参数 $p_2$：填充字符的重复个数。$p_2=k$ 表示同一个字符要连续填充 $k$ 个。例如，当 $p_2=3$ 时，子串`d-h` 应扩展为 `deeefffgggh`。减号两边的字符不变。<br><br>4. 参数 $p_3$：是否改为逆序。$p_3=1$ 表示维持原来顺序；$p_3=2$ 表示采用逆序输出。注意这时候仍然不包括减号两端的字符。例如，当 $p_1=1$、$p_2=2$、$p_3=2$ 时，子串 `d-h` 应扩展为 `dggffeeh`。<br><br>5. 如果减号右边的字符恰好是左边字符的后继，只删除中间的减号。例如：`d-e` 应输出为 `de`，`3-4` 应输出为 `34`。如果减号右边的字符按照 ASCII 码的顺序小于或等于左边字符，输出时，要保留中间的减号。例如：`d-d` 应输出为 `d-d`，`3-1` 应输出为 `3-1`。<br><br>## 输入格式<br><br>共两行。<br><br>第 $1$ 行为用空格隔开的 $3$ 个正整数，依次表示参数 $p_1,p_2,p_3$。<br><br>第 $2$ 行为一行字符串，仅由数字、小写字母和减号 `-` 组成。行首和行末均无空格。<br><br>## 输出格式<br><br>共一行，为展开后的字符串。<br><br>## 输入输出样例 #1<br><br>### 输入 #1<br><br>```<br>1 2 1<br>abcs-w1234-9s-4zz<br>```<br><br>### 输出 #1<br><br>```<br>abcsttuuvvw1234556677889s-4zz<br>```<br><br>## 输入输出样例 #2<br><br>### 输入 #2<br><br>```<br>2 3 2<br>a-d-d<br>```<br><br>### 输出 #2<br><br>```<br>aCCCBBBd-d<br>```<br><br>## 说明/提示<br><br>$40\%$ 的数据满足：字符串长度不超过 $5$。<br><br>$100\%$ 的数据满足：$1&nbsp; \le&nbsp; p_1&nbsp; \le&nbsp; 3$，$1&nbsp; \le&nbsp; p_2&nbsp; \le&nbsp; 8$，$1&nbsp; \le&nbsp; p_3&nbsp; \le&nbsp; 2$，字符串长度不超过 $100$。<br><br>NOIP 2007 提高组第二题。<span style=""color:#C586C0""><br></span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;string&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;algorithm&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;cctype&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> p1, p2, p3;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> s;
    cin &gt;&gt; p1 &gt;&gt; p2 &gt;&gt; p3 &gt;&gt; s;

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; i &lt; s.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">length</span>(); i++) {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 判断当前字符是否为需要处理的减号</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (s[i] == <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'-'</span> &amp;&amp; i &gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span> &amp;&amp; i &lt; s.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">length</span>() - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>) {
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">char</span> left = s[i - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>], right = s[i + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>];
            
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 判定准则：两侧同为数字或同为小写字母，且右侧 &gt; 左侧</span>
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">bool</span> both_digit = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">isdigit</span>(left) &amp;&amp; <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">isdigit</span>(right);
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">bool</span> both_lower = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">islower</span>(left) &amp;&amp; <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">islower</span>(right);
            
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> ((both_digit || both_lower) &amp;&amp; right &gt; left) {
                <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> res = <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""""</span>;
                <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 生成待填充的字符序列</span>
                <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">char</span> c = left + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; c &lt; right; c++) {
                    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">char</span> temp = c;
                    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 处理 p1: 填充方式</span>
                    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (p1 == <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span> &amp;&amp; <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">islower</span>(temp)) temp = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">toupper</span>(temp); <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 转大写</span>
                    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (p1 == <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">3</span>) temp = <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'*'</span>;                      <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 星号</span>
                    
                    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 处理 p2: 重复次数</span>
                    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> k = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; k &lt; p2; k++) res += temp;
                }
                
                <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 处理 p3: 是否逆序</span>
                <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (p3 == <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>) <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">reverse</span>(res.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">begin</span>(), res.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">end</span>());
                
                cout &lt;&lt; res;
                <span style=""color:#C586C0"">continue</span>; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 减号已处理，跳过输出当前 '-'</span>
            }
        }
        cout &lt;&lt; s[i];
    }
    cout &lt;&lt; endl;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>
        </div>
        <br>"	
"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 049 Code01 累加和大于等于 target 的最短子数组长度</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 测试链接 : https://leetcode.cn/problems/minimum-size-subarray-sum/</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 核心：滑动窗口。利用数组全是正数带来的单调性。</span>

<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;algorithm&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;climits&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">minSubArrayLen</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> target, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&amp; nums) {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n = nums.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>();
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> ans = <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">INT_MAX</span>;
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// sum维护的是窗口 [l, r] 内的累加和</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, r = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, sum = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; r &lt; n; r++) {
        sum += nums[r];
        
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 左神风格：如果剔除左边界依然达标，则缩窄窗口</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 这样可以保证每次 r 停止移动时，[l, r] 是以 r 结尾且满足条件的最短区间</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (sum - nums[l] &gt;= target) {
            sum -= nums[l++];
        }
        
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (sum &gt;= target) {
            ans = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">min</span>(ans, r - l + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        }
    }
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> ans == <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">INT_MAX</span> ? <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span> : ans;
}

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; nums = {<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">3</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">4</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">3</span>};
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> target = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">7</span>;
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 子数组 [4, 3] 长度为 2</span>
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""最小子数组长度: %d\n""</span>, <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">minSubArrayLen</span>(target, nums));
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 049 Code02 无重复字符的最长子串</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 测试链接 : https://leetcode.cn/problems/longest-substring-without-repeating-characters/</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 核心思路：滑动窗口 + 下标记录</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 复杂度：时间 O(N)，空间 O(1)（固定 256 大小的数组）</span>

<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;string&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;algorithm&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;cstring&gt;</span> <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// for memset</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">lengthOfLongestSubstring</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> str) {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n = str.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">length</span>();
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (n == <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 记录字符上一次出现的位置，初始化为 -1</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// C++ 中可以直接开 256 的数组，涵盖所有 ASCII 字符</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> last[<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">256</span>];
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">memset</span>(last, -<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">sizeof</span>(last));

    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> ans = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// l: 当前无重复子串的左起点</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// r: 当前探测的终点</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, r = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; r &lt; n; r++) {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 当前字符 s[r]</span>
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">unsigned</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">char</span> c = (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">unsigned</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">char</span>)str[r]; 
        
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 核心逻辑：</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 如果 c 之前出现过，那么左边界 l 必须更新</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 更新到 max(当前l, 该字符上次出现位置+1)</span>
        l = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">max</span>(l, last[c] + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 计算当前窗口 [l, r] 的长度并更新答案</span>
        ans = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">max</span>(ans, r - l + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 更新字符 c 上次出现的位置为当前下标 r</span>
        last[c] = r;
    }

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> ans;
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 简单测试</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> s = <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""abcabcbb""</span>;
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 预期结果：3 (""abc"")</span>
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""最长无重复子串长度: %d\n""</span>, <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">lengthOfLongestSubstring</span>(s));
    
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> s2 = <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""pwwkew""</span>;
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 预期结果：3 (""wke"")</span>
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""最长无重复子串长度: %d\n""</span>, <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">lengthOfLongestSubstring</span>(s2));
    
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 049 Code03 最小覆盖子串</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 测试链接 : https://leetcode.cn/problems/minimum-window-substring/</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 核心思路：欠债模型 + 滑动窗口</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 时间复杂度 O(N)，空间复杂度 O(1)</span>

<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;string&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;climits&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">minWindow</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> s, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> t) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (s.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">length</span>() &lt; t.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">length</span>()) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""""</span>;

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 记录每种字符的欠债情况</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// cnts[i] &lt; 0 : 欠 i 字符多少个</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// cnts[i] &gt; 0 : 多余了 i 字符多少个</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> cnts[<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">256</span>] = {<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>};
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">char</span> c : t) {
        cnts[(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">unsigned</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">char</span>)c]--;
    }

    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n = s.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">length</span>();
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> minLen = <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">INT_MAX</span>;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> start = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// debt 表示总共还差多少个字符才能达标</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> debt = t.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">length</span>();

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, r = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; r &lt; n; r++) {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// [还债/进窗]</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 如果当前字符在欠债名单里，debt 减少</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (cnts[(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">unsigned</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">char</span>)s[r]]++ &lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>) {
            debt--;
        }

        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 债还清了，开始尝试缩窗</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (debt == <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>) {
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// [收缩/去重]</span>
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 如果左边界的字符是盈余的 (cnts &gt; 0)，就扔掉它</span>
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (cnts[(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">unsigned</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">char</span>)s[l]] &gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>) {
                cnts[(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">unsigned</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">char</span>)s[l++]]--;
            }

            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 更新最小长度</span>
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (r - l + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span> &lt; minLen) {
                minLen = r - l + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
                start = l;
            }
        }
    }

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> minLen == <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">INT_MAX</span> ? <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""""</span> : s.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">substr</span>(start, minLen);
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 简单验证</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> s = <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""ADOBECODEBANC""</span>;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> t = <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""ABC""</span>;
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 结果应该是 ""BANC""</span>
    cout &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#CE9178"">""最小覆盖子串: ""</span> &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">minWindow</span>(s, t) &lt;&lt; endl;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 049 Code04 加油站</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 测试链接 : https://leetcode.cn/problems/gas-station/</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 核心思路：滑动窗口 + 断点跳跃贪心</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 复杂度：时间 O(N)，空间 O(1)</span>

<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">canCompleteCircuit</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&amp; gas, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&amp; cost) {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n = gas.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>();
    
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// l 是出发点，r 是尝试到达的下一个点</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// [l, r] 维护的是当前能够走通的区间</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, r = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, sum = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; l &lt; n; ) {
        sum = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
        r = l; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 每次重新从 l 开始计算</span>
        
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 尝试从 l 走，看最远能走到哪</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 注意：这里用 sum + gas - cost &gt;= 0 来判断能否跨过当前 r 站</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (sum + gas[r % n] - cost[r % n] &gt;= <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>) {
            sum += gas[r % n] - cost[r % n];
            r++;
            
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 如果窗口长度达到 n，说明走完一圈了</span>
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (r - l == n) {
                <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> l;
            }
        }
        
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 关键：如果从 l 走不到 r + 1，那么 l 到 r 之间的任何点都走不到 r + 1</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 下一次尝试直接从 r + 1 开始</span>
        l = r + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
    }
    
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> -<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
}

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; gas = {<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">3</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">4</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">5</span>};
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; cost = {<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">3</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">4</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">5</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>};
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 预期结果：3 (加油站编号)</span>
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""起始加油站编号: %d\n""</span>, <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">canCompleteCircuit</span>(gas, cost));
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 049 Code05 替换子串得到平衡字符串</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 测试链接 : https://leetcode.cn/problems/replace-the-substring-for-balanced-string/</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 核心思路：滑动窗口 + 欠债模型。目标是覆盖所有“多出来”的字符。</span>

<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;string&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;algorithm&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;climits&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">balancedString</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">string</span> str) {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n = str.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">length</span>();
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> target = n / <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">4</span>;
    
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 统计全词频</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> cnts[<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">4</span>] = {<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>}; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 0:Q, 1:W, 2:E, 3:R</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">auto</span> getIdx = [](<span style=""color:#569CD6"">char</span> c) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (c == <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'Q'</span>) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (c == <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'W'</span>) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (c == <span style=""color:#CE9178"">'E'</span>) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">3</span>;
    };

    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">s</span>(n);
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; i &lt; n; i++) {
        s[i] = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">getIdx</span>(str[i]);
        cnts[s[i]]++;
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 2. 确定“债务”：即那些超过 target 的部分</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> debt = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> require[<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">4</span>] = {<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>};
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">bool</span> alreadyBalanced = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">true</span>;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; i &lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">4</span>; i++) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (cnts[i] &gt; target) {
            require[i] = target - cnts[i]; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 用负数表示欠债量</span>
            debt -= require[i]; 
            alreadyBalanced = <span style=""color:#569CD6"">false</span>;
        } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
            require[i] = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 不超过 target 的字符不需要被替换掉</span>
        }
    }

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (alreadyBalanced) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 3. 滑动窗口寻找包含所有“多余字符”的最短子串</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> ans = <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">INT_MAX</span>;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, r = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; r &lt; n; r++) {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 进窗：尝试还债</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (require[s[r]]++ &lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>) {
            debt--;
        }

        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 债还完了（窗口包含了所有多余字符）</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (debt == <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>) {
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 缩窗：扔掉多余的盈余字符</span>
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (require[s[l]] &gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>) {
                require[s[l++]]--;
            }
            ans = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">min</span>(ans, r - l + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
        }
    }

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> ans;
}

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 示例：""QQQW"" -&gt; n=4, target=1. Q多出2个。最短覆盖Q,Q的子串是""QQ""，长度2</span>
    cout &lt;&lt; <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">balancedString</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""QQQW""</span>) &lt;&lt; endl; 
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>
        </div>
        <br>"	
"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 049 Code06 K个不同整数的子数组</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 测试链接 : https://leetcode.cn/problems/subarrays-with-k-different-integers/</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 核心思路：将“恰好K个”转化为“最多K个 - 最多K-1个”</span>

<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;cstring&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span> = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">20005</span>;
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> cnts[<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MAXN</span>];

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 计算 arr 中有多少个子数组，其不同数字的种类不超过 k</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">numsOfMostKinds</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&amp; arr, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> k) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (k == <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 重置频次数组（LeetCode中数值范围通常是1~n）</span>
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">memset</span>(cnts, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">sizeof</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>) * (arr.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>() + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>));
    
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n = arr.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>();
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> ans = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// collect 记录当前窗口内不同数字的种类数</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, r = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, collect = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; r &lt; n; r++) {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 进窗</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (++cnts[arr[r]] == <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>) {
            collect++;
        }
        
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 种类超过了k，缩窗</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (collect &gt; k) {
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (--cnts[arr[l++]] == <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>) {
                collect--;
            }
        }
        
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 关键：累加以 r 结尾的合法子数组数量</span>
        ans += (r - l + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
    }
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> ans;
}

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">subarraysWithKDistinct</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&amp; nums, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> k) {
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 恰好 k = 最多 k - 最多 k-1</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">numsOfMostKinds</span>(nums, k) - <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">numsOfMostKinds</span>(nums, k - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
}

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; nums = {<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">3</span>};
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> k = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>;
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 结果应为 7</span>
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""好子数组数目: %d\n""</span>, <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">subarraysWithKDistinct</span>(nums, k));
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>
