"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;"">package class050;

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 按奇偶排序数组II</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 给定一个非负整数数组 nums。nums 中一半整数是奇数 ，一半整数是偶数</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 对数组进行排序，以便当 nums[i] 为奇数时，i也是奇数</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 当 nums[i] 为偶数时， i 也是 偶数</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 你可以返回 任何满足上述条件的数组作为答案</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 测试链接 : https://leetcode.cn/problems/sort-array-by-parity-ii/</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">public</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">class</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Code01_SortArrayByParityII</span> {

	<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 时间复杂度O(n)，额外空间复杂度O(1)</span>
	<span style=""color:#569CD6"">public</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">static</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>[] <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">sortArrayByParityII</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>[] nums) {
		<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n = nums.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">length</span>;
		<span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> odd = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, even = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; odd &lt; n &amp;&amp; even &lt; n;) {
			<span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> ((nums[n - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>] &amp; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>) == <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>) {
				<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">swap</span>(nums, odd, n - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
				odd += <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>;
			} <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
				<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">swap</span>(nums, even, n - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);
				even += <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>;
			}
		}
		<span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> nums;
	}

	<span style=""color:#569CD6"">public</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">static</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">swap</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>[] nums, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> j) {
		<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> tmp = nums[i];
		nums[i] = nums[j];
		nums[j] = tmp;
	}

}
</pre>
        </div>
        <br>"	
"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 050 Code02 寻找重复数</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 测试链接 : https://leetcode.cn/problems/find-the-duplicate-number/</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 核心思路：快慢指针找环入口</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 时间复杂度 O(N)，额外空间复杂度 O(1)</span>

<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">findDuplicate</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&amp; nums) {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (nums.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>() &lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> -<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 初始位置：slow 在 0 走一步，fast 在 0 走两步</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> slow = nums[<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>];
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> fast = nums[nums[<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>]];

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 第一阶段：找相遇点</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (slow != fast) {
        slow = nums[slow];
        fast = nums[nums[fast]];
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 第二阶段：fast 回到起点，寻找环入口</span>
    fast = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (slow != fast) {
        fast = nums[fast];
        slow = nums[slow];
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 相遇处即为重复的数字</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> slow;
}

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; nums = {<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">3</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">4</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>};
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 预期结果：2</span>
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""重复的数字是: %d\n""</span>, <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">findDuplicate</span>(nums));
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>
        </div>

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 050 Code03 接雨水</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 测试链接 : https://leetcode.cn/problems/trapping-rain-water/</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 核心思路：双指针贪心（木桶原理）</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 时间复杂度 O(N)，额外空间复杂度 O(1)</span>

<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;algorithm&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">class</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Solution</span> {
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 最优解：双指针</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">trap</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&amp; height) {
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n = height.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>();
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (n &lt;= <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;

        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// l, r 是当前待处理的左右指针</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// lmax, rmax 分别是 [0, l-1] 和 [r+1, n-1] 范围内的最大值</span>
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, r = n - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>;
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> lmax = height[<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>], rmax = height[n - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>];
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> ans = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;

        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (l &lt;= r) {
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (lmax &lt;= rmax) {
                <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 左侧最大值较小，可以结算左侧</span>
                <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 因为位置 l 的水位受限于 min(lmax, 右侧某个&gt;=rmax的数)</span>
                <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 既然 lmax &lt;= rmax，那么水位上限就是 lmax</span>
                ans += <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">max</span>(<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, lmax - height[l]);
                lmax = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">max</span>(lmax, height[l++]);
            } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
                <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 右侧最大值较小，结算右侧</span>
                ans += <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">max</span>(<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, rmax - height[r]);
                rmax = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">max</span>(rmax, height[r--]);
            }
        }
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> ans;
    }
};

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Solution</span> sol;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; h = {<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">3</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>};
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 预期结果：6</span>
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""接到的雨水总量: %d\n""</span>, sol.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">trap</span>(h));
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>
        </div>

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 050 Code04 救生艇</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 测试链接 : https://leetcode.cn/problems/boats-to-save-people/</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 核心思路：排序 + 双指针贪心</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 时间复杂度 O(N log N)，空间复杂度 O(log N) (取决于排序实现)</span>

<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;algorithm&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">class</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Solution</span> {
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">numRescueBoats</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&amp; people, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> limit) {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 排序是双指针的前提</span>
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">sort</span>(people.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">begin</span>(), people.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">end</span>());
        
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n = people.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>();
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> r = n - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> ans = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
        
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (l &lt;= r) {
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 判定当前最轻和最重的是否能同船</span>
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 如果 l == r，说明只剩一个人了，sum 就是那个人的体重</span>
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> sum = (l == r) ? people[l] : people[l] + people[r];
            
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (sum &gt; limit) {
                <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 太重了，最重的 r 必须自己坐一艘，l 等待下次机会</span>
                r--;
            } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
                <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 能装下，l 和 r 凑一对走</span>
                l++;
                r--;
            }
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 无论是哪种情况，都需要消耗一艘船</span>
            ans++;
        }
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> ans;
    }
};

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Solution</span> sol;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; p = {<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">3</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>};
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> limit = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">3</span>;
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 排序后: 1, 2, 2, 3</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// (1, 2), (2), (3) -&gt; 3艘</span>
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""最小船数: %d\n""</span>, sol.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">numRescueBoats</span>(p, limit));
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>
        </div>
        <br>"	
"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 050 Code05 盛最多水的容器</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 测试链接 : https://leetcode.cn/problems/container-with-most-water/</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 核心思路：双指针贪心。每次舍弃高度较短的那一端，尝试寻找更高的边界。</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 时间复杂度 O(N)，额外空间复杂度 O(1)</span>

<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;algorithm&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">class</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Solution</span> {
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">maxArea</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&amp; height) {
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> ans = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> r = height.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>() - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
        
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (l &lt; r) {
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 当前木桶原理：水面高度由短板决定</span>
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> h = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">min</span>(height[l], height[r]);
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 更新最大面积</span>
            ans = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">max</span>(ans, h * (r - l));
            
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 谁小移动谁</span>
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 如果左侧短，l 右移尝试寻找更高板；反之 r 左移</span>
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (height[l] &lt;= height[r]) {
                l++;
            } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
                r--;
            }
        }
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> ans;
    }
};

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Solution</span> sol;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; h = {<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">8</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">6</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">5</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">4</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">8</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">3</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">7</span>};
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 预期结果：49 (下标 1 的 8 和下标 8 的 7 构成的容器)</span>
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""盛最多水的容器面积: %d\n""</span>, sol.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">maxArea</span>(h));
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>
        </div>
        <br>"	
"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 050 Code06 供暖器</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 测试链接 : https://leetcode.cn/problems/heaters/</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 核心思路：排序 + 双指针。对每个房屋寻找最近的供暖器，指针不回退。</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 时间复杂度 O(N log N + M log M)，额外空间复杂度 O(1)</span>

<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;algorithm&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;cmath&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">class</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Solution</span> {
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 判断对于第 i 号房屋，第 j 号供暖器是否比第 j+1 号更好</span>
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">bool</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">best</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&amp; houses, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&amp; heaters, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> j) {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 如果 j 已经是最后一台供暖器了，那没得选，j 就是最好的</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (j == heaters.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>() - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>) {
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">true</span>;
        }
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 比较当前供暖器和下一台供暖器到房屋的距离</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 注意：这里用 &lt;= 是为了在距离相等时也倾向于跳到下一个，优化逻辑</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">abs</span>(heaters[j] - houses[i]) &lt; <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">abs</span>(heaters[j + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>] - houses[i]);
    }

    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">findRadius</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&amp; houses, <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&amp; heaters) {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 1. 排序是双指针的前提</span>
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">sort</span>(houses.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">begin</span>(), houses.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">end</span>());
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">sort</span>(heaters.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">begin</span>(), heaters.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">end</span>());

        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> ans = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n = houses.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>();
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> m = heaters.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>();

        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// i 扫描房屋，j 扫描供暖器</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, j = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; i &lt; n; i++) {
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 如果当前的供暖器 j 不是最优的（即 j+1 离 i 更近），则 j 右移</span>
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (!<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">best</span>(houses, heaters, i, j)) {
                j++;
            }
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 当前房屋到最近供暖器的距离</span>
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> curDist = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">abs</span>(heaters[j] - houses[i]);
            <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 全局半径取所有房屋所需距离的最大值</span>
            ans = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">max</span>(ans, curDist);
        }

        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> ans;
    }
};

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Solution</span> sol;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; houses = {<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">3</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">4</span>};
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; heaters = {<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">4</span>};
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 房屋1找1(0), 房屋2找1(1), 房屋3找4(1), 房屋4找4(0)</span>
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 最大距离是 1</span>
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""最小加热半径: %d\n""</span>, sol.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">findRadius</span>(houses, heaters));
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 050 Code07 缺失的第一个正数</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 测试链接 : https://leetcode.cn/problems/first-missing-positive/</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 核心思路：原地哈希 / 区域划分。l 为有效区边界，r 为垃圾区边界。</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 时间复杂度 O(N)，额外空间复杂度 O(1)</span>

<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;algorithm&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">class</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Solution</span> {
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">public</span>:
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">firstMissingPositive</span>(<span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt;&amp; arr) {
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n = arr.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">size</span>();
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// [0, l-1] 是有效区：i位置放着 i+1</span>
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> l = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// [r, n-1] 是垃圾区</span>
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> r = n;

        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">while</span> (l &lt; r) {
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (arr[l] == l + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>) {
                <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 情况1：当前数字就在它该在的位置</span>
                l++;
            } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (arr[l] &lt;= l || arr[l] &gt; r || arr[arr[l] - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>] == arr[l]) {
                <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 情况2：当前数字是垃圾（负数、太大、或是重复的数）</span>
                <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 扔进垃圾区，预期上限 r 减小</span>
                <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">swap</span>(arr[l], arr[--r]);
            } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> {
                <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 情况3：是好数但没在位，送去它该去的位置 arr[l]-1</span>
                <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">swap</span>(arr[l], arr[arr[l] - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>]);
            }
        }
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 最后有效区 l 的下一个数 l+1 就是缺失的最小正整数</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> l + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>;
    }
};

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">Solution</span> sol;
    <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">vector</span>&lt;<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span>&gt; nums = {<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">3</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">4</span>, -<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>};
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 调整后可能为 [1, -1, 3, 4]，l停在1处（下标），返回 2</span>
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">printf</span>(<span style=""color:#CE9178"">""缺失的第一个正数: %d\n""</span>, sol.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">firstMissingPositive</span>(nums));
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>
        </div>
        <br>"	
"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""># P3799 小 Y 拼木棒<br><br>## 题目背景<br><br>上道题中，小 Y 斩了一地的木棒，现在她想要将木棒拼起来。<br><br>## 题目描述<br><br>有 $n$ 根木棒，现在从中选 $4$ 根，想要组成一个正三角形，问有几种选法？<br><br>答案对 $10^9+7$ 取模。<br><br>## 输入格式<br><br>第一行一个整数 $n$。<br><br>第二行往下 $n$ 行，每行 $1$ 个整数，第 $i$ 个整数 $a_i$ 代表第 $i$ 根木棒的长度。<br><br>## 输出格式<br><br>一行一个整数代表答案。<br><br>## 输入输出样例 #1<br><br>### 输入 #1<br><br>```<br>4 <br>1<br>1<br>2<br>2<br>```<br><br>### 输出 #1<br><br>```<br>1<br>```<br><br>## 说明/提示<br><br>#### 数据规模与约定<br><br>- 对于 $30\%$ 的数据，保证 $n \le 5 \times 10^3$。<br>- 对于 $100\%$ 的数据，保证 $1 \leq n \le 10^5$，$1 \le a_i \le 5 \times 10^3$。<br><br>关于标题：因为一些不可抗力的原因，名称进行了更改。深表歉意。<span style=""color:#C586C0""><br></span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;iostream&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;vector&gt;</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> cnt[<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">5005</span>];
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">const</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MOD</span> = 1e9 + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">7</span>;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n, max_len = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    cin &gt;&gt; n;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>; i &lt; n; ++i) {
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> a;
        cin &gt;&gt; a;
        cnt[a]++;
        max_len = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">max</span>(max_len, a);
    }

    <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> ans = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 枚举正三角形的边长 i</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>; i &lt;= max_len; ++i) {
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (cnt[i] &lt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">continue</span>;
        
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// C(cnt[i], 2)</span>
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> ways_to_pick_two_sides = cnt[i] * (cnt[i] - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>) / <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span> % <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MOD</span>;
        
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 枚举组成第三边的两根木棒，长度分别为 j 和 i-j</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 为了不重复计算，j 只需要枚举到 i/2</span>
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> j = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; j &lt;= i / <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>; ++j) {
            <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> k = i - j;
            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (cnt[j] == <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span> || cnt[k] == <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">continue</span>;

            <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (j != k) {
                <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 两根长度不等：cnt[j] * cnt[k]</span>
                ans = (ans + ways_to_pick_two_sides * cnt[j] % <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MOD</span> * cnt[k] % <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MOD</span>) % <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MOD</span>;
            } <span style=""color:#C586C0"">else</span> <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (cnt[j] &gt;= <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>) {
                <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 两根长度相等：C(cnt[j], 2)</span>
                <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> ways_to_pick_third_side = cnt[j] * (cnt[j] - <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>) / <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span> % <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MOD</span>;
                ans = (ans + ways_to_pick_two_sides * ways_to_pick_third_side % <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MOD</span>) % <span style=""color:#4EC9B0"">MOD</span>;
            }
        }
    }

    cout &lt;&lt; ans &lt;&lt; endl;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""># P2392 kkksc03考前临时抱佛脚<br><br>## 题目背景<br><br>kkksc03 的大学生活非常的颓废，平时根本不学习。但是，临近期末考试，他必须要开始抱佛脚，以求不挂科。<br><br>## 题目描述<br><br>这次期末考试，kkksc03 需要考 $4$ 科。因此要开始刷习题集，每科都有一个习题集，分别有 $s_1,s_2,s_3,s_4$ 道题目，完成每道题目需要一些时间，可能不等（$A_1,A_2,\ldots,A_{s_1}$，$B_1,B_2,\ldots,B_{s_2}$，$C_1,C_2,\ldots,C_{s_3}$，$D_1,D_2,\ldots,D_{s_4}$）。<br><br><br>kkksc03 有一个能力，他的左右两个大脑可以同时计算 $2$ 道不同的题目，但是仅限于同一科。因此，kkksc03 必须一科一科的复习。<br><br><br>由于 kkksc03 还急着去处理洛谷的 bug，因此他希望尽快把事情做完，所以他希望知道能够完成复习的最短时间。<br><br>## 输入格式<br><br>本题包含 $5$ 行数据：第 $1$ 行，为四个正整数 $s_1,s_2,s_3,s_4$。<br><br>第 $2$ 行，为 $A_1,A_2,\ldots,A_{s_1}$ 共 $s_1$ 个数，表示第一科习题集每道题目所消耗的时间。<br><br>第 $3$ 行，为 $B_1,B_2,\ldots,B_{s_2}$ 共 $s_2$ 个数。<br><br>第 $4$ 行，为 $C_1,C_2,\ldots,C_{s_3}$ 共 $s_3$ 个数。<br><br>第 $5$ 行，为 $D_1,D_2,\ldots,D_{s_4}$ 共 $s_4$ 个数，意思均同上。<br><br>## 输出格式<br><br>输出一行，为复习完毕最短时间。<br><br>## 输入输出样例 #1<br><br>### 输入 #1<br><br>```<br>1 2 1 3&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <br>5<br>4 3<br>6<br>2 4 3<br><br>```<br><br>### 输出 #1<br><br>```<br>20<br>```<br><br>## 说明/提示<br><br>$1\leq s_1,s_2,s_3,s_4\leq 20$。<br><br>$1\leq A_1,A_2,\ldots,A_{s_1},B_1,B_2,\ldots,B_{s_2},C_1,C_2,\ldots,C_{s_3},D_1,D_2,\ldots,D_{s_4}\leq60$。<span style=""color:#C586C0""><br></span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;bits/stdc++.h&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> s[<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">5</span>];           <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 存储 4 科各自的题目数量</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> t[<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">21</span>];          <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 存储当前科目的每道题耗时</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> total_time;     <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 当前科目的总耗时</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> total_ans = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;  <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 最终累加的总最短时间</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> min_time;       <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// solve1 用：记录当前科目最小的最大脑负担</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> max_left;       <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// solve2 用：记录单脑在不超过一半时间下的最大负荷</span>

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">/**
 * 解法一：直观搜索 (Recursive Brute Force)
 * 思路：遍历每道题放在“左脑”还是“右脑”。
 * 当所有题分配完，计算两脑中的最大值，取这些最大值中的最小值。
 */</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">dfs1</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> step, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> current_left, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> subject_size) {
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 边界条件：所有题目都已决定去向</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (step &gt; subject_size) {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// total_time - current_left 就是右脑的时间</span>
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 这一科完成的时间取决于耗时较长的那个大脑</span>
        min_time = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">min</span>(min_time, <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">max</span>(current_left, total_time - current_left));
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span>;
    }
    
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 决策 1：把这道题给左脑</span>
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">dfs1</span>(step + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, current_left + t[step], subject_size);
    
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 决策 2：把这道题给右脑（左脑时间不变）</span>
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">dfs1</span>(step + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, current_left, subject_size);
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">/**
 * 解法二：折半偏移搜索 (Subset Sum / Knapsack Thinking)
 * 思路：将问题转化为“求左脑能承担的最大时间，且该时间不能超过总时间的一半”。
 * 这样右脑自然承担剩下的部分，且右脑时间必然 &gt;= 左脑。
 */</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">dfs2</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> step, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> current_left, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> target, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> subject_size) {
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 剪枝：如果当前左脑时间已经超过了目标（总和的一半），则不需要再试</span>
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (current_left &gt; target) <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span>;

    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span> (step &gt; subject_size) {
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 更新左脑能达到的最大耗时（且 &lt;= target）</span>
        max_left = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">max</span>(max_left, current_left);
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span>;
    }

    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 决策：选或者不选入左脑</span>
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">dfs2</span>(step + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, current_left + t[step], target, subject_size);
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">dfs2</span>(step + <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, current_left, target, subject_size);
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 对应 solve1 的调用逻辑</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">run_solve1</span>() {
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &lt;= <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">4</span>; i++) cin &gt;&gt; s[i];
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &lt;= <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">4</span>; i++) {
        total_time = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
        min_time = 1e9;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> j = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; j &lt;= s[i]; j++) {
            cin &gt;&gt; t[j];
            total_time += t[j];
        }
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">dfs1</span>(<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, s[i]);
        total_ans += min_time;
    }
    cout &lt;&lt; total_ans &lt;&lt; endl;
}

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 对应 solve2 的调用逻辑</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">run_solve2</span>() {
    total_ans = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &lt;= <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">4</span>; i++) cin &gt;&gt; s[i];
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; i &lt;= <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">4</span>; i++) {
        total_time = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
        max_left = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span> (<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> j = <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>; j &lt;= s[i]; j++) {
            cin &gt;&gt; t[j];
            total_time += t[j];
        }
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 目标是让左脑尽量接近总时长的一半</span>
        <span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> target = total_time / <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">2</span>;
        <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">dfs2</span>(<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>, target, s[i]);
        <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 完成时间 = 总时间 - 较短的大脑时间</span>
        total_ans += (total_time - max_left);
    }
    cout &lt;&lt; total_ans &lt;&lt; endl;
}

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>() {
    ios::<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">sync_with_stdio</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">false</span>), cin.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">tie</span>(<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>), cout.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">tie</span>(<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>);
    <span style=""color:#6A9955"">// 两个解法逻辑均正确，solve2 带有简单剪枝，效率略高</span>
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">run_solve2</span>(); 
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>

"<div class=""vscode-cpp-block"" style=""background-color: rgb(30, 30, 30); color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding: 12px 18px; border-radius: 6px; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.5; margin: 10px 0px; border: 1px solid rgb(45, 45, 45); overflow-x: auto; tab-size: 4;"">
            <pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""># P2036 [COCI 2008/2009 #2] PERKET<br><br>## 题目描述<br><br>Perket 是一种流行的美食。为了做好 Perket，厨师必须谨慎选择食材，以在保持传统风味的同时尽可能获得最全面的味道。你有 $n$ 种可支配的配料。对于每一种配料，我们知道它们各自的酸度 $s$ 和苦度 $b$。当我们添加配料时，总的酸度为每一种配料的酸度总乘积；总的苦度为每一种配料的苦度的总和。<br><br>众所周知，美食应该做到口感适中，所以我们希望选取配料，以使得酸度和苦度的绝对差最小。<br><br>另外，我们必须添加至少一种配料，因为没有任何食物是只以水为配料的。<br><br>## 输入格式<br><br>第一行一个整数 $n$，表示可供选用的食材种类数。<br><br>接下来 $n$ 行，每行 $2$ 个整数 $s_i$ 和 $b_i$，表示第 $i$ 种食材的酸度和苦度。<br><br>## 输出格式<br><br>一行一个整数，表示可能的总酸度和总苦度的最小绝对差。<br><br>## 输入输出样例 #1<br><br>### 输入 #1<br><br>```<br>1<br>3 10<br>```<br><br>### 输出 #1<br><br>```<br>7<br>```<br><br>## 输入输出样例 #2<br><br>### 输入 #2<br><br>```<br>2<br>3 8<br>5 8<br>```<br><br>### 输出 #2<br><br>```<br>1<br>```<br><br>## 输入输出样例 #3<br><br>### 输入 #3<br><br>```<br>4<br>1 7<br>2 6<br>3 8<br>4 9<br>```<br><br>### 输出 #3<br><br>```<br>1<br>```<br><br>## 说明/提示<br><br>对于第三组样例，选择最后三种食材，此时的总酸度为 $2 \times 3 \times 4 = 24$，总苦度为 $6+8+9=23$，差值为 $1$。<br><br>#### 数据规模与约定<br>对于 $100\%$ 的数据，有 $1 \leq n \leq 10$，且将所有可用食材全部使用产生的总酸度和总苦度小于 $1 \times 10^9$。<br>#### 说明<br>- 本题满分 $70$ 分。<br>- 题目译自 [COCI2008-2009](https://hsin.hr/coci/archive/2008_2009/) [CONTEST #2](https://hsin.hr/coci/archive/2008_2009/contest2_tasks.pdf) PERKET，译者 @[mnesia](https://www.luogu.com.cn/user/115711)。<span style=""color:#C586C0""><br></span></pre><pre style=""margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; font-family: inherit;""><span style=""color:#C586C0"">#include </span><span style=""color:#CE9178"">&lt;bits/stdc++.h&gt;</span>
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">using</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">namespace</span> std;
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// #define int long long</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// const int N = ;</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// int n;</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// int min_abs;</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">//     vector&lt;vector&lt;int&gt;&gt; v(n);</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// dfs(int count ,int tocount,int start)</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// {</span>

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">//     if(count == tocount){</span>

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">//             dfs(count+1,i,start+1);</span>




<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// }</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// void solve()</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">// {</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">//     int min_abs = 1e9;</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">//     cin&gt;&gt;n;</span>

<span style=""color:#6A9955"">//     for(int i = 0;i&lt;n;i++){</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">//         for(int j = 0;i&lt;2;i++){</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">//             cin&gt;&gt;v[i][j];</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">//         }</span>
<span style=""color:#6A9955"">//     }</span>

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> n;
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> s[<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">15</span>],b[<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">15</span>];
<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> min_diff =2e9;

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">dfs</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> index, <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> current_s,<span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> <span style=""color:#569CD6"">long</span> current_b,<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> chosen_cnt){
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span>(index ==n){
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">if</span>(chosen_cnt&gt; <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>){
            min_diff = <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">min</span>(min_diff, <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">abs</span>(current_s - current_b));
        }
        <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span>;
    }

    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">dfs</span>(index +<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>,current_s * s[index],current_b + b[index] ,chosen_cnt +<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>);

    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">dfs</span>(index +<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>, current_s,current_b,chosen_cnt);
}

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">void</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">solve</span>(){
    cin&gt;&gt;n;
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">for</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">int</span> i =<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;i&lt;n;i++) cin&gt;&gt;s[i]&gt;&gt;b[i];

    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">dfs</span>(<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>,<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">1</span>,<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>,<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>);

    cout&lt;&lt; min_diff&lt;&lt;endl;

}

<span style=""color:#569CD6"">signed</span> <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">main</span>()
{
    ios::<span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">sync_with_stdio</span>(<span style=""color:#569CD6"">false</span>), cin.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">tie</span>(<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>), cout.<span style=""color:#9CDCFE"">tie</span>(<span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>);
    <span style=""color:#DCDCAA"">solve</span>();
    <span style=""color:#C586C0"">return</span> <span style=""color:#B5CEA8"">0</span>;
}</pre>
